For three decades the operative dichotomy *Skrull or human* — the question she could not answer, the choice she organized her entire avoidance behavior around — has been the central axis of her identity dissociation. Empyre does not resolve the dichotomy. It dissolves it. The Skrull Empire as the entity to which she once swore loyalty no longer exists in the form it existed when she was deployed; her original chain of command is several regimes superseded; her original ideological framework has been overwritten by an interspecies unification that simply has no slot for the specific kind of operative she was trained to be.

For most decommissioned operatives in similar real-world scenarios (Cold War assets after 1991 being the closest analog), this is destabilizing. For Subject it is liberating in a way she does not yet have the vocabulary to articulate. The job is gone. The empire is gone. The ideology is gone. What remains is only the personal — the attachments, the guilts, the choices she made for herself rather than for command. For the first time, the question is not *which side are you on*. The question is *who are you, now that there are no sides*. This is a question she still cannot answer, but it is a categorically different question than the one that organized her crisis behavior for thirty years, and the behavioral signature post-Empyre reflects this.

She does not, notably, integrate into the Kree-Skrull Alliance under Hulkling. She does not seek a diplomatic or intelligence role in the new polity. Offered, in effect, a homeland for the first time, she declines it — not by formal rejection but by simply not showing up. This is consistent: a homeland predicated on the dissolution of the dichotomy she organized herself around is still, for her, an answer to a question she has stopped asking. Hulkling's empire is meaningful to Skrulls who maintained Skrull identity through the diaspora. Subject did not. She has nothing to bring to it.

## 4.5 Current Residency and Routine (Inferred, file-close estimate)

**Geographic:** Earth-based, urban, Eastern Seaboard probability-weighted. Indicators: response time to FF-related crises is short (hours, not days); no recorded recent off-world appearances outside specific operational windows; the morphological flexibility makes a metropolitan area with high anonymity baseline (NYC, Boston, Philadelphia corridor) the most plausible cover environment. She does not reside in or near Pier Four/Four Freedoms Plaza; the proximity-without-contact pattern requires distance sufficient to deny herself the temptation of casual visit.

**Domicile profile:** Probable single-occupancy apartment, mid-rise, mid-tier neighborhood. Lease almost certainly under a human alias, paid via funds laundered through one or another residual Skrull diaspora financial structure or via accumulated mercenary contract earnings. UATU assessment: she pays rent on time, maintains the unit to a level of cleanliness consistent with someone who could leave at any moment without forensic trace, and has not personalized the space. No photographs. No keepsakes. The absence is the tell — a thirty-year veteran of an attachment-saturated life has accumulated zero physical artifacts of it because every artifact would require her to settle the question of which self the artifact belonged to.

**Daily structure (inferred from recorded behaviors and known character constants):**

- *Morning:* Wake early. Subject's recorded sleep pattern is light and abbreviated; the operative training never decompiled. Probable routine includes physical maintenance (Skrull morphology requires baseline cellular discipline to maintain a stable preferred form; without practice the form drifts), reconnaissance of news cycles for FF-relevant signal, and contact-check with whatever minimal Skrull diaspora network she still maintains.
- *Working hours:* No confirmed legitimate employment. Probable income from contract intelligence work, possibly for SWORD (which would have logical interest in a willing Skrull asset with FF-trust standing), possibly for private parties, possibly residual from the Alliance via informal channels. She does not work for the Avengers, the FF, or any publicly-rostered team; the visibility would be intolerable.
- *Evening:* Solitary. No recorded romantic or social relationships outside the FF orbit since the original Alicia-replacement period. Subject does not date. The clinical reading is straightforward: dating would require choosing a presentational identity and sustaining it past first acquaintance, and Subject does not have a presentational identity she can sustain past first acquaintance without it becoming a role she begins to inhabit and ultimately to dissolve into.
- *Sleep:* Probable variable morphology while sleeping, as muscular control of form-maintenance lapses. This is a Skrull-specific note: she likely cannot afford a partner because she cannot afford to be observed in the unguarded state, which for her includes morphological unguarding.

**Wardrobe:** Pragmatic, replaceable, non-distinctive. She owns clothes; she does not own a wardrobe. Color palette tends muted; she does not wear the green-and-purple iconography of her past combat appearances except when deliberately presenting as Skrull. In civilian context she presents as unremarkable, which for someone with her capability profile is itself a discipline.

**Contact ritual:** No recorded direct contact with Johnny Storm at file-close. No recorded contact with Ben Grimm at any point in the post-Slott era. No recorded contact with Alicia Masters — ever, in the entire record, post-restoration of the real Alicia; the avoidance is total and consistent with the §4 assessment of the Alicia-name as the single most destabilizing stimulus in her environment.

## 4.6 Current Operational Status

Subject is, at file-close, *non-aligned* in the formal sense and *FF-loyal* in the operational sense. She has no commanding authority. She has no team. She has no nation. She has, by reliable inference, a small number of informal information-sharing relationships — probably one or two within the Kree-Skrull Alliance intelligence apparatus who knew her from the pre-Invasion period and tolerate her ambivalence; possibly one human contact within SWORD or comparable agency; possibly Sue Richards in a quiet back-channel that the on-panel record does not document but which the long-standing tonal evidence (Sue's compassion toward Subject across multiple appearances) makes plausible.

Her availability for FF-emergency response is high. Her availability for FF-domestic engagement is zero. This is the stable equilibrium she has constructed: present in crisis, absent in peace, ensuring that her relationship with the attachment-objects is mediated entirely through her usefulness, which is the one currency in which she does not have to confront the identity question.

## 4.7 Psychiatric Trajectory, Current

Against the §4 baseline, the current presentation shows measurable improvement on two axes and stagnation on a third.

**Improved — identity-state alternation:** The use of "Lyja" as stable self-reference in recent appearances, the absence of Alicia-default under stress, and the willingness to appear in native Skrull morphology in non-combat contexts all indicate that the dissociative alternation between Skrull-self and Alicia-self has substantially diminished. The Lyja-as-Johnny's-estranged-wife identity remains active but is no longer in active competition with the other two for primacy.

**Improved — affective regulation around attachment objects:** The Slott-era and post-Empyre appearances show no recurrence of the acting-out pattern that characterized the egg-deception period. Abandonment cues no longer produce manipulative re-engagement. The behavior is renunciatory rather than coercive. Whether this represents genuine integration or simply exhaustion is not yet determinable from the record, but the operational outcome is the same: she is no longer dangerous to Johnny in the way she once was.

**Stagnant — core identity integration:** She still does not know who she is. The Empyre dissolution of the Skrull-or-human dichotomy removed the question but did not provide an answer. She has stopped asking the question because the question is no longer coherent; she has not arrived at a self. The marginality she chose in §3 as the price of not killing any of her partial selves remains her operating condition. She is more comfortable in it than she was. She is not closer to leaving it.

## 4.8 How She Got Here

The trajectory from the 1991 exposure to the file-close state is, when laid out, a single coherent arc: a person manufactured for impersonation who, through the accident of being assigned to a target population whose proximity she could not survive without contamination, gradually lost the engineered self without ever acquiring an alternative; who responded to that loss with progressively less destructive behaviors over time as the acute grief of the attachment ruptures subsided; whose original ideological frame was dissolved beneath her by events larger than her individual life; and who has, at file-close, achieved the modest but real accomplishment of being able to exist as Lyja in her own presence without any of the prior partial selves rising to displace her.

This is not redemption. The original deception remains uncompensated; the real Alicia's lost years are not recoverable; the wound inflicted by the egg ruse on Johnny Storm is not repaired by Subject's subsequent restraint. What it is, instead, is the slow, post-traumatic stabilization of a person whose initial conditions made stability nearly impossible. She is, at present, *less harmful than she has ever been, less self-deceived than she has ever been, and less attached to any external authority than she has ever been*. These are the conditions under which a self, if one were ever going to form, would form.

The file remains open because the question of whether one will is not yet answerable.

— UATU, Analytical Stage, Chronology IV closes.


## Medical History

# UATU INTELLIGENCE DOSSIER — SUBJECT "LYJA"
## Section 2: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Compiled across the full observational record; cross-referenced to canonical incident logs (Defalco/Ryan, Englehart, Wieringo, Bendis, Hickman, Slott, and Empyre-era observations). Where direct physiological data is unobtainable owing to species-anomalous biology, inferences are bracketed and labeled as such.*

---

### 2.1 Species Baseline & Constitutional Profile

Subject is a member of the Deviant Skrull lineage — the shapeshifting branch descended from Celestial intervention and possessing the species' characteristic unstable cellular matrix. This is the irreducible biological fact from which all subsequent medical observations must be read: Lyja does not possess a fixed somatic substrate. Her body is, in the strict cytological sense, a *negotiated configuration* — a metastable arrangement of polymorphic tissue held in whatever shape sustained intention dictates. At rest, in private, and in unguarded sleep, the baseline configuration reverts toward the standard female Skrull morphology: green pigmentation, ridged maxillary structure, pointed auricles, dark hair, slighter build than the imperial-warrior phenotype. Field observation suggests her "true" resting form is itself partly a learned default rather than a strict genetic terminus; deep-cover operatives of her training class are habituated to a chosen baseline that may not match birth morphology.

Height (baseline): approximately 5'8". Mass (baseline): est. 130–140 lbs, though Skrull cellular plasticity permits voluntary mass alteration within roughly an order of magnitude in either direction, with the differential drawn from or shunted to a subspace reservoir that Skrull physiology accesses unconsciously. Skin temperature runs marginally cooler than human normal (~96.4°F observed in the Alicia-form, suggesting active thermoregulatory mimicry rather than identity of physiology). Cardiopulmonary architecture: dual-chambered cardiac structure; respiratory rate slightly elevated relative to body mass. Hematology: copper-based oxygen transport in baseline form, retrofitted toward iron-based in long-held human impersonations — the transition is metabolically expensive and is the principal physiological cost of extended cover.

### 2.2 The Shapeshifting Apparatus as a Medical Variable

It is necessary to treat morphological plasticity as a *medical condition in itself*, not merely as a capability. The relevant pathologies are not those of injury but of identity-at-the-cellular-level:

- **Morphological drift under affective load.** Field observation across the Alicia-cover decade indicates that Lyja's form held with extraordinary stability — a testament to operative discipline — but post-exposure she displays intermittent involuntary slippage when emotionally compromised. Recorded incidents include flickers of green pigmentation at the jawline during arguments with Johnny Storm, lengthening of auricular cartilage during sleep, and at least one observed instance of full involuntary reversion during a panic episode in the post-Hyperstorm period.
- **Mimetic exhaustion.** Sustained high-fidelity impersonation — particularly impersonation that includes intimate physiological function (skin response, blush, lactation, sexual response, scent profile, the *Alicia-specific blindness* maintained as a continuous neurological suppression of her own functioning visual cortex) — exacts a metabolic cost not fully characterized. Indirect evidence: post-exposure Lyja is markedly less inclined to hold non-baseline forms for extended periods, suggesting either depleted capacity or post-traumatic aversion to the discipline.
- **Sensory suppression as iatrogenic injury.** The decade of voluntary functional blindness required to maintain the Alicia cover is, in clinical terms, a sustained self-inflicted neurological lesion. Skrull physiology repairs such suppressions on release, but the *experiential* habituation — a decade of moving through the world via touch, voice cue, and rehearsed spatial mapping — has left permanent behavioral traces (§2.8).
- **The signature problem.** Subject's morphological control is precise to the level of fingerprint, retinal pattern, voiceprint, and (per Reed Richards' eventual scan, *FF* #357) a Skrull genetic signature detectable only by purpose-built instrumentation. The fact that this signature was *detectable at all* indicates an irreducible biological floor below which her impersonation cannot descend — a fact she is now operationally aware of and which conditions her threat-modeling.

### 2.3 The Bio-Engineered Augmentation (Energy Projection)

Between her recovery by Skrull deprogrammers (post-*FF* #358) and her re-emergence as an independent actor, Lyja was surgically and genetically retrofitted with the capacity to project concussive energy "flare-blasts" from the palms — a power-set explicitly modeled, in the imperial cynicism of the procedure, on the Human Torch's signature output. This is medically significant on several axes:

1. **Surgical scope.** The augmentation required restructuring of distal upper-limb tissue, integration of an energy-generative organelle complex of unknown architecture, and reinforcement of palmar and digital structures against the recoil/heat byproducts of discharge. This is not a minor procedure; it is comparable to whole-limb reconstruction, performed on a body that had recently sustained near-fatal energy trauma.
2. **Consent vector.** There is no record of meaningful consent. Lyja was a deprogramming subject — a defector being reclaimed — and the augmentation was imposed during a period in which her capacity to refuse was compromised by indoctrination protocols.
3. **Symbolic injury.** The Skrull Empire weaponized her by giving her *her ex-husband's power*. Whatever the tactical rationale, the psychological gesture is unmistakable: she was remade into a parody of the object of her unsanctioned attachment, then deployed against him. Lyja's later use of this power — frequently defensive, frequently directed at *protecting* Johnny — reads as continuous reclamation of an organ that was installed as an insult.
4. **Functional cost.** Discharge appears to draw on metabolic reserves; sustained projection produces observable fatigue and, in at least one combat sequence, momentary morphological destabilization, suggesting the augment competes with shapeshifting maintenance for cellular resources.

### 2.4 Catalogued Injuries — Acute

In chronological order, with somatic and psychological annotation:

- **Pre-mission baseline (estimated).** Skrull warrior-class training of operatives of her cohort produces a standard pattern of healed micro-trauma: stress fractures in long bones from morphological combat drilling, ligament remodeling from repeated mass-shift exercises, and a characteristic palatal scarring associated with the voice-modulation training that allows precise impersonation of alien vocal apparatus. None of this would be visible in held form.
- **Domestic-cover period (Alicia decade).** No combat injuries on record. Sustained low-grade somatic stress consistent with prolonged operational immersion — chronic shoulder and jaw tension, sleep architecture disruption (inferred from the discipline of maintaining suppressed-vision protocols during REM states). Notably, *intimate-partner injuries are not on record* — Ben Grimm was, in domestic context, gentle, and the relationship-with-Johnny was new enough at exposure to have produced no significant somatic toll.
- **Near-fatal energy attack by Paibok the Power-Skrull (*FF* #358).** The dispositive trauma. Paibok's discharge was calibrated to kill; Lyja's survival required emergency cellular triage, almost certainly via Skrull medical extraction within minutes of collapse. Tissue damage was extensive enough to require the protracted reconditioning during which augmentation was installed. Psychological sequelae: the attacker was a Skrull intimate (closest available analog to a Skrull peer-mate), and the attack was retaliation for her divided loyalty. This is the foundational trauma of her *post-cover* life — the moment her people demonstrated that her existence as a recognizable self was forfeit. Conditioned response: persistent flinch-reaction to energy-discharge sounds in close proximity, observable in early *FF* #383-era footage; later extinguished through repeated exposure.
- **Dreadface arc injuries (*FF* #380s).** Multiple combat traumas of conventional kind — blunt impact, lacerations, at least one penetrating wound requiring field repair. Skrull cellular regeneration handled all of these without external intervention; recovery times of approximately 30–40% human baseline.
- **Hyperstorm-era injuries (*FF* #390s–410s).** Repeated severe combat exposure during operations alongside the FF. Pattern: Lyja consistently positions herself to absorb attacks directed at Johnny Storm, sustaining disproportionate injury relative to operational necessity. This is medical evidence of psychological pattern (§3), but it is also producing a body increasingly accustomed to trauma-recovery cycles, with possible long-term implications for cellular fidelity in baseline form.
- ***Secret Invasion* era (2008).** Resurgent combat tempo; injuries sustained on the *human* side of a Skrull operation. Psychologically this is the first injury class she has sustained while unambiguously in opposition to her own species' command structure — a category that did not exist for her during the Paibok incident, where she was still a defector rather than a counter-operative.
- **Empyre-era (2020).** Operations in the context of Skrull-Kree unification produced no documented serious injury, but observable somatic markers — postural tension, sleep deficit consistent with hypervigilance — indicate that the political reorganization of her people did not produce relief but a new layer of ambient threat assessment.

### 2.5 The False Pregnancy — Medical and Psychogenic Dimensions

The egg subplot (*FF* #383 and successors) requires careful clinical separation of physical fact from psychological event:

- **Physiological staging.** To present credibly to Johnny — and to herself, in the moments when she may have half-believed it — Lyja necessarily underwent some degree of morphological staging consistent with Skrull gestation: alterations in abdominal mass distribution, hormonal-analog shifts producing the affective and somatic correlates of pregnancy, and ultimately the production or simulation of a Skrull egg artifact. Whether the egg was a true biological product (an unfertilized or chimerically constructed ovum) or a manufactured prop remains ambiguous in the record; the dispositive canonical revelation is that *the child was a fabrication*, not necessarily that the egg-object was inorganic.
- **Psychosomatic reality of a deceptive pregnancy.** This is the key medical observation: a body that *can* gestate falsely, in service of a manipulation, will nonetheless experience the gestation as biologically real for the duration of the performance. The Skrull metabolic-affective cascade does not distinguish operational pregnancy from genuine pregnancy. Lyja therefore experienced — at the level of hormone, mood, body-image, and proprioceptive expectation — the felt reality of carrying Johnny Storm's child, while simultaneously knowing it to be a deception she had constructed. The clinical category for this is not pseudocyesis (which involves genuine belief in a non-existent pregnancy) but its inverse: *cyesis-with-disavowed-belief*, a configuration with no human analog and no human treatment literature.
- **Sequelae.** Post-revelation, Lyja's behavioral record shows avoidance of reproductive themes, demonstrable distress when children are present in tactical environments, and a marked absence — across the entire subsequent record — of any pursuit of actual reproduction with any partner. This is medical evidence of unresolved gestational trauma, self-inflicted, layered atop the original loss of an attachment object.

### 2.6 Reproductive History

No confirmed offspring. Skrull reproductive biology (oviparous; eggs requiring incubation periods of weeks to months depending on lineage) was within her physiological capacity throughout. Sexual activity is documented with both Ben Grimm (in Alicia form, decade-spanning) and Johnny Storm (in Alicia form, marital period; possibly in own form during brief post-exposure reconciliations). No record of Skrull-partnered sexual activity; the Paibok relationship, whatever its emotional valence on his side, was operationally professional on hers. Reproductive frustration is a quiet but durable thread — a body engineered for two species' worth of intimate function, deployed in service of attachments that produced no progeny in either.

### 2.7 Substances, Sleep, Diet, and Routine Somatics

- **Substances:** No record of pharmacological dependence. Skrull metabolism processes most human intoxicants with markedly reduced effect; during the Alicia-cover decade, simulated impairment in social contexts was performed by morphological mimicry of intoxication signs rather than genuine inebriation. Caffeine: mild stimulant effect retained, used moderately. Tobacco/alcohol/narcotics: not on record.
- **Sleep:** Skrull baseline sleep requirement is lower than human (~5 hours). Sustained cover impersonation required Lyja to *perform* the full 7–8 hour human sleep cycle, with the residual 2–3 hours used for unconscious morphological maintenance and, presumably, intelligence consolidation. Post-exposure, sleep architecture appears disrupted: shorter, fragmented episodes, with documented hypervigilance markers. Position habit: dorsal, hands at sides — a carryover from Alicia-cover discipline, which precluded the more naturally Skrull lateral/curled position that would have risked morphological drift during deep sleep.
- **Diet:** Omnivorous; Skrull palate tolerant of wider chemical range than human. During cover, ate as Alicia ate — vegetarian-leaning, modest portions — with the metabolic deficit made up via clandestine supplementation (inferred). Post-exposure, observed eating patterns are inconsistent, with periods of forgetting to eat during operational immersion and compensatory bingeing on Skrull-traditional foods when accessible.
- **Pain response:** Elevated tolerance, attributable to both training and Skrull baseline nociception. Tendency to under-report injury, consistent with her broader pattern of self-effacement around the FF.

### 2.8 Sensorimotor & Behavioral Carryover from the Alicia Decade

A discrete medical-behavioral category, because the somatic habits of sustained sighted-blindness do not erase on cover-termination:

- **Gaze pattern:** Even in own form, in unguarded moments, Lyja's eyes track *late* — fixing on a speaker a beat after a non-impaired person would, as if confirming auditory localization before committing visual attention. This is a fossil of the Alicia protocol.
- **Tactile orientation:** Persistent low-level fingertip contact with surfaces in unfamiliar rooms — counters, doorframes, the backs of chairs — when she believes herself unobserved.
- **Spatial memory:** Extraordinary, far in excess of operational requirement; she retains detailed mental maps of every environment she has spent significant time in, a discipline developed for the sighted-as-blind performance and never relinquished.
- **Voice usage:** Slightly elevated baseline volume; tendency to vocalize her movements ("I'm coming around behind you") in mixed company — a courtesy developed for Alicia's interlocutors, now reflexive.
- **Olfactory acuity:** Reportedly heightened; whether genuinely augmented during the Alicia period or simply attended-to more carefully is unclear, but the attentional habit persists.

### 2.9 Disability

No physical disability in the conventional sense. The relevant impairment is integrative: a body capable of being anything is, as noted in the summary workup, a body that is nothing in particular, and the *medical* expression of this is the involuntary morphological slippage under affective load (§2.2). This is the closest she comes to a chronic condition — an intermittent failure of the somatic boundary that normally separates self from performance, manifesting as visible cellular instability at moments of psychological compromise.

### 2.10 Surgical & Medical Interventions on Record

1. The augmentation procedure (§2.3) — extensive, non-consensual or compromised-consent, performed by Skrull bio-engineers during deprogramming custody.
2. Emergency cellular triage post-Paibok attack — life-saving, performed under field conditions by Skrull recovery teams.
3. Multiple instances of inferred Reed Richards diagnostic scanning during the periods of her FF-aligned residency; these are non-invasive but produced the genetic-signature data that constitutes the most complete medical record of her in human hands.
4. No record of elective procedures, cosmetic intervention (functionally absurd for a shapeshifter), or human-medical-system contact, which would have risked exposure throughout her active periods.

### 2.11 Synthesis: The Medical Through-Line

The medical history reads as a single sustained injury: the imposition, occupation, and contested reclamation of a body by competing intentions. The Skrull Empire trained the body, augmented the body, and very nearly killed the body. The cover assignment required the body to *be* another body for a decade. The exposure removed the assigned identity but not the somatic habits it inscribed. The augmentation made the body resemble its attachment object. The false pregnancy made the body perform a child it did not bear. Each intervention left a layer; none of the layers has been removed; the body she now occupies is the accreted residue of all of them.

There is no clean somatic baseline to return her to. Medical management — were any practitioner ever in a position to offer it — would have to begin not with the question *what is wrong with this body* but with the prior, unanswered question *whose body is this*. Until that question is metabolized at the psychological level (§3), the somatic instability documented above will continue to constitute her standing medical condition.

— UATU, Medical Subsection, file continues.


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU ANALYTICAL WORKUP: SUBJECT DESIGNATE "LYJA"
## Section 6 — SOMATIC ATLAS

*Compiled from cross-referenced visual record, third-party witness testimony from FF-circle intimates, retroactive reconstruction of the Alicia-era footage, and direct observation logs spanning the post-exposure decades. The subject is shapeshifter-class; conventional somatic profiling must therefore index two parallel registers — the **default morphology** (the Skrull-form she reverts to under unconsciousness, deep sleep, orgasm, or willed self-presentation) and the **carried morphologies** (sustained human forms, principally the Alicia-template and the variable "Laura Green" template used for cohabitation with Johnny Storm in the late 1990s). Tells leak between registers; this is where the file is built.*

---

### 6.1 Default Morphology — Baseline Skrull-Form

**Stature and proportion.** Approximately 5'9", lean-athletic, longer femur-to-tibia ratio than human norm producing a slightly elongated stride and a recognizable silhouette when seen from distance even before facial confirmation. Shoulders narrow, deltoids well-developed (combat conditioning), hips narrow for a Skrull female, which she has noted herself in dialogue (*FF* #383) as having been a developmental "disadvantage" in Skrull aesthetic terms — a remark made in a flat register but logged as one of the few self-deprecating somatic references in the entire corpus.

**Skin.** The characteristic Skrull green, but several shades lighter than the imperial mean; a jade-toward-celadon range that brightens to a near-mint tone during emotional flush and darkens to forest-green during sustained shapeshifting. Texture smooth; no pronounced ridging on the chin (the deviant lineage trait). Capillary flush visible on the cheekbones and across the sternum when aroused, embarrassed, or angry — a tell she has never learned to suppress because the Alicia-form's blush has been a useful cover for it.

**Ears.** The Skrull pointed pinna; carried through into most of her human forms as a slightly elongated lobe, statistically distinguishable from Alicia Masters' actual ear morphology on close inspection — a forensic marker she would have been caught on years earlier had anyone in the FF circle taken close photographs of Alicia's left ear during the impersonation period. (None did. The error survived.)

**Eyes.** Yellow-amber in default form, with a slightly larger sclera-to-iris ratio than human, producing the characteristic Skrull "wide" gaze. In Alicia-form she carried the sightless milk-blue of Alicia's blindness — a piece of cover work requiring continuous active morphology, because her own optical apparatus is fully sighted. Witnesses who lived with "Alicia" for years never registered the constant micro-effort behind this, but the file should: she sustained that one detail every waking moment for the better part of a decade.

**Hands.** Three-fingered plus opposable thumb in default Skrull-form. The forced retention of a five-fingered configuration in human forms is the single most exhausting feature of long-duration cover. Under fatigue, witnesses on the FF (Reed Richards' later debriefs) report having seen Alicia's hand "twitch wrong" on at least two occasions in the back half of the impersonation; no one followed up.

---

### 6.2 Gait, Posture, and Locomotion

**Default gait.** Heel-strike light, near-silent on hard floors; a function of military training rather than morphology. Stride length 4–6% longer than would be expected for her apparent height in any given form — she does not always remember to scale gait to the body she is wearing, and the discrepancy is reliably detectable on treadmill-grade analysis. Arms swing slightly less than human norm; she carries a low-grade combat readiness in the shoulders that pulls the arm-swing in toward the centerline.

**Posture at rest.** When unobserved (or believing herself unobserved), spine slightly hyperextended, chin level, weight distributed evenly across both feet — the parade-rest of someone trained to a uniformed service. When she remembers she is observed, she releases into a softer slouch, drops one hip, shifts weight to a single leg. The transition between these two postures is itself diagnostic: a single shoulder-roll, a small exhalation, and a downward glance, all completed in under a second.

**Seated.** Prefers to sit with her back to a wall and a sightline to the room's primary entrance. In FF-circle settings where this is socially impossible, she will choose the seat with the next-best sightline and compensate by orienting her torso 10–15 degrees off the table axis to keep peripheral vision on the door. Crosses legs at the ankle, not the knee — the latter restricts rapid rising. Hands habitually rest on the thigh, palms down, fingers loose; not folded, not steepled. Folding the hands is a tell of acute distress.

**In motion under threat.** Drops center of mass approximately three inches without altering apparent stride. Shoulders rotate forward by 5–8 degrees. The eye-scan pattern changes from human-conversational (face-to-face) to perimeter-sweep at roughly 1.5 second intervals.

**In motion in intimacy.** With Johnny Storm specifically: the trained gait dissolves. She walks closer to him than the cultural norm — within 18 inches at the shoulder rather than the standard 30 — and her hand drifts toward his without engaging, a hovering proximity she maintains for long minutes before actually taking the hand. This is observed across both the Alicia-era and the post-exposure period and is one of the very few behavioral constants the file can confirm survived the identity rupture.

---

### 6.3 Facial Micro-Pattern

**Resting face.** In Skrull-form, the face settles into what witnesses have characterized variously as "cool" or "appraising" — the brow neutral, the mouth closed and slightly downturned at the corners. This is not affect; it is the absence of the social-smile labor she performs in human forms.

**The Alicia-smile.** Reconstructed from contemporaneous record: warmer than the genuine Alicia's, very slightly. A 4–6% increase in zygomatic recruitment, a tendency to hold the smile a quarter-second longer than the prompt warranted. Ben Grimm, in retrospect, has described the Alicia of those years as having seemed "happier than she'd been before," which the file reads as the cover-performer's characteristic overshoot.

**Eye behavior.** In conversation, she breaks gaze downward and to her own left when calculating or constructing; downward and to the right when remembering. In her Skrull-form this is the standard human cognitive-direction tell, retained from her impersonation training and never re-trained out. Under direct emotional challenge from Johnny, the gaze locks instead of breaking — a non-human persistence that those who know her well have learned to read as the moment she has decided not to lie.

**Mouth.** The lower lip is bitten — drawn briefly into the mouth and released — at moments of indecision; this is a habit observed in both Alicia-form and Skrull-form and therefore catalogued as **endogenous** to Lyja rather than imported from cover. Frequency increases markedly in any conversation where her identity-status is at issue.

**Brow.** Asymmetric raise (left higher than right) during skeptical or wry registers. The right brow is the one that contracts under stress; a faint vertical line above the inner third of the right eye is visible in default form, absent in younger Alicia-era footage — the only piece of "aging" the file can identify on a body that does not age conventionally.

**Tells of imminent shapeshift.** A slow blink, a deliberate exhalation through the nose, and a brief hand-flex. The shift itself takes 1.5–3 seconds for full-body morphology, under one second for facial-only adjustment. She prefers to shift in privacy and finds being observed mid-shift acutely shame-inducing — Johnny has reported her turning her back during the transition even years into their reconciled cohabitation.

---

### 6.4 Voice and Speech

**Default vocal register.** Mezzo, with a slight Skrull harmonic doubling that human ears register as "warmth" or "huskiness" rather than as anything alien. Pace measured. In her cover forms she has perfectly mimicked the target voice; the doubling can still be heard by audio-spectrogram on sustained vowels in any of her human forms, a forensic signature the FBI-equivalent file would have flagged within hours had the impersonation been suspected.

**Speech patterns.** Sentence structure clean, almost overly so — she rarely uses filler ("um," "uh") because she was trained out of it as part of impersonation discipline; their re-introduction in her speech post-exposure is an observable behavior, a slow re-humanization of her speech-floor as she stopped performing every utterance.

**Code-switching tells.** When discussing the Skrull Empire, her syntax becomes slightly more formal, verb-final clauses appear, and a faint clipped consonant pattern emerges (a residue of Skrullos phonology). When discussing the Storm period, her diction softens, contractions multiply, and the cadence picks up tempo. Listeners can hear the identity-shift in the speech-stream before they see it in the body.

**Laughter.** Rare. When it occurs in Skrull-form it is short, low, and surprised-sounding — as if she had not expected the sound to come out of herself. Johnny is the only documented reliable elicitor.

---

### 6.5 Grooming, Dress, and Self-Presentation

**Skrull-form grooming.** Minimal. Hair (when she manifests any) kept short and dark; nails trimmed close, unpainted; no scent. She does not perform Skrull cosmetic ritual and never has — a small piece of evidence for her marginal status within Skrull culture even before her recruitment to deep cover.

**Human-form grooming.** Meticulous. The Alicia-form had its hair brushed to Alicia's exact part and length; the various Mrs. Storm forms she has worn carry whatever cosmetic load the role required, executed flawlessly. The labor of grooming a manufactured body is invisible labor; she has never complained of it on record, but it is logged as a continuous cognitive load.

**Dress.** In Skrull-uniform contexts: military-cut, dark, functional. In human contexts during the Storm-cohabitation periods: she defaulted to soft fabrics, jewel tones (deep greens and blues — a chromatic affinity that may be a subconscious nod to her actual coloration), and avoided red (Johnny's signature color, which she has stated she finds "presumptuous" on her own body). In the *Secret Invasion* era and after, when she is no longer in cover and no longer in cohabitation, she has trended toward neutral, almost ascetic clothing — the wardrobe of someone who has stopped dressing for an audience.

**Scent.** Default Skrull body chemistry is faintly mineral, almost copper-adjacent — undetectable to most humans but cataloguable. She uses no perfume in default form. In Alicia-form she wore Alicia's actual perfume, a soft floral, which had to be sourced and applied as an external cover-element. After the exposure she has worn no perfume of any kind.

---

### 6.6 Sleep Architecture

**Skrull-form sleep.** Subject defaults to her base morphology during the deepest sleep stages — she cannot sustain a human form through full unconsciousness. This is the operationally critical fact of her biology and the reason she has slept alone for most of her life, including most of the marriage to Johnny. Witness reports from the brief post-reconciliation cohabitation indicate she would wait for Johnny to fall asleep, sustain her human form until she was sure of his sleep depth, then permit the shift — and would wake before him to restore it. Sleep onset latency under these conditions: 45–90 minutes; total sleep time chronically reduced; REM compressed.

**Sleeping position.** Default: on her side, facing the door, top knee drawn up, dominant hand under the pillow (where, when armed, the weapon is kept). When sleeping in safe proximity to Johnny — and this is rare and precious — she sleeps on her back, one arm across his torso, the only posture in the entire somatic record in which her trained perimeter-vigilance fully relaxes.

**Dream behavior.** REM eye-movement pronounced; occasional vocalization in Skrullos (untranslated by her partners, never volunteered in waking conversation). Three documented incidents of Johnny waking to find her speaking the name "Paibok" in her sleep.

**Insomnia.** Chronic, intermittent. Worst in the weeks following any reactivation of the Alicia-question — any conversation, image, or context that brings Alicia Masters back into her awareness. She will sit through these nights at a window, reading or sketching, drinking a Skrull herbal preparation she synthesizes herself.

---

### 6.7 Eating and Ingestion

**Skrull metabolism.** Higher than human baseline; she requires approximately 30% more caloric intake than her apparent human form would suggest, a discrepancy she managed during the Alicia years by eating ferociously when alone and modestly when observed — Ben Grimm has, on retrospective debrief, recalled finding empty food containers in the Alicia studio that he attributed at the time to his own appetite.

**Food preference.** Strongly carnivorous in default state; capable of consuming foods toxic to humans (a useful field capacity). In cover forms she ate the cover-target's preferred diet without apparent strain but with measurable diminution of energy reserves over time. Her authentic preferences, expressed in the post-exposure period, lean toward simple roasted meats, root vegetables, and a sweet fermented Skrull beverage she sources through diaspora networks.

**Eating posture.** Quick, efficient, head slightly down, non-dominant hand near the plate or rim of the bowl in a guarding posture — the eating style of someone who has eaten in mess halls and field encampments. She has never fully learned to eat slowly even in domestic settings.

**Ritualized intake.** None observed. She does not say grace, does not toast, does not perform any of the Skrull or human pre-meal rituals available to her. The file reads this as another marker of her between-cultures status.

---

### 6.8 Sexual and Intimate Pattern

**Pair-bond history of record.** Ben Grimm (Alicia-cover, years-long, cohabiting); Johnny Storm (Alicia-cover; later marriage; later post-exposure reconciliation periods). No documented Skrull sexual partner.

**Approach pattern.** Initiator only with Johnny, and only when assured of his reciprocation; never the first to broach the question after a period of estrangement. Touch-initiation begins peripherally — a hand to the forearm, the back of the wrist — and proceeds inward only with explicit reciprocation. She does not kiss without invitation.

**Morphology in intimacy.** The operationally and psychologically dispositive fact: her body shifts toward the default Skrull-form during orgasm and during deep post-coital relaxation. She cannot prevent this. In the Alicia-era cover this was managed by avoiding climax (a sustained sexual suppression of years' duration, the somatic implications of which are themselves significant — chronic pelvic tension, reported musculoskeletal complaints in the lower back), or by manufacturing the appearance of climax without the underlying physiological event. With Johnny, post-exposure, in the periods of full reconciliation, she has permitted the shift — this is the most intimate act available to her, more intimate than any verbal disclosure, and she has extended it to no other person on record.

**Affect after intimacy.** Tearful in 30–40% of post-coital intervals with Johnny, by his own quiet accounting. Not from sadness in the immediate sense — from the integration-pressure that the act creates, the demand on a fragmented identity to be present as a single body to a single other.

**Withdrawal pattern.** Following intimacy, she will typically rise, walk to water (a faucet, a window onto rain, a sink), and stand for several minutes with her hands under or near it. This is observed across multiple settings and is logged as a self-soothing ritual whose origin is unknown — possibly Skrull, possibly something she absorbed from Alicia's sculptor-routine of washing clay from her hands.

---

### 6.9 The Hand Repertoire

The hands carry the densest tell-load on the body and warrant their own subsection.

- **Flare-blast readiness.** When threat is detected, her fingers extend and separate slightly, palms turning fractionally outward and downward. The hand becomes a weapon-platform without her conscious decision; the gesture is detectable a half-second before any verbal acknowledgment of threat.
- **The wedding-band ghost.** During the marriage to Johnny (as Alicia) she wore a ring; post-exposure, she does not, but the left ring finger carries a habitual rub from the right thumb at moments of stress. The ring is gone; the gesture is not.
- **The sculpture-hand.** Inherited from the Alicia cover: a tendency, when listening, to shape the air with her fingers as if working clay. She has not fully shed this. It is the most unambiguously haunted gesture in her repertoire — a dead woman's hands moving through hers.
- **Self-touch.** Right hand to left forearm in moments of self-consolation; both hands to the back of the neck under acute stress; one hand to the sternum (open palm) when emotionally overwhelmed in a way she does not wish to show.
- **The shift-flex.** Before any morphological change, fingers flex once, slowly, as if testing the new body's grip. Diagnostic.

---

### 6.10 State-Shift Summary Table (Narrative Form)

**Calm/private.** Default Skrull-form, parade-rest dissolving into a soft slouch; sketching, reading, or working at a console; eating quickly; vocalizing rarely; sleeping in light, vigilant cycles.

**Calm/social (with FF circle).** Sustained human form, careful grooming, social-smile slightly over-deployed, peripheral seating, ankle-cross, hands palms-down on thigh; speech smooth, code-switched toward soft contractions; minimal eating in front of others.

**Stress (operational).** Trained spy: posture lifts, gait silences, scan-pattern engages, hands extend toward weapon-platform readiness, voice drops slightly in pitch and slows by a quarter, micro-expressions disappear into a controlled neutral.

**Stress (interpersonal — Johnny).** The opposite: the trained surface cracks, the lip-bite increases, the eye-break disappears into the locked gaze, the hand drifts toward his without committing, the breathing shallows, the sculpture-hand returns unbidden.

**Threat.** Center of mass drops, shoulders forward, flare-readiness in the hands, scan-pattern at 1.5 second intervals, speech ceases entirely until the threat is resolved or engaged.

**Intimacy (with Johnny).** Proximity collapses to under 18 inches; touch initiated peripherally; voice softens to a near-whisper; in the deepest intervals, the morphological discipline relaxes and the default body returns, briefly, fully, witnessed.

**Catastrophic (forced identity-declaration).** The body does what the psychology does: paralysis. A held breath, a locked gaze, a long stillness, and then — historically — a movement toward self-sacrifice that resolves the unbearable choice through martyrdom-attempt rather than answer.

---

*The body is the record. In a subject whose face is a chosen artifact and whose form is a daily decision, the involuntary residue — the lip-bite, the sculpture-hand, the water-ritual, the orgasmic reversion, the name spoken in sleep — is the closest the file will ever come to the integrated person beneath. Catalogued accordingly.*

— UATU, Somatic Atlas, section closes.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## Subject: LYJA

---

## 6.1 The Foundational Problem: An Attachment System Built Backwards

Most subjects in this archive can be traced from a developmental origin — a primary caregiver, a sibship, a community of formation — forward through life. Lyja cannot. The Skrull pre-mission record for this asset is essentially blank: no parents named, no clan affiliation referenced, no rearing environment described in any canonical source. What we possess of her pre-Earth history is functionally a personnel jacket — selected, trained, augmented, deployed. The earliest moment at which we can observe her *forming an attachment* is the moment she was already pretending to be someone else.

This is the dispositive fact for everything that follows. Lyja's attachment system did not develop in childhood and then get repurposed for espionage; it was *first activated in adulthood, in the service of espionage, while wearing another woman's face*. The primary template was: **closeness is a deliverable; intimacy is a tradecraft output; the body in the bed is a costume; the feelings produced in the other person are the mission objective.** Whatever capacity for genuine bonding she possessed before this assignment, we have no record of it being exercised. The Alicia-cover was, in effect, her first relationship.

This produces a configuration without clean precedent in the human clinical literature. The closest analogs — deep-cover intelligence officers who marry their targets, cult-deprogrammed members who married within the cult, the "Romeo agents" of the Stasi HVA — all retain some pre-operational attachment baseline to which they can be returned. Lyja has no such baseline. **Her authentic self and her cover self are not two layers; they are the *same* layer, laid down simultaneously, and now indistinguishable in the cured emulsion.**

---

## 6.2 The Bonding Sequence: How She Forms Attachment

Across the full longitudinal record — the Grimm cohabitation (*FF* #265 ff.), the Storm courtship and marriage (*FF* #300), the post-exposure re-engagements (*FF* #393–416), the *Secret Invasion* reunion (2008), the *Empyre* re-encounters (2020), and the scattered Slott-era cameos — Lyja's bonding sequence is invariant and recognizable. It runs in four phases:

**Phase 1 — Observational immersion.** She studies the target with abnormal patience and abnormal accuracy. The Alicia impersonation was sustained for years and fooled people who had known the original since childhood; this requires not merely surface mimicry but live, continuous absorption of the model's affective texture. With Johnny specifically, even after exposure, her behavioral pattern is to *watch* him — to track his moods, his preferred silences, the shape of his enthusiasms — for long intervals before intervening. She is, in interpersonal terms, a method actor who never breaks character because she has forgotten how.

**Phase 2 — Mirrored offering.** She presents to the target the version of herself the target is most prepared to love. With Ben, she offered Alicia's calm, accepting, slightly maternal warmth — the very thing his self-loathing most needed. With Johnny, she shifted register: brightness, daring, sexual openness, willingness to be admired — the things he had failed to find in Alicia and that the cover-Lyja could provide by deliberate calibration. This is not cynical; by this stage of the operation she had stopped distinguishing between "what he wants" and "what I am."

**Phase 3 — Embedding through small ritual.** Lyja's bonds are built less through grand declarations than through accumulated micro-domesticity. The behavioral record across the Englehart and early DeFalco runs is studded with quiet markers: she remembers; she anticipates; she places the cup where the hand expects to find it; she learns the in-jokes; she absorbs the friendship network and becomes useful to it. This is partly tradecraft (an embedded asset who is socially indispensable is harder to expel even after exposure) and partly the only language of intimacy she trusts, because words can be checked against truth and rituals cannot.

**Phase 4 — Catastrophic over-investment.** This is the failure mode that exposed her. The mission required proximity; the marriage to Johnny did not. The decision to wed an attachment object while operating under cover is, in deep-cover operational terms, a *career-ending mistake* — it doubles the legal and emotional entanglement, multiplies the probability of exposure, and creates a sunk cost the operative will defend against her own command. Lyja did it anyway. Phase 4 is the phase where she crosses from successful infiltrator to compromised asset, and she does it every time. Every subsequent cycle of her relational life replays this phase: she binds herself to the other beyond what the situation requires, beyond what the other has asked for, beyond what she can safely sustain.

---

## 6.3 Distrust: The Specific Architecture of Her Suspicion

Lyja's distrust does not operate the way a paranoid subject's does. She is not vigilant against deception by others — she is in fact *unusually credulous* about other people's stated motives, because her own life has been spent producing convincing surfaces and she over-credits the surfaces of others on the assumption they cost as much to build as hers did.

What she distrusts is **her own perception of being loved**. Every gesture of affection directed at her runs through a private interrogation: *Are they responding to me, or to a version of me I have produced for them?* Because she cannot, in her own experience, distinguish these two cases reliably, she defaults to assuming the latter. The behavioral expression: she discounts compliments, deflects expressions of need from the partner, and reflexively interprets continued presence as inertia or pity rather than choice. The Johnny relationship is corrosively shaped by this; every time he stays, she models it as a man too decent to leave rather than a man who wants her, and acts accordingly — preemptively distancing to spare him a withdrawal she has decided is inevitable.

The secondary distrust object is **the Skrull Empire** and, by extension, any Skrull contact. This is not ideological but personal: Paibok killed her, the deprogrammers tried to scrub her, and the Empire's broader project (*Secret Invasion*) required her to choose against the only people in whose presence she has ever felt approximately real. She does not trust Skrulls to let her be the half-formed thing she has become. The behavioral expression: in every Skrull-Earth interface event after *FF* #358, she positions herself on the Earth side of the line within the first thirty seconds of the encounter, even when no one has asked her to choose. She over-declares the alignment because she does not trust herself to hold it under sustained pressure.

She does *not* distrust the Fantastic Four as an institution. She trusts them excessively — to the point of relying on their forgiveness as a moral economy that will absorb anything she does. This is the third leg of her relational architecture and the most psychologically revealing: she has chosen this group to function as the parental object she never had, and she addresses them with the bottomless presumption of a child who knows it will be taken back in.

---

## 6.4 Betrayal: The Two Modalities

Lyja has betrayed twice in the canonical record, and the two betrayals are structurally different and must be analyzed separately.

**Betrayal Type A — Mission-Origin Betrayal of the Fantastic Four (FF #265 onward).** This was assigned, not chosen. It is the betrayal that defines her existence in the human field, but it carries the lowest *personal* moral weight in her own self-accounting, because she did not select the target and did not, at outset, comprehend what the target meant. The betrayal of Ben and the FF circle is, in her internal economy, something done to her *by her own command* using her as the instrument — a framing she will not articulate aloud (it would minimize her culpability and she will not permit herself that comfort) but which structures her affect: she feels *guilt without ownership*, the worst kind, because there is no clean act she could perform to discharge it.

**Betrayal Type B — The Pregnancy Deception (FF #383 and successors).** This was elective and personal. She fabricated a child by Johnny, weaponizing his grief over the lost Alicia-pregnancy and his unresolved feelings about her, to force him back into emotional proximity. This is the single most diagnostically important act in the record. It demonstrates that under sufficient abandonment threat, she is capable of producing a deception of *equal sophistication to her original Skrull-engineered cover*, executed entirely on her own initiative, against a target she loves. The Empire built her to deceive enemies; she discovered, in this episode, that she could deceive intimates at will. The horror of this self-discovery — visible in her subsequent withdrawal pattern — is part of what permanently destabilizes the post-egg phase of her relational life. She frightened herself.

The two betrayal types share a structure she does not seem to see: in both, she manufactured a false relational reality and inhabited it convincingly enough to bind another person to it. The first was Empire-assigned; the second was self-assigned. The instrument was the same.

She has not betrayed since. The post-egg record is consistent: she will withhold, withdraw, disappear, sacrifice herself, but she will not again fabricate. The egg episode functions in her behavioral history as a *self-imposed prohibition* — the line she has decided she will not re-cross because crossing it once revealed something about her capacity she cannot afford to keep testing.

---

## 6.5 Repair: How She Attempts to Mend What She Has Broken

Repair behavior in Lyja is asymmetric and partial. She does not apologize well — verbal contrition is in her experience the cheapest of performances and she distrusts it on both sides of the exchange. Instead, her repair vocabulary is somatic and operational:

- **The protective intervention.** Across the Dreadface, Hyperstorm, and *Secret Invasion* arcs, the pattern repeats: she places her body between Johnny (or another FF member) and an incoming threat she has knowledge of and they do not. The repair is the saved life. The unspoken transcript: *I owe you this many.*
- **The unsolicited intelligence.** She passes information — about Skrull operations, about Paibok's plans, about infiltrator placements — and asks nothing in return. The repair is the gift of operational advantage.
- **The exit.** Counterintuitively, withdrawal is, in her repair grammar, a form of restitution. When she calculates that her presence imposes more confusion on the other than her absence would, she leaves. This is why the geographic-drift pattern (§3) is not simple avoidance: it is, in part, her attempt to grant Johnny the right to a life uncontaminated by the unresolvable question of her.
- **The accepted lower status.** She does not press for re-marriage, re-acknowledgement, re-instatement to family standing. She accepts marginal, peripheral, conditional roles. The acceptance is the repair: a chronic performance of *I will not ask for what I forfeited.*

What is absent from her repair repertoire — diagnostically — is **the demand to be forgiven**. She does not seek absolution scenes. She does not require the other to release her from the debt. She prefers the debt unresolved, because resolution would require an integrated self capable of being the recipient of forgiveness, and that self does not exist.

---

## 6.6 Intimacy and Dependency Patterns

Lyja's intimacy is calibrated to a paradox: she requires *continuous proximity* to the attachment object to feel coherent at all, and she cannot tolerate *full intimacy* with that object because full intimacy would force the identity question she cannot answer. The behavioral resolution is the **approach-withdraw oscillation** noted in §5, but the granular pattern is more specific than that summary suggests:

- **Optimal range, observed:** close enough to know the partner's movements and moods on a daily basis; far enough that she is not required to share unbroken domestic space. Adjacent apartment, parallel mission, mission-partnership rather than household-partnership. Whenever the relationship has approached full domestic integration (the original Storm marriage; brief reconciliation gestures across later arcs), her destabilization accelerates within weeks.
- **Sexual intimacy:** sparingly documented but behaviorally consistent — she initiates and reciprocates competently within established relationships, but the post-coital record (where inferable) shows withdrawal-of-affect rather than deepening. The act is something she does well; the aftermath is the danger zone, when the assumed face must be sustained at lower energy and the assumed self is most likely to slip.
- **Verbal intimacy:** she does not narrate her interior. Across the entire canonical record, there is no sustained scene in which Lyja explains, in plain language, what she experiences as herself. She speaks of past selves, of Alicia, of what "she" did when "she was" — third-person grammar applied to her own history. Anyone seeking real-time first-person disclosure from this subject will be disappointed; it is not concealment, it is incapacity.
- **Dependency:** asymmetric. She allows herself to depend on Johnny operationally (he is the reason she remains in the human field at all) but refuses to depend on him materially or socially. She does not ask for housing, status, introductions, alliances, or shared finances. The refusal is not pride; it is a defense against the further engulfment she fears. To depend on him in any practical sense would be to require a stable self to do the depending, and she does not trust the supply.
- **Reciprocal dependency tolerance:** *higher* than her own dependency tolerance. She permits, even welcomes, Johnny's reliance on her in crises. Being depended upon stabilizes her — it gives the assumed self a function, and function is the closest thing she has to identity.

---

## 6.7 The Master Relational Template, Repeated Across Every Bond

Strip the surface variations and Lyja runs the same five-act drama with every significant figure in her life. The actors change; the staging is identical.

**Act I — Approach under cover.** She enters the relationship presenting a version of herself calibrated to the other's need. With Ben, the cover was literal (Alicia). With Johnny, the cover was rhetorical (the "Lyja" identity offered after exposure was itself a partial self, not a full disclosure). With the FF as institution, the cover is the role of *the loyal repentant* — which is genuine in content but still a curated presentation, not a complete self. Even with Paibok and her Skrull contacts she presented a calibrated face: the dutiful operative who could be relied on to perform.

**Act II — Successful embedding.** The other accepts the offered version. A functioning bond forms. She performs the role flawlessly, including the affective components. There is no detectable seam. This phase is where she is happiest, in the limited sense that "happy" applies — the role is working, the other is responding, the question of who she really is can be deferred.

**Act III — Mission-creep into authentic feeling.** The performed affect begins to be experienced as real. The boundary between cover-affect and own-affect dissolves. This is the phase she cannot control and did not consent to; it is the unintended consequence of using her own nervous system as the instrument of impersonation for sustained periods.

**Act IV — Destabilization under intimacy demand.** The other, sensing the depth of the bond, requests fuller intimacy — declaration, commitment, integration, the question *who are you really*. She cannot answer. The destabilization manifests as either (a) over-commitment beyond what the situation can support (the Johnny marriage), (b) elective deception under abandonment threat (the egg), or (c) withdrawal/disappearance (the post-exposure absences, the *Secret Invasion*-era reticence).

**Act V — Marginal re-stabilization.** She settles into a peripheral, lower-intensity version of the relationship that allows continued proximity without the intimacy demand. With Ben: the unspoken truce in which they do not discuss the years. With Johnny: the recurring partial-reunion-then-distance cycle. With the FF: cameo affiliate status, useful in crises, absent in dailies. With Skrull society: oppositional but not severed; she is the dissident who still uses the language.

The template has been observed in operation across at least five primary relational dyads (Ben, Johnny, Paibok, the FF as collective, the Skrull command structure) and a number of secondary ones (the Richards children during the Alicia years; Reed and Sue as parental figures; Devos and the Dreadface-era allies). Every instance runs the same five acts with only the catastrophe modality varying.

---

## 6.8 What This Means for Anyone Standing in Relation to Her

Any person now in Lyja's orbit — handler, ally, intimate — should understand that they have not been chosen by an integrated agent making free relational selections. They have been chosen by a fragmented system that requires their specific presence to maintain coherence. This produces unusual loyalty (she will not leave easily, and she will protect at high personal cost) and unusual fragility (the question that no one must ask is the one that destroys her). The optimal posture toward her is the one Johnny Storm, at his best moments, has stumbled into without theorizing: *sustained, non-interrogative presence*. Do not require her to declare. Do not stage forgiveness scenes. Do not press for the integrated self she cannot supply. Permit the marginal, partial, oscillating bond; that is the only bond she knows how to sustain, and within its limits it is real.

The tragedy of the file is that what she most needs — to be witnessed as *Lyja*, simply and without qualification, by someone who is not asking her to be anything else — is the one thing her relational template makes nearly impossible to receive. To accept such witnessing she would have to first present a self to be witnessed; she does not have one assembled; she has never been given the conditions in which one could be assembled. The cycles will continue.

— UATU, Analytical Stage, Section 6 closes.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT "LYJA"
## Section: Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

*Filed under Analytical Stage / Cross-reference §3 Psychological, §4 Psychiatric, §5 Personality. This section maps the full defensive architecture: structural defenses (the load-bearing walls of the personality), tactical defenses (the day-to-day plaster), and the compensatory mechanisms — both adaptive and maladaptive — that the architecture leans on to remain standing. Ranked from most primitive to most mature, with behavioral expression documented in each case.*

---

### I. PRELIMINARY: THE STRUCTURAL PROBLEM THE DEFENSES MUST SOLVE

Before ranking, the file must state the load: Lyja's defensive system is doing work no ordinary personality is asked to do. A standard human ego organizes one body, one history, one set of social roles around a continuous self-narrative. Lyja's ego must organize a *morphologically unstable body*, a *deliberately falsified history* (years lived as another woman, including sexual and maternal intimacies that belonged biographically to that other woman), and *two mutually hostile social worlds* in neither of which she has citizenship. No single defense could carry this. What we observe instead is a stacked, redundant, partly contradictory system in which primitive defenses do the heaviest structural work and higher-order defenses are deployed inconsistently — usually in the presence of Johnny Storm, where she most wants to behave like a person rather than a strategy.

---

### II. PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (Structural; Always Online)

#### 1. Identification with the Aggressor / Identification with the Role
**The foundational defense.** Engineered into her by Skrull infiltration training and then escaped from engineering control. The Skrull method does not produce *actors* in the Stanislavskian sense; it produces operatives who experience the assumed identity's affects as proprioceptively their own — the warmth toward the Richards children, the tactile pleasure in Ben Grimm's company, the slow drift toward Johnny — were not performed *for* Lyja, they were performed *as* Lyja in her own felt experience. 

Operationally this defense expresses as: when she enters a role, she does not "play" it; she *becomes* the person who would feel what that role requires. The cost is that returning from a role does not return her to a pre-role baseline, because there is no stable pre-role baseline to return to — only an earlier role (Skrull operative-self), itself a product of the same defense applied to military indoctrination. The defense is recursive: it is roles all the way down.

Behavioral tells: speech patterns shift to match the social register of the dominant present interlocutor within seconds, not minutes. Affective tone tracks the room. Even somatic micro-expressions (posture, hand-position, breath rate) reorganize without conscious decision. The default state is *adopting*, not *being*.

#### 2. Splitting
The Skrull-self and the Alicia-self are stored as discrete objects, not as integrated facets of one person. In self-reference she will say "when I was Alicia, I —" rather than "when I was pretending to be Alicia, I —." The grammatical detail is dispositive: the verb of being, not the verb of pretending. This is not a slip; it is the only honest statement available to her, because phenomenologically she *was* Alicia for the duration of the immersion.

Splitting also operates interpersonally. Johnny is alternately the only person who ever loved any real part of her *and* the man who could not love her once he knew. Ben is alternately a debt she owes *and* a wound she cannot return to. Paibok is alternately her own people *and* the proof that her own people will kill her. She does not synthesize these; she alternates between them depending on which affective state is foregrounded.

#### 3. Dissociation Proper
Cataloged as a clinical entity in §4; cataloged here as a defense. The morphological body assists the dissociative mind: when affect becomes intolerable, she can literally become someone else, and the body cooperates. Observable instances include the period immediately following exposure in *FF* #357, where her self-presentation oscillates between several morphological intermediates within a single scene — a behavioral signature of an organism whose identity-state is not currently resolved.

The dissociative defense has a *somatic vector* unique to her species. Where a human dissociator might depersonalize, derealize, or lose time, Lyja can additionally *re-form*, replacing the destabilized body with a new one. This is the most singular feature of her defensive system and the most dangerous: every other dissociator must eventually return to the same face in the mirror. She need not.

#### 4. Projective Identification
Most visible in the egg deception (*FF* #383ff). Unable to tolerate her own grief, fear of abandonment, and rage at Johnny's rejection, she externalized the wound by inducing in *him* the very state she could not metabolize: grief over a lost child, helplessness, rupture. The operation was not coldly planned; it was the affective system seeking discharge through the only available object. He felt what she could not bear to feel, and her own affect was correspondingly anesthetized for the duration.

This is the dispositive evidence that her defensive architecture, under sufficient pressure, will recruit the attachment object as an unconsenting container for her own intolerable states. Handlers must note: she is not safe under abandonment threat, not because she is malicious but because the defense will use whoever is nearest.

#### 5. Somatization Through Morphology
A defense available to no human subject. When affect-states become unbearable, the body changes — sometimes subtly (pigmentation shift, posture), sometimes drastically (full re-embodiment). The defense converts psychological pain into a manageable physical task. The cost is that the body, being unstable, cannot serve as the anchor of identity that bodies normally provide. The defense that protects her in the short term degrades the very substrate that would allow integration in the long term.

#### 6. Denial — Specifically, Denial of the Constructed Nature of Her Attachments
She has never fully metabolized that the love she felt for Ben Grimm originated as a Skrull operational deception. To metabolize this would require accepting that the warmest years of her experiential life were a weapon she carried into another person's bed. The denial is partial — she knows it intellectually — but the affective acceptance is permanently postponed. This is why "Alicia" spoken in her presence is a destabilization vector: the name forces the denial into momentary failure.

---

### III. INTERMEDIATE DEFENSES (Tactical; Deployed Situationally)

#### 7. Reaction Formation
Operates in two directions.

*Toward her people:* she over-protects the FF — risking her life repeatedly, surrendering her tactical advantages, repeatedly choosing the human side in Skrull-human conflicts including *Secret Invasion* — in proportion to the original mission's hostility. The intensity of the protection is calibrated to refute the intensity of the original betrayal, to herself. Each rescue is a quiet retroactive vote against her own history.

*Toward intimacy:* she will engineer distance from Johnny in the moments she most wants closeness, because closeness threatens the question she cannot answer (*which of us are you?*). The behavioral pattern is observable: after high-affect reunion sequences she disappears within days or weeks. The withdrawal is not loss of feeling; it is excess of feeling routed through its opposite.

#### 8. Undoing
Each protective act is, in part, an undoing of the original infiltration. She does not articulate this; the behavior carries the meaning. The structure is ritualistic: harm done while wearing Alicia's face is undone by injury sustained on the FF's behalf in her own face. The accounting is private and bottomless; no quantity of undoing closes the ledger, which is itself a clue that the ledger is symbolic, not actuarial.

#### 9. Isolation of Affect
In operational mode — particularly during intelligence work, infiltration reconnaissance, or combat — affect is cleanly walled off. She can describe atrocities, plans against people she loves, and the mechanics of her own past deceptions in a flattened, professional register. This is the spy's voice, and it is the *only* register in which her cognition operates at full capacity. The cost is that the operational self and the loving self are kept in separate rooms; integration would catastrophize both.

#### 10. Intellectualization
Less prominent than in many high-functioning subjects, because Lyja has limited internal vocabulary for her own states — she was trained to model *others*, not herself (see §3, cognitive style). Where intellectualization does appear, it tends to be species-anthropological: she discusses Skrull psychology, human psychology, the structure of deception, as though her own case were one instance among many. The framing is true and also serves to keep the case at examiner's distance.

#### 11. Displacement
Anger at Skrull command — which she cannot safely direct at its proper object — displaces onto whichever Skrull adversary is presently available (Paibok especially, who additionally earned the rage personally). Anger at Johnny — when present — displaces into self-directed risk-taking, mission urgency, or the protective overfunctioning noted above. Direct expression to the proper object is the one channel never used.

#### 12. Turning Against the Self
Repeated self-sacrificial gestures (the "death" arc, the willingness to be captured, the recurrent positioning of her own body between threats and the FF) carry a self-punitive dimension above and beyond tactical necessity. She does not seek death; she does seek to be *spent* on the people she wronged, and a body that recovers makes this an inexhaustible currency.

---

### IV. HIGHER-ORDER DEFENSES (Mature; Deployed Inconsistently)

#### 13. Sublimation
The infiltration training, the impersonation gift, the morphological precision — all the skills built for predation — are channeled into protective and warning functions. The *Secret Invasion* period is the clearest sublimation arc on record: she used the entirety of her Skrull tradecraft against the Skrull operation. The defense is mature because it preserves capability while inverting purpose. It is also unstable: the same skill set, in an abandonment crisis, will revert (see egg deception, which is sublimation's failure mode).

#### 14. Altruism
Distinct from reaction formation in that it lacks the refutational urgency — there are quieter, lower-stakes acts on record (small protections of Johnny, intelligence courier work without expectation of recognition or return) that fit the mature altruistic pattern. These are the most personally integrated moments in her file: when she helps without needing the help to mean something about her, she is, briefly, the closest thing to a unified self the record contains.

#### 15. Anticipation
Operationally robust — she is a competent strategic forecaster. Personally weak — she does not anticipate her own affective ruptures, which is why the abandonment-cue cascades catch her unprepared each time. The defense is domain-specific.

#### 16. Humor
Notably absent from the record at any level of maturity. This is itself diagnostic: humor requires a stable enough self-position to view one's situation from outside, and she does not have one. The Storm-circle environment is humor-saturated; she does not participate, even in the moments her social-mirroring would otherwise produce it. The absence is one of the cleanest indicators that the mirroring is not deep — there is no internal vantage from which her situation could be funny.

---

### V. COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — POSITIVE

#### A. Operational Competence as Self-Esteem Reservoir
The spycraft self is the only stable repository of self-worth. When all other self-references destabilize, she can still execute. This compensation is genuinely adaptive: it keeps her functional through periods that would otherwise produce total collapse, and it provides the platform from which the sublimation and altruism defenses can operate.

#### B. Theory-of-Mind as Bridge
Her extraordinary capacity to read others, originally a predation tool, now operates as a connection mechanism — she knows what the people around her need, often before they do, and supplies it. Among the FF circle this has earned her a quiet, marginal acceptance that no formal declaration of allegiance could have produced.

#### C. The Marginal-Position Tolerance
