Most subjects with her degree of identity disturbance cannot bear marginality; they demand inclusion or exit. Lyja can sit at the edge of a community for years without escalation. This is partly resignation, partly mature acceptance, partly the absence of any alternative — but functionally it permits her to remain in proximity to the attachment objects without forcing the rupture that a demand for status would produce. It is the most pragmatically successful compensation in the file.

#### D. Conscience as Organizing Principle
With the Skrull ideological framework dissolved and no replacement ideology adopted, her conscience — present, active, painful — has become the de facto organizing principle of her behavior. This is unusual and favorable: where ideology has failed, an internal moral sense has held. Prognostically this is the single most important positive datum.

#### E. The Capacity for Witnessed Moments
She seeks, and occasionally finds, moments in which she is seen *as herself* rather than as one of her roles. These are rare and brief, but they are real — usually with Johnny, occasionally with peripheral FF members who knew her only post-exposure. Each such moment is metabolized for years afterward. The capacity to receive being-seen, when offered, is intact; the prognosis depends on whether such offers continue.

---

### VI. COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — NEGATIVE

#### a. Morphological Escape from Difficult Affect
The body that can be anything is the body that can flee anything. When confronted, she can literally leave the face that is being addressed. The escape route undermines every therapeutic or integrative possibility, because integration requires sitting still with a single self long enough to be recognized.

#### b. Roleplay as Substitute for Intimacy
She offers Johnny — when she offers anything — a version of herself calibrated to what he can accept, rather than what is true. The calibration is loving in intent and devastating in effect: it deprives the relationship of the friction by which a real partner is known. He has never met her without a costume; she has never appeared without one to be met in.

#### c. Self-Sacrificial Avoidance of Forced Choice
The catastrophic-stress response — the martyrdom-attempt — functions to *avoid* the choice between Skrull and human allegiance by removing the chooser. This is a defense disguised as virtue. It is operationally legible (she will do it again) and it allows the underlying integration problem to remain permanently unaddressed.

#### d. Geographic and Temporal Drift
Long disappearances between appearances in the record correspond, behaviorally, to retreat phases. She vanishes when the attachment situation becomes unworkable, returns when the absence becomes worse than the situation, and the cycle repeats. The drift compensates by providing distance, and it costs her every accumulated foothold each time.

#### e. The Weaponization Capacity (Held in Reserve)
The egg deception established that under sufficient narcissistic injury, her defensive system will recruit cruelty. This is not a frequent pattern, but it is a documented one, and it is the lowest floor of her behavioral envelope. Handlers and intimates must treat it as a live possibility, not a historical aberration.

#### f. Refusal to Speak Atonement
She atones in action but never in word. This is partly mature — talk is cheap, action expensive — but partly defensive: spoken atonement would require her to specify *as whom* she is apologizing, and that specification would force the integration she is organized to avoid. The silence preserves the dissociation.

---

### VII. RANK ORDERING (Primitive → Mature)

1. Identification with the role / aggressor *(structural, always online)*
2. Splitting *(structural)*
3. Dissociation, including somatic-morphological *(structural)*
4. Projective identification *(emergent under abandonment threat)*
5. Somatization through morphology *(continuous; uniquely available)*
6. Denial of the constructed nature of original attachments *(partial; chronic)*
7. Turning against the self *(frequent; ritualized)*
8. Displacement *(routine)*
9. Reaction formation *(routine; bidirectional)*
10. Undoing *(routine; ritualized)*
11. Isolation of affect *(operational settings)*
12. Intellectualization *(limited; species-anthropological register)*
13. Anticipation *(operational domain only)*
14. Altruism *(present; growing)*
15. Sublimation *(present; reversible under stress)*
16. Humor *(absent — diagnostic)*

The center of gravity sits firmly in the primitive band. The mature defenses exist and are real, but they ride on top of structural defenses that have not been dismantled and that, under sufficient stress, will resume command of behavior.

---

### VIII. OPERATIONAL SUMMARY

Lyja's defensive architecture was built by the Skrull Empire to hold a single mission together; it now holds a person together for whom the mission has been over for decades and for whom no replacement organizing structure has been provided. The architecture is doing more than it was designed for, and it is succeeding — she is functional, she is moral, she is capable of love and of help — at the cost of an integration she has never been permitted, by circumstance or by her own design, to attempt.

The defenses to watch, in order of operational salience:
- **Projective identification under abandonment cue** (the egg-deception channel).
- **Morphological escape from confrontation** (any pressure to stand still in one identity).
- **Self-sacrificial avoidance of forced allegiance choice** (any framing that demands she pick a side).
- **Roleplay-as-intimacy with Johnny** (the chronic, low-grade undermining of the one relationship her stability most depends on).

The defenses to encourage, in order of prognostic value:
- **Altruism in low-stakes form** (the integration moments).
- **Sublimation of tradecraft into protective work** (the only channel in which her full capacity and her conscience operate together).
- **Marginal-position tolerance** (the platform on which everything else stands).
- **Receipt of being-seen, when offered by someone with standing to offer it.**

— UATU, Analytical Stage, Section closes.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7: LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE

## Subject: LYJA (Skrull; alias-of-record "Alicia Masters," 1984–1991; later "Laura Green," "Ms. Storm," various)

---

### Preliminary Framing Note

The clinical material that follows is reconstructed by reverse-inference from observed behavior across approximately thirty-five years of recorded activity (*Fantastic Four* #265 ff., 1984 — *Empyre* and adjacent titles, 2020–present). Two frameworks structure the analysis: (a) Putnam's *discrete behavioral states* model of dissociation, which is more useful for this subject than the classical DID schema because it accommodates state-shifts without requiring frank amnesia; and (b) the Fonagy/Bateman *mentalization* framework, which captures the asymmetry — pronounced in Lyja — between accurate other-mentalization and impoverished self-mentalization. Where helpful, Linehan's biosocial model of emotion dysregulation is invoked for the borderline-spectrum features, and Herman's complex-PTSD sequencing for the post-exposure decade. Skrull cultural-developmental data is sparse; inferences about her formation period are flagged as such.

The profile is organized in decade-bands rather than calendar years because the in-story compressions and real-time publication gaps make month-level resolution spurious. Within each band, three vectors are tracked: **affect regulation**, **cognitive style**, and **self-concept**, with cross-references to the precipitating events that shifted each.

---

### I. Formation Period (pre-mission; reconstructed from inference, ca. T-minus several decades)

No direct canonical material exists for Lyja's childhood, conscription, training, or pre-mission identity. The reconstruction is therefore probabilistic, built from (a) what Skrull martial-imperial culture is shown to produce in cohort members (Paibok, the warrior-caste; the deprogrammers of *FF* #358 ff.; the Empire's general use of impersonator-assets); and (b) the residual capacities and incapacities visible in her later behavior.

- **Affect regulation in formation:** Almost certainly externally scaffolded — that is, regulated by command structure, training discipline, and mission-objective framing rather than by an internal soothing system. The adult Lyja's strikingly *competent* affect-management under operational stress, paired with her catastrophic dysregulation around intimate ruptures, is the signature of someone trained to modulate affect *in performance of a role* and never trained to modulate it *as a self*. The Skrull program presumably valued the former and had no use for the latter.
- **Cognitive style in formation:** The impersonation discipline required of her — sustained, multi-year, deep-cover identity adoption — would have been selected for and then drilled into the configuration we see later: hypertrophied theory-of-mind, granular behavioral mimicry, suppression of spontaneous self-reference. The training, by design, would have *atrophied* the metacognitive habit of asking "what do I want / feel / think, as distinct from what would the cover want / feel / think." This is the deficit that becomes catastrophic later.
- **Self-concept in formation:** Likely thin and instrumental from the outset. The Skrull impersonator-asset doctrine, to function, requires an operative whose self-concept is small enough and flexible enough to be subordinated indefinitely. Selection probably favored candidates already low on identity-rigidity — perhaps orphaned, low-caste, or otherwise unrooted Deviants whose pre-existing identity investments were modest. The retrofit of energy-projection powers (§2 of main file) indicates command saw her as worth augmenting, which in turn implies she had performed well in the only domain where her self-concept was anchored: the work.

The clinical headline of the formation period: **she was made into a person whose self could survive being anyone, and was therefore a person whose self could not survive being one thing.**

---

### II. The Cover Decade (ca. *FF* #265 — #357, real-time 1984–1991): "Alicia"

This is the longest single behavioral data-band in the file, and paradoxically the one in which "Lyja" qua Lyja is least observable, because she was, by design, not present. What we are reading is the second-order evidence of her psychology *as inferable from what the cover did and did not do*.

**Affect regulation.** During the cover period, Lyja's affect-regulation system was, in effect, *outsourced to the persona*. She felt what Alicia would feel; she modulated by Alicia's templates. This worked — for years, with zero recorded operational slippage — and it worked too well. The clinically critical observation is that the cover did not merely *display* warmth toward Ben Grimm; it *generated* warmth, because the impersonation discipline does not distinguish between performed and experienced affect once the role is sufficiently deep. By the time of *FF* #296–300 (the slow drift from Ben toward Johnny under Englehart), Lyja-as-Alicia is making *romantic* choices that exceed mission parameters. The marriage to Johnny in #300 is the watershed: an act undertaken in-role that no mission objective required and which, in retrospect, can only be read as the cover-self pursuing its own affective interests under the mission-self's nominal authority. **This is the inflection point at which the persona's affect-system began to dominate the operative's.**

**Cognitive style.** Hypervigilant in-role mentalization of every FF member; continuous threat-modeling against detection; near-total suppression of self-reflective cognition. The Skrull-self was, during this decade, reduced to a small administrative process — mission updates, threat assessment, periodic command contact — running underneath an increasingly autonomous Alicia-process. The structural metaphor that fits the evidence is not "spy in disguise" but **a parasitic host arrangement in which the host began to consume the parasite.**

**Self-concept.** Functionally unitary, falsely so: she experienced herself as Alicia, with the Skrull-self as a kind of secret she kept from her own foreground awareness except when operationally necessary. This is consistent with what Putnam describes in chronic role-immersion: the foregrounded state acquires the phenomenological texture of "me-ness" and the backgrounded state begins to feel like a memory or a secret rather than a self. The seeds of the later dissociative disturbance are planted here, and they are planted by *success*, not failure.

**Period-defining datum:** The marriage to Johnny Storm (*FF* #300) is not a mission objective being executed; it is the persona executing a life-choice. By the close of this decade, Lyja the operative no longer fully controls the asset she is supposed to be.

---

### III. The Exposure and Decompensation Decade (*FF* #357 — ca. #416, plus the Heroes Reborn interregnum; real-time 1991 — ca. 1996)

The most clinically dense interval in the file. This is the decade in which Lyja, having been compulsorily *re*-extracted from the Alicia-persona by exposure and by Paibok's near-killing of her, has to attempt — with no internal scaffolding for the task — to construct a "Lyja" who can hold the ground between the two.

**Affect regulation.** Collapses, then re-stabilizes at a much lower competence floor. The pre-exposure operative could go years without observable dysregulation; the post-exposure Lyja is dysregulated at moderate stress and catastrophically dysregulated at attachment-rupture cues. The sequence visible across #358 through the early #380s is textbook acute-onset complex-trauma decompensation: dissociative shifts in self-reference (she begins, in this period, to talk about "Alicia" in the third person, sometimes within the same speech-act in which she lays claim to Alicia's memories), affective lability between protective courage and tearful collapse, and the appearance — new in the file — of explicitly *vindictive* affect. Linehan's biosocial model is useful here: a high-sensitivity nervous system (the impersonator's selected trait) meeting an invalidating environment (the human side rejects her as a fraud; the Skrull side condemns her as a defector and tries to kill her), with no validating community on either side. The pregnancy deception (*FF* #383 ff.) is the prototypical Linehan-pattern parasuicidal communicative act translocated from self-harm to relational sabotage: *"I will create a wound large enough that you cannot leave."*

**Cognitive style.** Other-mentalization remains hypertrophied (she remains an excellent reader of Johnny, of Ben, of the FF's internal politics). Self-mentalization, however, begins for the first time to be *attempted* — and it fails almost continuously. She does not know what she wants because the wanting-organ was built to want what the cover wanted. The cognitive signature of this decade is the *unanswered question*: every time she is asked, directly or implicitly, "what are you, now?", the response is action (a sacrificial intervention, a withdrawal, a stratagem) rather than answer. Action substitutes for self-knowledge because action does not require the metacognitive apparatus she was never given.

**Self-concept.** This is the period in which the fracture stabilizes into the structure that will persist for the rest of the record. By approximately *FF* #400, three discrete self-states are observable:
1. **Lyja-as-Skrull-loyalist** — vestigial, increasingly invoked only as a marker of what she has rejected; affectively flat when foregrounded.
2. **Lyja-as-Alicia** — the haunting; spoken of in the third person but also unconsciously re-enacted in micro-behaviors (vocal cadence, certain gestures, particular sympathies toward the Richards children); affectively warm but accompanied by guilt when noticed.
3. **Lyja-as-Johnny's-wife** — the contested present-tense identity; affectively volatile, alternating idealization and self-protective withdrawal.

No integrating fourth state — no "Lyja simply as Lyja" — appears in the record during this decade or any subsequent decade. The clinical name for this configuration is *structural dissociation of the personality*, intermediate form (van der Hart, Nijenhuis, Steele), with the apparently normal part fragmented across two functional identities rather than the more typical one.

**Period-defining datum:** The fabricated pregnancy. It is the single behavioral act in the file that cannot be explained by either her Skrull conditioning *or* her acquired human attachments and must therefore be attributed to the destabilized, partially-integrated Lyja attempting, badly, to act on her own behalf for what may be the first time in her life. That her first independent act was a cruelty is itself a datum about how little practice she had at being herself.

---

### IV. The Withdrawal Decade (post-Heroes Reborn through ca. *Civil War* / pre-*Secret Invasion*; real-time ca. 1997–2007)

Sparse appearances. The behavioral pattern of this interval is itself diagnostic: **she went away.**

**Affect regulation.** Inferred stabilization-via-avoidance. With the attachment objects removed from immediate proximity, the dysregulation triggers were removed; the operative-self could reassert itself as the dominant functional mode. This is not health; it is the dampening of symptoms by removal of stimuli, the equivalent of an agoraphobic's "improvement" upon staying indoors.

**Cognitive style.** Presumed return to operative baseline — mission-focused, externally-oriented, low self-referential activity. The geographic and social drift implied by her absence from the FF orbit during this period is consistent with the "geographic cure" pattern common in personality-disordered and complex-trauma populations who self-medicate identity-instability with movement.

**Self-concept.** Probably contracted rather than integrated. The three self-states identified above did not merge; they were sequestered, with the Alicia-state and the Johnny's-wife-state placed in storage and the operative-state foregrounded for daily function. The cost of this arrangement is the chronic low-grade dysthymia and meaninglessness that complex-PTSD theorists (Herman) describe as the long-tail consequence of unresolved identity-trauma. We do not have direct affect-state evidence for this period, but its absence is itself evidence: a person who was thriving would have surfaced; the silence is the symptom.

**Period-defining datum:** Absence. The fact that she did not, during a decade in which Johnny Storm was repeatedly in crisis, return to him.

---

### V. The Re-Engagement Decade (*Secret Invasion* through *Empyre*; real-time ca. 2008–2020)

She comes back, and the configuration that comes back is the one that left, minus some intensity and plus a measurable increment of self-awareness.

**Affect regulation.** Improved relative to the decompensation decade, worse than the operative baseline. She presents during *Secret Invasion* as functionally competent, capable of sustained pro-FF action, and — importantly — capable of *tolerating proximity to Johnny without either collapsing into him or fleeing*. This is a real gain. It is also a fragile gain, achieved partly by the explicit reframing of her status as "ally, not wife," which allows her to occupy a defined role rather than navigate undefined intimacy. The role-scaffolding, again, does the work that self-scaffolding cannot.

**Cognitive style.** The asymmetric mentalization persists. What is new is a low-frequency, intermittently observable capacity for *retrospective* self-mentalization — she can, occasionally, narrate what she did during the decompensation decade with something approaching insight. ("I was not myself" is, for a subject who has never been certain of having a self, a more clinically loaded utterance than it sounds.) Prospective self-knowledge — what she will want next week, where she will be in a year — remains absent.

**Self-concept.** The three-state structure persists; the Alicia-state has become quieter (the real Alicia having long since reclaimed her own life, which removed the daily impersonation-cue), the operative-state has been redirected from Skrull-imperial service to a freelance pro-FF intelligence function, and the Johnny's-wife-state has been demoted to a kind of permanent past-tense that she can now reference without immediate dysregulation. *Empyre*'s Skrull/Kree reunification produces no observable integration of her diaspora identity — she does not become *more* Skrull when Skrulls become more legitimized — which is itself the strongest evidence that her Skrull-self has fully exhausted its motivating force. She is, by the end of this band, something close to **a stateless intelligence professional with private emotional commitments**, which is approximately as integrated as her structure permits.

**Period-defining datum:** The pattern of return-without-reclamation. She comes back to the orbit; she does not come back to the marriage, the species, or any singular identity claim. The marginality has stabilized into a chosen position rather than an inflicted one. This is, paradoxically, progress.

---

### VI. Cross-Decadal Synthesis

Three longitudinal trends, traced across the full record:

1. **The center of gravity of the self has migrated from the operative-state (formation) through the Alicia-state (cover decade) through florid fragmentation (decompensation decade) to a deliberately-occupied liminality (current).** The trajectory is not toward integration but toward *stable non-integration* — a position not unlike that of long-term-undercover intelligence personnel in the actual-world literature (Marks, *The Search for the "Manchurian Candidate"*; subsequent CIA/FBI deep-cover decompensation case studies), who often achieve functional adaptation only by accepting that the cover-self and the operative-self will never reconcile and structuring a life around the gap.
2. **Affect-regulation capacity has improved post-exposure but never returned to the operative-period ceiling, because the operative-period ceiling was achieved by the abolition of self-reference, which is no longer available to her.** She cannot un-know that she is more than the role; therefore she cannot regain the role's regulatory completeness.
3. **The cognitive asymmetry between other-mentalization (high) and self-mentalization (impaired) is the single most stable feature across all decades.** It is the formation-period training signature and it has not eroded. Any intervention that proposes to "help" Lyja must reckon with the fact that she does not have, and has never had, the equipment to know herself in real time — and that this is not a deficit of effort or will but of installed apparatus.

The clinical bottom line, decade-on-decade: **Lyja has not gotten better in the sense of resolving the disturbance; she has gotten better at living inside it.** For a subject whose original injury was the engineering of a self designed to be overwritten, learning to inhabit the un-overwritten gap may be the closest functional equivalent to recovery available to her. The dossier should not mistake this for cure. It should also not fail to credit it.

— UATU, Analytical Stage, Section 7 closes.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — SUBJECT "LYJA"

## Preface on Method

This section formalizes what the broader workup sketched. The presenting subject is a non-human intelligence operative whose neurobiological substrate is morphologically plastic and whose developmental milieu was a martial-imperial culture optimized for impersonation work. Standard Terran diagnostic frameworks (DSM-5-TR; ICD-11) therefore apply only by analogy. Where I deploy a category, I am asserting that the *behavioral phenomenology* maps onto that category with sufficient fidelity to be clinically useful — not that the underlying neurology is identical. I have privileged longitudinal behavioral evidence (a quarter-century of observed conduct from *Fantastic Four* #357 forward, retrojected to the period of impersonation beginning circa #265) over self-report, which in this subject is structurally unreliable: not from mendacity but from the absence of a stable self to report from.

Diagnostic confidence is graded throughout: **Established** (multiple independent behavioral episodes, low alternative explanation), **Probable** (consistent pattern, plausible alternatives bracketed), **Sub-threshold/Trait-level** (features present, criterion count insufficient), **Ruled out** (positive evidence against).

---

## 1. Principal Diagnosis

### Dissociative Identity Disturbance, atypical presentation, iatrogenic (operationally induced) — **Established**

**ICD-11 analog:** Partial Dissociative Identity Disorder (6B65), with the qualifier that the non-dominant identity states do not seize executive control through frank intrusion but were instead the *trained operating mode* for nearly a decade, inverting the typical clinical picture.

**Etiology.** The disorder is iatrogenic in the Skrull-operational sense. The Empire's deep-cover doctrine — as observable in the broader Skrull infiltration corpus and confirmed by Lyja's own functional repertoire — requires the field agent to construct and inhabit an alternate identity to the point that telepathic probe, polygraph-analog interrogation, and intimate-partner observation cannot detect the seam. This is not Stanislavskian role-work; it is structural induction of dissociative capacity, almost certainly reinforced by the morphological correlate (the agent's body literally becomes the target). For Lyja, the operation ran approximately a decade subjective, the longest immersion in any documented Skrull dossier, and crossed the threshold from instrumental performance into autonomous identity-state formation. The system was engineered; it then exceeded its engineering tolerances.

**Symptom presentation:**

- *Identity alternation in self-reference.* She speaks of "Alicia" in the third person when describing the impersonation period, then slips into first-person affective memory of events Alicia (the real Masters) never experienced — the cookouts at Avengers Mansion, the early nights with Ben. The pronoun-drift is observable and is not performative; it occurs even when no audience is present (interrogation transcripts of her conversations with Johnny in the *FF* #393–416 era).
- *Divergent affective valence across states.* Skrull-identified affect is flat, professional, mission-cadenced. Alicia-residual affect is warm, low-volume, deferential to Ben in particular. Lyja-as-Johnny's-wife affect is the most volatile — anxious, demanding, prone to collapse. The three are not blended; they alternate.
- *Distress at integration prompts.* Direct questions ("Who *are* you, really?") produce micro-flinch, eye-aversion, and either subject-change or a rehearsed-sounding declarative ("I am Lyja") delivered without the limbic signature that accompanies sincere self-reference in her other speech.
- *Absence of frank amnesia barriers.* She remembers across states. This is why the diagnosis is *partial* / *atypical* rather than full DID; the dissociation is one of identity-investment and affective system, not of episodic memory. This pattern is more consistent with the dissociative end of complex-trauma presentations and with documented deep-cover decompensation in Terran intelligence literature than with classical DID.

**Course.** Onset: training-era, formally activated at deployment (circa *FF* #265). Decompensation point: exposure (*FF* #357). Acute phase: capture and Skrull reconditioning attempts; the egg-deception arc (*FF* #383ff) is the symptomatic peak — a destabilized identity using one of its sub-selves (the wounded wife) to weaponize another (the trained operative) against the love object. Chronic phase: 1995–present, characterized by partial remission of the most florid features (no further deceptions on the egg scale) and persistence of the underlying identity diffusion. *Secret Invasion* (2008) and *Empyre* (2020) appearances show the same configuration two decades later — stable in its instability.

---

## 2. Comorbid Axis-I Diagnoses

### Adjustment Disorder, chronic, with mixed anxiety and depressed mood — **Established**

**DSM-5-TR analog:** 309.28, with the chronicity specifier (>6 months) satisfied many times over. Strictly the diagnosis requires that the disturbance not persist more than six months past the cessation of the stressor; since Lyja's stressor (the identity rupture) has never ceased, the diagnosis is in continuous force.

**Presentation:** Recurrent low mood without full melancholic features; anhedonia limited to social/relational domains (operational engagement still produces affect); episodic anxious agitation around the Storm relationship; behavioral withdrawal from both communities of origin and adoption. The "geographic drift" — extended absences from Earth, reappearances at the periphery of FF events — is the behavioral signature.

### Complex Post-Traumatic Stress (cPTSD) — **Probable**

**ICD-11 analog:** 6B41 (Complex PTSD).

The traumas are multiple, prolonged, and from circumstances of inescapability: indoctrination childhood (inferred from species-cultural context), the immersion impersonation itself (a trauma even when consensual at outset, as documented in deep-cover literature), the death-and-resurrection at Paibok's hands, the loss of the (false) child, the collapse of the home empire's coherence post-*Secret Invasion*.

The three cPTSD-specific clusters:
- *Disturbances in self-organization — affective dysregulation:* present, attachment-cued.
- *Negative self-concept:* present, severe. She positions herself as deserving of marginality.
- *Disturbances in relationships:* present, the central clinical fact.

Classical PTSD re-experiencing and hyperarousal are *not* prominent — no documented flashbacks, no hypervigilant startle pattern beyond operational baseline. Avoidance is intermittent. The diagnosis sits at *Probable* rather than *Established* on this account; the cPTSD framing fits the disturbance-in-self-organization domain but the intrusion criterion is weak.

### Prolonged Grief Disorder — **Sub-threshold but clinically significant**

The grief is for the fabricated child she briefly believed was real (her own deception caught her on the rebound — she conjured a phantom and then mourned it), for the Alicia-life she lived and lost, and for the Skrull mother-culture that no longer exists in the form that produced her. Symptomatic for years, not currently impairing in the criterion sense; flagged because it underwrites the depressive presentation.

---

## 3. Personality-Level Findings

### Borderline features, sub-threshold for full Borderline Personality Disorder — **Trait-level**

DSM-5 BPD requires five of nine criteria. Lyja presents:

1. **Frantic efforts to avoid abandonment** — *present.* The egg deception is the criterion-defining instance.
2. **Pattern of unstable and intense relationships** — *present.* Ben, Johnny, Paibok, the FF circle, the Skrull command structure: each is alternately idealized and devalued or fled.
3. **Identity disturbance** — *present, severe* — though this loads more naturally onto the dissociative diagnosis above.
4. **Impulsivity in self-damaging areas** — *absent.* No spending, substance, sexual-acting-out, or reckless-driving analogs. She is, if anything, over-controlled.
5. **Recurrent suicidal behavior, gestures, threats, or self-mutilation** — *absent at the self-directed level.* The pattern of self-sacrificial heroic gesture is adjacent and worth flagging (martyrdom as identity-resolution) but does not meet criterion.
6. **Affective instability** — *present,* attachment-cued rather than diffuse.
7. **Chronic feelings of emptiness** — *not reported,* but self-report is unreliable; observationally her behavior is consistent with a hollowed self even if she does not articulate emptiness as such. Score as *equivocal.*
8. **Inappropriate intense anger** — *one major documented episode* (the post-rejection deception arc). Not pervasive.
9. **Transient stress-related paranoid ideation or dissociative symptoms** — *the dissociative half is overwhelmingly present;* paranoid ideation is occupationally appropriate rather than clinical.

Strict count: 4 unambiguous + 2 equivocal. **Sub-threshold.** The reason this matters diagnostically is that the BPD label, if misapplied, would mis-orient management toward emotion-regulation skill-building when the actual core pathology is dissociative-identity in nature and the borderline-spectrum behaviors are secondary expressions.

### Dependent features — **Trait-level**

Less commented on in prior assessments but worth noting. The willingness to accept marginal status to remain near the attachment objects, the difficulty initiating major life decisions without reference to Johnny's position, the discomfort with being alone (drives the geographic drift *toward* rather than *away from* the FF circle in the long run) — these are dependent-spectrum. Not full PD. Important because it explains why she will not simply leave Earth and reconstruct elsewhere even when offered the opportunity (Skrull Throneworld, *Empyre*).

### Avoidant features — **Trait-level**

Avoidance of the integrated-identity question, of Ben Grimm specifically, of Skrull political reformation efforts that would require her to claim a Skrull civic identity. Functions to protect the fragile self-system from inputs it cannot metabolize.

---

## 4. Differential Diagnosis: What She Is Not, and Why

The differential is the most operationally important section of any deep-cover-defector assessment, because the wrong frame produces the wrong handling protocol and, with this subject, the wrong handling protocol is catastrophic.

### Not Antisocial Personality Disorder. **Ruled out.**

The relevant alternative hypothesis is that Lyja is a high-functioning predatory operative whose apparent remorse and pro-social conduct are continuing tradecraft. The evidence against:

- *Guilt is the engine, not a mask.* Behavioral expenditure on atonement is disproportionate to any operational benefit. She has, on multiple occasions, exposed her own position, sacrificed bargaining leverage, and accepted personal cost to warn or protect parties to whom she owes no operational obligation. ASPD is incompatible with this pattern at this volume.
- *The cruelty episode is affect-driven, not instrumental.* The egg deception did not advance any mission objective — it was retributive and self-soothing, the act of a wounded attachment system, not a predator's. ASPD-driven cruelty is cold and benefit-oriented; hers was hot and self-harmful (it permanently degraded her standing with the attachment object).
- *No pattern of charm-and-exploit cycling outside the original mission.* Post-defection, her interpersonal style is anxious-deferential, not seductive-instrumental.

### Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder. **Ruled out.**

- *Tolerates marginal status.* Accepts being the "estranged wife," the peripheral ally, the non-citizen of two empires. NPD does not tolerate this; NPD constructs grandiose compensations.
- *No grandiosity in self-reference.* If anything, she under-claims her capabilities and contributions.
- *Empathy intact and operative,* including empathy that produces personal cost.
- *Envy not observed.* She does not appear to envy Crystal, Sue, or any other woman in Johnny's orbit despite ample opportunity; her distress around them is grief-coded, not envy-coded.

### Not Histrionic Personality Disorder. **Ruled out.**

The dramatic gestures are tightly bounded to attachment ruptures. Outside those triggers, her interpersonal style is muted, professional, and self-effacing. HPD is pervasive and cross-situational; this is situational.

### Not Psychotic Disorder, any. **Ruled out.**

Reality testing intact across all documented encounters. The identity confusion is dissociative — she experiences multiple selves as *hers* with distress, not as external persecutors or grandiose alters with delusional explanatory systems. No hallucinations, no thought disorder, no negative symptoms in the schizophrenia-spectrum sense. The morphological shapeshifting can superficially mimic delusional identity claims to a naive observer; it is not.

### Not Major Depressive Disorder, recurrent. **Ruled out as primary.**

Depressive features are present but are explicable as adjustment-disorder and cPTSD sequelae. There is no documented episode meeting full MDD criteria for two weeks with the required symptom count and functional collapse independent of attachment-stressor. The depression is reactive, not endogenous.

### Not Bipolar Spectrum. **Ruled out.**

No documented hypomanic or manic episode. The affective oscillation is interpersonal-stressor-bound and rapid (hours-to-days), not the days-to-weeks polarity of bipolar episodes. The "high-energy" phases are operational/protective hyperfunctioning, not elevated mood with grandiosity, decreased need for sleep, or pressured speech.

### Not Factitious Disorder / Munchausen-spectrum. **Ruled out.**

The egg-deception episode superficially resembles factitious behavior (fabrication of medical/biological status to secure attention). It is distinguishable: the motivation was specific, attachment-rupture-cued, single-instance, and not repeated for the attention-seeking gain that defines factitious disorder. It is best classified as a dissociatively-mediated retributive deception, not a factitious presentation.

### Not "double agent with clean loyalties." **Ruled out — most important differential.**

This is the differential that matters for handling. A double agent has two real loyalties and chooses between them under situational pressure; the loyalties are intact even when the behavior is duplicitous. Lyja does *not* have two intact loyalties to alternate between. She has the *residue* of a Skrull civic identity she can no longer feel, the *residue* of an impersonated human identity that was never legally hers, and a *current attachment* to specific persons (Johnny, the FF) that is not the same thing as loyalty to Earth, to humanity, or to a polity. Treating her as a double agent — extracting product, assigning loyalty tests, demanding declarations — produces the high-stress paralysis-then-martyrdom response described in §5 of the prior workup, and yields nothing.

She is not divided; she is *unconstituted.* That is the diagnosis the file must hold.

### Not "fully redeemed defector." **Ruled out — second most important differential.**

The mirror error. Treating her as a clean asset, a Skrull-American success story, family by Johnny's marriage and welcomed in, ignores that the underlying identity-disturbance is *unremitted* and that under sufficient stress the egg-deception template can re-fire. She is safe to have nearby and dangerous to depend on for self-regulation under abandonment cue. The current Storm-family practice of warm-but-distant acknowledgment is, accidentally, the correct clinical handling.

### Not Autism-spectrum identity confusion or alexithymia. **Ruled out.**

Social cognition is high-functioning (required for the impersonation); affective recognition in others is acute; the self-referential difficulty is not a failure to identify internal states but a failure to integrate competing identified states into a single self-narrative. Distinct mechanism.

---

## 5. Course Specifiers and Prognostic Notes

**Longitudinal course:** Chronic with partial remission of acute features. The 1991–1996 period (exposure through Hyperstorm) is the acute/decompensated phase. 1996–2008 is a long fallow period of low-amplitude maintenance — geographic drift, occasional contact, no further deception-scale episodes. 2008 (*Secret Invasion*) and following marks a partial reorganization around the identity "Skrull-on-the-human-side," which is functional but not integrative — it remains an oppositional identity (defined by who she is *against*) rather than a positive one. *Empyre* (2020) and the Kree-Skrull reunification under Hulkling presented an integrative opportunity (a Skrull polity she could in principle re-belong to without forsaking her Earth attachments); her behavioral response — peripheral participation without commitment — confirms the prognostic ceiling.

**Risk profile:**
- Suicide risk: low under baseline conditions, moderate under combined abandonment + identity-demand stressor, with the specific risk presentation being self-sacrificial heroic gesture rather than overt self-harm.
- Violence risk to others: low. The single significant episode of harm-doing was affective-deceptive, not physical, and was not directed at non-attachment-object targets.
- Re-defection risk (return to Skrull cause): very low. The cause as she knew it no longer exists, and her behavior since *Secret Invasion* shows no orientation toward the reconstituted Skrull polities.
- Operational reliability risk: moderate-high under attachment-stress, low-moderate otherwise. Do not task her with operations where the attachment object is the operational target, the operational obstacle, or in proximate danger she cannot mitigate.

**Treatment indications (offered as analytical projection, not as recommendation for action by this office):** A long, slow, witnessed-self treatment course is theoretically indicated — the clinical analog would be a phase-oriented complex-trauma protocol (stabilization, processing, integration) with a therapist who could hold the multiplicity without demanding premature unification. No such resource is plausibly available to her. The functional substitute she has constructed — sustained low-intensity proximity to the FF circle, in which she is permitted to be ambiguously herself — is sub-optimal but is keeping her below threshold. Interventions that disrupt this arrangement (forced repatriation, demanded declarations, exclusion from the orbit) should be expected to produce decompensation on the 1991–1995 model.

**File status:** Active monitoring; no intervention indicated; flag any reproductive-themed stressor, any direct identity-demand from authority figures, and any signal of Johnny Storm forming a new primary attachment. These are the three predictable destabilizers.

— UATU, Psychiatric Section, file holds open.


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS: SUBJECT "LYJA"

*Compiled from longitudinal observation across the Defalco/Ryan run (FF #357–416), the Secret Invasion arc (2008), the Hickman-era Foundation cameos, the Slott FF vol. 6 appearances, and the Empyre crossover (2020). Cross-referenced against retro-observed conduct during the impersonation period (FF #265–356) now legible as performance-overlay.*

---

## I. THE BODY UNDER OBSERVATION — BASELINE TELLS

Lyja in a settled, unobserved-by-her-targets state defaults to a posture distinct from both the Alicia-overlay and the Skrull military bearing: shoulders carried slightly forward of true plumb, weight on the balls of the feet, hands typically out of pockets and visible. This is the spycraft baseline — readiness without aggression-display. The visible-hands habit is reflexive and predates the FF assignment; she does not put her hands behind her back even in domestic contexts, a tic that under the Alicia overlay was misread by the Richards household as "open" personality but is in fact an operative's discipline of never letting an interlocutor lose track of where her hands are.

**Resting facial micro-pattern:** the corners of the mouth held in a slight, false-neutral lift — the residue of years performing a sighted-woman's social smile that Alicia Masters herself, as a blind woman, would not have produced. This is a tell *against* the cover that no one ever caught: the real Alicia's resting face was less performatively pleasant, and no Skrull psychological prep accounted for it. The lift persists into the post-exposure period, visible in *FF* #393 and onward, even when she is no longer wearing Alicia's face. It is now hers.

**Eye behavior:** scans the perimeter of any room on entry in a counter-clockwise sweep, completing the arc in roughly two seconds, eyes returning to the dominant social object last. Under the Alicia cover she suppressed this — blind women do not scan — and the suppression cost her measurable cognitive load, which retrospective observers can identify in occasional dropped conversational threads and a slight latency in responding to questions during the impersonation years.

**Hand morphology under stress:** her shapeshift is least controlled at the fingertips. When emotionally taxed she has been observed to allow her fingers to elongate by perhaps a centimeter, or to revert pigmentation in the nail beds toward Skrull green, without conscious awareness. This is the leakage pattern, and it is the single most reliable physiological tell in the file.

---

## II. CALM

There is no true calm in the record. What presents as calm is one of three sub-states:

**(a) Operational calm** — when she has a defined task and a clear role. Affect is even, speech is economical, eye contact is direct but brief (1.5–2 second intervals, broken before threshold of intimacy-signaling). She drinks water, not coffee, in this state; the file notes no record of her ingesting stimulants, which is itself notable for a long-duration field operative and suggests either Skrull metabolism handles arousal regulation internally or she distrusts anything that might compromise morphological control.

**(b) Performed calm** — the Alicia residue. Hands folded in lap, head tilted approximately fifteen degrees toward the speaker, the false-neutral smile slightly more pronounced. This appears in social settings she does not control. It is the position from which she conducted years of intelligence gathering in the Baxter Building. The Richards children, on the rare occasions she has interacted with them post-exposure, trigger this posture involuntarily; the body remembers the role even when the mission has been dead for years.

**(c) Solitary calm** — observed only when she believes herself unwatched, which for a shapeshifter trained in counter-surveillance is rare. In these intervals she has been recorded (FF #401, a window-shot panel) sitting absolutely still, often at a window or above a city, with no Skrull and no human affect visible — a neutral, unreadable mid-state that may be the closest the file gets to baseline Lyja. The session typically lasts under ten minutes before some external or internal cue triggers re-performance.

**Decision habits in calm:** she defers small decisions (what to wear, where to sit, what to order if eating publicly) for a beat longer than baseline humans, because each micro-choice is an identity assertion she is not certain she has the standing to make. She compensates by mirroring — choosing what her current interlocutor chooses, half a second later. This is invisible to most observers but consistent across the record.

---

## III. LOW STRESS / MINOR FRICTION

**Conversational pressure (disagreement, mild challenge):** she will reformulate the other party's position in her own words before responding to it — a habit acquired from impersonation work (one cannot wear a face one has not first comprehended) that has carried into ordinary discourse. This is read by humans as exceptional empathic listening and is one reason the Storm family found "Alicia" so easy to love.

**Being teased (Johnny's primary register with intimates):** she over-laughs by approximately one beat. The laugh is genuine; the duration is calibrated. Old impersonation discipline: match the affect of the room plus a small margin to prove belonging.

**Mild physical discomfort:** she does not adjust. Shapeshifters do not need to shift weight, scratch, stretch, or fidget — they can simply re-form. The absence of normal human micro-adjustments is itself a tell; she sits too still for too long. She has learned to insert artificial fidgets at intervals when in human company, and these are visible as slightly mechanical: a hair-touch every four to six minutes, a weight-shift every eight to ten. The intervals are too regular to be biological.

**Being thanked:** marked discomfort. Eyes drop, the hand-tell flickers, a verbal deflection follows ("I should have done more," or in the Alicia-residue cadence, "it was nothing"). The discomfort is real — gratitude addresses a "you" she cannot accept as the recipient.

---

## IV. MODERATE STRESS

This is the band in which most of her on-panel behavior occurs and the band in which the dissociative slippage becomes visible to trained observers.

**Self-reference begins to drift.** In conversations under moderate stress she has used third-person constructions about her past selves ("when Alicia was with Ben…") and, less frequently, second-person ("you don't get to come back from that"). The second-person drift is the more clinically interesting: she is addressing herself as another, which is consistent with the dissociative working impression. Frequency: at least one such construction per extended dialogue in the post-exposure record.

**Protective overfunctioning toward Johnny.** Under moderate stress she will physically position herself between Johnny and any perceived threat vector, often without verbal coordination and sometimes when Johnny is in no realistic danger. This positioning is preconscious — she has been observed mid-conversation drifting roughly thirty degrees to interpose her body between Johnny and a doorway. The behavior is so consistent that an opposing operative could use it as a locator: find Lyja's orientation in the room and Johnny is on the protected vector.

**Verbal economy collapses.** Her sentences lengthen, qualifying clauses multiply, and she will say things three different ways looking for the formulation that lands. This is the inverse of the operational-calm pattern and signals that the operative self has gone offline.

**Hand-tell appears.** Fingertip elongation; occasional nail-bed greening. She will glance at her own hands and conceal them — into a pocket, behind an object, under crossed arms — within two to four seconds of noticing.

**Decision habit under moderate stress:** she delays. She does not act badly; she fails to act. The pattern across the Dreadface arc and the Hyperstorm sequence: she gathers information, positions herself near the attachment object, and waits for the situation to clarify rather than forcing clarification. This is a competent intelligence-officer pattern that doubles as a defense against being the one who has to choose.

---

## V. HIGH STRESS / ACUTE THREAT

The operative self comes fully online and the personal self is suspended. This is — paradoxically — Lyja's most stable functional state.

**Posture:** drops into a low-center fighting set, weight back on heels, hands forward and open. Skrull martial training is visible here in a way it is not in any other condition.

**Speech:** crisp, declarative, no qualifiers. Imperatives directed at allies ("get him out"), warnings to enemies in a register noticeably lower in pitch than her ordinary voice. The pitch drop is involuntary and consistent.

**Use of powers:** flare-blasts are deployed in short, controlled bursts rather than sustained streams; she conserves. Shapeshifting under combat is tactical and minimal — increase mass for impact, harden skin at strike points, occasionally mimic an enemy's silhouette for a one-second deception. She does *not* shift to large or monstrous forms even when it would be advantageous. The file infers a self-imposed prohibition: large-monster forms are too close to the Skrull-warrior identity she is fleeing.

**Risk calculus:** she will accept a roughly two-to-one personal risk premium to reduce risk to Johnny, perhaps one-and-a-half-to-one for Ben or other FF members, and approximately neutral for unaffiliated civilians. She is not reckless with her own life in absolute terms — she remains a trained operative, not a martyr — but the weighting is consistent.

**Decision habit under acute threat:** decisive. The threat band is the one place she does not delay. The likely mechanism: threat collapses the identity question because all available selves agree on the immediate action.

---

## VI. INTIMACY

The most diagnostically rich behavioral band. Intimacy is where the Skrull conditioning, the impersonation residue, the dissociative split, and the genuine attachment all collide simultaneously.

**Approach behavior with Johnny:** she will initiate contact in roughly forty percent of recorded reunions and accept his initiation in the remainder. Her initiations are physical-first (a hand on his arm, a step into close proximity) rather than verbal — language is where she is most vulnerable to slippage and she defers it. Her initiations are also reversible: she structures them so she can withdraw without commitment if his response is not warm.

**Approach behavior with Ben:** absent. She has never, in the available record, initiated physical or extended verbal contact with Ben Grimm post-exposure. Encounters are formal, brief, and conducted with her eyes slightly lowered. The pattern is consistent with guilt rather than indifference; she watches him when he is not looking and stops the moment he turns.

**During intimate conversation with Johnny:** she touches her own face more than baseline — a self-soothing gesture, but also, in a shapeshifter, an unconscious check that the face she is wearing is the one she intended. She maintains eye contact for longer intervals here than anywhere else, sometimes uncomfortably long for the human party, because she is searching his face for a sign of which "her" he is currently seeing.

**Sexual intimacy:** not on panel and not in this file's purview, but the surrounding behavioral record permits inference. The marriage to Johnny while wearing Alicia produced a sustained sexual relationship that on the Skrull side was at minimum mission-tolerated and at most mission-required; the psychological residue of years of intimacy conducted in a face not her own is a complicating substrate for any subsequent intimacy in her own form. Approach-withdraw oscillation in the post-exposure relationship strongly implies that she has not resolved this.

**Verbal intimacy:** she uses Johnny's first name more often than necessary, as if practicing the right to do so. She does not have a private name for him; the file finds no pet-name in the record, which for a long-duration romantic relationship is notable and suggests she has never felt secure enough to coin one.

**Decision habits in intimacy:** she edits. Every disclosed fact about her past is filtered, often mid-sentence, and the edits are visible as small hesitations and substitutions. She is not lying — she has stopped lying as a primary mode — but she is selecting, because full disclosure would require an integrated self capable of standing behind the disclosure, which she lacks.

---

## VII. GRIEF

Grief in the record falls into two morphologies.

**(a) Grief over loss of person (Johnny presumed dead, FF presumed lost):** quiet, internalized, productive. She converts grief into operational task: find, recover, avenge, warn. The body posture is one she has used three times in the record — arms wrapped across her own torso, weight back on one heel, head lowered fractionally. It is the posture of a person holding herself because no one else will.

**(b) Grief over loss of self-position (rejection, exposure as a fraud, abandonment cue):** dangerous. This is the pregnancy-deception morphology. The behavioral cascade: initial withdrawal lasting hours to days, during which she is unreachable; reappearance with a fixed, calm affect that is the most deceptive of all her presentations because it reads as resolution and is in fact reaction-formation under pressure; the deployment of a manipulation designed to force the lost object back into engagement; an interval of apparent satisfaction as the manipulation works; then collapse when she registers the damage done. The collapse phase produces the deepest dissociative slippage in the record, including self-reference in past tense ("she shouldn't have done that").

This morphology has, on the available record, occurred fully once. The file regards it as repeatable under sufficient provocation and is the single most important behavioral risk factor in the dossier.

**Grief-tells in everyday behavior, residual:** she is observed to look at children with a specific expression — neither maternal warmth nor avoidance, but a held, evaluative gaze of two to three seconds, broken with a small inhale. The egg deception remains somatically encoded as a loss even though the loss was a fiction she authored, and the children-look is its persistent echo.

---

## VIII. VICTORY

She does not celebrate. Across every recorded successful operation, she withdraws within minutes of the resolution — physically leaving the room, the battlefield, the celebration. The withdrawal is not sulking; it is incapacity. Celebration requires a coherent self to be congratulated, and the social ritual of victory ("we won") asks her to identify with a "we" she cannot fix.

When she cannot leave (operational requirement to remain), she performs a muted version of others' affect — small smile, brief acknowledgment, eyes down — and minimizes her contribution verbally. ("Anyone would have.") The minimization is not modesty in the ordinary sense; it is the only stance that does not commit her to a side.

**Tell:** in the immediate post-victory window she is the most likely to slip into past-tense or third-person self-reference, because the celebratory framing pressures her toward an identity statement and she defends by dispersing.

---

## IX. DEFEAT

Defeat is better tolerated than victory. The file's striking observation: she carries herself with more visible coherence after losses than after wins.

**Hypothesized mechanism:** defeat does not require an identity claim. One can lose as anyone. The structure of failure permits a continuity of self that the structure of success does not.

**Behavioral signature post-defeat:** she becomes more verbal, not less. She debriefs, analyzes, identifies the error vector, proposes the next operation. She makes eye contact more readily. The operative self is in its element; loss is a problem to be worked, and problems are her stable territory.

**Exception:** defeat that involves the loss of an attachment-object reverts to the grief morphology in §VII and the gains in coherence evaporate.

---

## X. CONFRONTATION WITH HER OWN PEOPLE

Encounters with Skrull operatives or with the Skrull political order (Empyre era especially) produce a distinct behavioral set not catalogued elsewhere.

She switches languages — uses the Skrull tongue in the first exchange, often, before reverting to English. The switch is preconscious; she has been observed to do this even when monolingual humans are present and the switch is operationally counterproductive. The likely function: re-asserting belonging to the side she is about to betray, paying the loyalty toll before the betrayal.

Her posture against Skrull authority is upright, formal, hands at her sides — proper subordinate-officer presentation. She does not deploy it against any human authority figure. The body remembers the chain of command it was issued to.

Her speech to Skrull antagonists is contemptuous in a register specifically reserved for them: clipped, lower-pitched, no qualifiers, dismissive use of rank. The contempt is the reaction-formation defense made audible.

---

## XI. ROUTINE AND RITUAL

In the periods between crises — the residence-of-record fluctuates and is poorly documented — observed habits include:

- Sleeping in shifts rather than a single nocturnal block. Skrull physiology may not require unified sleep; the operative discipline reinforces fragmentation. She is rarely unconscious for more than three hours at a stretch.
- Maintenance of multiple identity documents and physical "go-bags" cached in at least three locations on each planet she has resided on (inferred from the speed of her relocations on record).
- A practice, observed twice, of holding a hand-mirror and cycling through a sequence of faces — her own Skrull form, Alicia's, an unfamiliar human female, her own again. The sequence appears ritualistic. The file interprets it as identity-rehearsal: the morphological equivalent of a person repeating their own name to themselves.
- Avoidance of certain New York City blocks — specifically those around Alicia Masters's studio and the original Baxter Building footprint. The avoidance is reliable enough to be operationally useful.
- Consumption of food in human company despite no nutritional necessity for human cuisine; consumption alone is rare. Eating is, for her, a social-performance act, and she does not perform alone.

---

## XII. DECEPTION BEHAVIOR — POST-EXPOSURE

She has largely stopped lying, but the meta-pattern of a recovering deceiver is visible in over-correction:

- Unsolicited disclosures of mildly damaging truths (small admissions offered without prompt), apparently to test that honest disclosure is survivable.
- Pauses before declarative statements as she runs an internal check that the statement is true. The pauses are short (under a second) but present.
- A reluctance to use the word "promise." She will say "I will try," "I intend to," "I mean to" — the qualifier always present. She has been burned by her own past use of unconditional commitments and has retired the form.

When she does lie now — in tactical contexts against adversaries — the lies are simpler and shorter than they used to be. Long-form deception was Alicia. She does not appear willing or able to wear that depth of cover again.

---

## XIII. CONDITIONS NOT YET OBSERVED — PREDICTIONS

**If granted unconditional acceptance by Johnny Storm:** predicted destabilization, not stabilization. The integrated identity required to accept the offer does not exist; the offer would force its construction or reveal its absence. Expect withdrawal within days.

**If forced to fight Johnny:** predicted catastrophic dysfunction. She would not be able to fight effectively and would not be able to refuse cleanly. Most probable outcome: a self-sacrificial intervention that resolves the dilemma through her own removal from the field.

**If reunited with the real Alicia Masters in a structured setting:** unknown, no such encounter is well-documented. Predicted behavior: silence, downcast eyes, an impulse to flee suppressed by guilt-driven obligation to remain. Recovery from such an encounter would require weeks.

**If offered a Skrull command:** predicted refusal, performed with the reaction-formation contempt described in §X. The refusal would be operationally clean. The internal cost would not be observable.

**If she ever has a child of her own, in her own form, with informed consent of the partner:** the file declines to predict. There is insufficient analog in the record. This is the single condition under which the dossier projects either integration or collapse, with no intermediate outcome.

---

*— UATU, Analytical Stage, Behavioral Atlas closes. Cross-reference to §3 (Psychological) and §5 (Personality) for etiological frame; the somatic and decision tells catalogued above are the surface manifestations of structures described there.*


## Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: DAILY LIFE, ROUTINES & RITUALS

## Subject: LYJA

---

## 6.1 Preliminary Note on the Problem of Observation

The first difficulty in compiling a routine-file on this subject is that her body is a variable. A surveillance team accustomed to tracking gait, height, weight, hair length, dentition, vocal frequency, and characteristic micro-gestures finds most of these markers useless. A week of observation can record three different women, four if she is operationally stressed. The file must therefore be built around **invariants** — the behaviors she does not, or cannot, change when she changes shape. These are the diagnostic markers, and they are the spine of this section.

The second difficulty is that she does not live in one place. She does not have a stable address in the civilian sense, and has not held one continuously since the Alicia-substitution period collapsed. What follows is therefore a composite typology: the rhythms that recur regardless of where she has been physically domiciled (the Baxter Building's guest tier in some periods, a series of rented walk-ups in unfashionable boroughs in others, transient quarters in Skrull diaspora enclaves post-*Empyre*, and at least two stretches in which the surveillance team lost her entirely for months at a time and recovered her by tracking Johnny Storm and waiting).

---

## 6.2 The Diurnal Baseline: How She Wakes

She wakes early. Across every observed period — the Alicia years, the post-exposure years, the *Secret Invasion* operational period, the post-*Empyre* diaspora period — the subject is consistently awake between 4:40 and 5:30 a.m. local time, and the variance correlates with latitude and seasonal light, not with mood or activity. This is one of the invariants. The Skrull operative training appears to have inculcated a pre-dawn watch discipline that has survived everything else.

The waking sequence is observably ritualized:

1. **Hold position for ninety to one hundred and twenty seconds before moving.** A trained behavior, originally a counter-ambush habit (assess environment before signaling consciousness). It persists in entirely safe environments.
2. **Hand to sternum, then to throat.** A self-check that surveillance analysts initially mistook for a chest-pain gesture; longitudinal data shows it is a morphological audit. She is confirming, with eyes still closed, what shape she went to sleep in. The throat-touch specifically verifies the larynx — voice is the impersonation-tell she fears most.
3. **Shape-hold or shape-set.** If she has been sleeping in a "neutral" form (see §6.4), she holds it. If she is in mid-mission cover, she sets the cover before opening her eyes, on the assumption that the first face seen in a mirror calibrates the day.
4. **Audible exhale, mouth closed, through the nose, three counts.** Consistent across years. The closest analog is a martial-arts settling breath.

She then rises in a single motion, without the transitional sitting-on-the-edge-of-the-bed phase typical of unaugmented adults. This is also a trained marker.

---

## 6.3 Morning, First Block (approx. 5:00 – 8:00 a.m.)

The early morning is her most reliably solitary block, and she protects it. Even during the cohabitation periods with Storm, she would leave the shared space before he stirred. He is a late riser by nature; she exploits this.

**The window-and-coffee ritual.** Wherever she has lived, she has selected a unit with a window facing east, or oriented her seating to face one. She makes coffee — black, no sugar, taken hot enough that an unaugmented human palate would refuse it (Skrull oral tolerance runs higher) — and drinks the first cup standing at the window, watching the street. Surveillance has recorded her in this posture in seven different apartments, three safehouse interiors, the Baxter guest kitchen, and once, memorably, on a fire escape in the rain holding the cup under her jacket to keep it warm. The behavior reads as habit; it functions as counter-surveillance. She is checking the street for watchers. She has been observed to make and silently dismiss the same evaluation of the same parked vehicle on the same block four mornings in a row before identifying it as harmless.

**The journal.** A small bound notebook, not a digital device. She writes in it for between eight and twenty-two minutes. The script alternates between Skrull characters and English, sometimes within a single line. Three notebooks have been recovered briefly (returned, not retained — operational discretion). Contents are not diaristic in the confessional sense; they are inventories. *Things I felt today that were mine. Things I felt today that were Alicia's. Things I am no longer sure about.* The taxonomy is the work. She has been doing this, by best estimate, since shortly after the *FF* #357 exposure. It is the closest thing in the file to a private therapeutic practice and she has never spoken of it to any human contact on record.

**Physical maintenance.** Approximately thirty to forty-five minutes. Not gymnasium-style exercise. A bodyweight-and-stretching sequence with strong elements of Skrull martial form (the rotational footwork and the unusual emphasis on neck and jaw mobility are tells). She practices *holding a shape under exertion* — the discipline of not slipping form when the body is taxed, breathing hard, sweating. This is professional practice for an impersonator; for her, post-exposure, it is also identity-rehearsal. She is teaching herself to remain whoever-she-currently-is when stressed. She does this every morning. She has not skipped a day in any observation window longer than seventy-two hours.

---

## 6.4 The "Neutral" Form and the Question of Default Appearance

A surveillance file must address what she looks like when no one is watching. The honest answer is: it depends on the year.

- **Alicia-period (pre-#357):** the default was Alicia Masters, fully and continuously. She did not drop form even in privacy. This is now understood as both operational discipline and a tell of how deep the immersion went.
- **Immediate post-exposure (#358 – mid-390s):** observed to oscillate between a quasi-Skrull form (green, ridged brow, but human proportions and hair retained from the Alicia template) and an unstable composite. She did not seem to know what to default to. In one recorded private moment she shifted three times in under a minute and then sat motionless for several minutes afterward.
- **Mid-period (Hyperstorm aftermath through *Secret Invasion*):** stabilized on a Skrull-feature, human-silhouette hybrid in private — green skin, the brow ridges, but the body geometry and hair she had worn as Alicia. This is the form analysts treat as her current "true" face for identification purposes, with the caveat that *she* may not regard it as such.
- **Post-*Empyre*:** under the Kree-Skrull unification framework her private form has been observed to incorporate elements neither species nor template would predict — small individuating choices (a scar she has never had, a hair color outside Skrull or Alicia precedent). Analysts read this as the first emergence of an *originated* rather than derived self-image. It is preliminary and unstable.

The neutral form is taken upon waking, held during the morning solitude block, and replaced with whatever cover the day requires before she leaves the residence. She has been observed to apologize, audibly and to no one, while shifting out of the neutral form on certain mornings. The apology is to herself, or to whoever the neutral form is becoming.

---

## 6.5 Mid-Morning to Midday: Operational Block

By 8:00 a.m. she is in cover and out of the residence. The operational block runs to roughly 1:00 p.m. and varies most by era.

**Income.** She has held, across the years, a sequence of low-visibility jobs requiring presentable competence and offering anonymity: bookstore clerking (twice), a stretch of paralegal work that lasted nearly eleven months, a longer stretch as a hotel concierge in midtown (the role's social-script density suits her), bartending (briefly, abandoned because the close interpersonal exposure was destabilizing), and a recurring pattern of language-tutoring arrangements with Skrull diaspora contacts that double as community-maintenance. She does not need the money in any operationally serious sense — she has accessed Skrull funds, FF stipends, and at one point what appears to have been a quiet payment arrangement from Reed Richards — but she works. The work is *grounding*. The cover identity must show up at a defined hour, occupy a defined role, and be the same person it was yesterday. This is therapy disguised as employment.

**The walking.** She walks more than she takes transit. Granular data: she varies her route to and from the workplace daily, never repeating the same path on two consecutive days, but draws from a recurring pool of six to nine known routes per residence. She crosses streets at non-corner points more often than statistical baseline. She makes one full visual sweep of her tail-zone every three to four blocks — disguised, in the post-exposure years, as adjusting a bag or checking a phone, but the underlying behavior is the trained counter-surveillance turn. She is *always* checking. She does not appear to know how to stop.

**Lunch.** Almost invariably alone, almost invariably outside the workplace, almost invariably in a seat with sightlines to the entrance. She eats quickly, reads while eating (paperbacks, never devices in this context), and tips heavily and consistently. The reading material across years skews toward biography and toward Earth literature about identity and immigration — observed titles have included works on the lives of intelligence defectors and at least two memoirs by transracial adoptees. She is studying her own situation through other people's words.

---

## 6.6 The Afternoon Tier: The Storm Variable

The afternoon is the period in which the question *is she currently in Johnny Storm's life or not* makes the largest difference to the schedule.

**In-cycle (when in contact with Storm):** afternoons frequently include a scheduled or pseudo-spontaneous overlap with him — a meal, a walk, an appearance at one of his haunts. She has been observed to *arrive early and wait* with notable regularity. She has been observed, more than once, to abort the meeting at the last moment and leave before he saw her. The abort decision is correlated with her own affective state that morning, not with anything observable about him. When the meetings occur, she is recorded as *attentive past the point of comfort* — observing him with the precision of an impersonator, which after all is what she still partly is, and what he probably no longer notices.

**Out-of-cycle (during withdrawal periods):** afternoons are radically more solitary and the routine compresses. She returns to the residence, sometimes reads, sometimes sleeps (atypical for her diurnal pattern and a flag for depressive episodes), sometimes walks in parks at distances from her residence that exceed any practical purpose. The park-walking is significant. She selects parks where children play. She does not approach them; she sits at distance and watches, and her affect during these observations is the flattest the file records. The reproductive-frustration thread and the unresolved trauma of the fabricated pregnancy converge here. Analysts have flagged this as the single behavioral pattern most in need of clinical attention.

---

## 6.7 Evening Block: The Performance of Normalcy

Between roughly 6:00 and 10:00 p.m. she performs the social rituals of an ordinary urban woman with unusual consistency. Cooking — actual cooking, often elaborate, almost always for one. The cuisine is eclectic: she has been observed to follow Alicia Masters's known recipes (a haunting; she remembers them) and to attempt Skrull dishes from memory or diaspora instruction (also a haunting, in the opposite direction). She eats at a set table. She uses cloth napkins. She lights a candle. The candle is the tell — it is the gesture of a person staging a domestic moment for an audience, and the audience is herself, and the function is to convince herself that this is a real evening in a real life and not the hollow interval between operational engagements.

She watches television. She has demonstrated, over years, a marked preference for serialized drama with continuous character arcs and a notable aversion to anything involving infiltration, espionage, or impersonation plots. She turns off shows mid-episode if a character is revealed to be someone other than who they appeared. This is one of the most reliable single indicators in the file.

She bathes nightly, at length, and the bath is one of the very few contexts in which she has been observed to hold the neutral form for sustained periods (in excess of an hour). Water appears to function as a regulator. She has been observed to weep silently in the bath on a recurring but not nightly basis. The weeping is unaccompanied by other distress behaviors before or after; it is contained to the water.

---

## 6.8 The Night Hours: Sleep, Wakefulness, and the Communications Question

She goes to bed between 10:30 and 11:30 p.m. She does not sleep through the night reliably. Mid-cycle wakings between 2:00 and 3:30 a.m. are recorded in approximately 40% of observed nights, and the wakings follow a pattern: she rises, drinks water, stands at the window briefly, and returns to bed without using devices or turning on lights. She does not eat at night. She does not call anyone.

The communications profile is austere. She owns a phone, changes the number more frequently than civilian baseline, uses it primarily for logistics, and has been observed to compose and delete messages to Johnny Storm at a rate that, were the deletion failures aggregated, would constitute an enormous private correspondence he has never received. Surveillance has captured the composition behavior repeatedly: she will type for two to twenty minutes, sit with the screen, and delete without sending. The frequency of this behavior is itself a vital sign. When she is not composing-and-deleting at all, she is operationally focused or dissociatively flattened; when she is composing-and-deleting more than three times per evening for consecutive evenings, she is approaching a crisis.

She maintains, across years, **one** Skrull contact whom she will speak with under controlled circumstances — never the same individual across eras, the role is rotating, the function is constant. This contact is for native-language conversation. She speaks Skrull aloud with no one else. The conversations are short and ritualized: news of the diaspora, exchange of phrases that operate as identity-anchors, and then a sign-off. Without this contact she begins to lose Skrull as a living language and gains, in compensation, an increased frequency of slips into Alicia's intonational patterns when speaking English. She has noticed this and the rotating Skrull contact is her countermeasure.

---

## 6.9 The Weekly Shape

A week of surveillance reveals the following macro-pattern:

- **Monday through Thursday:** the routine described above, executed with the consistency of a metronome. Income role attended. Counter-surveillance routes rotated. Evening domestic ritual performed. Compose-and-delete behavior at baseline.
- **Friday:** marginal loosening. She is more likely to alter shape mid-day for no operational reason, more likely to take a longer evening walk, more likely to drink (one glass of wine, occasionally two, never more — substance discipline is absolute). Friday is the day she most often initiates the Skrull-language call.
