The granularity is deliberate: a total-surveillance file lives or dies by the micro-pattern.

---

## A. WAKING, SOLITUDE, AND THE PRIVATE BODY

**GIVEN** Lyja waking alone in a safehouse or apartment, unobserved →
**EXPECT** a measurable lag (estimated 8–40 seconds) before she settles into a morphological default. The Skrull baseline is rarely the first form chosen; nor is the late-era "Lyja with red hair and humanoid features" she presents to Johnny. Field observation would likely show involuntary partial-Alicia features (the cheekbone structure, the set of the mouth) as the first unconscious configuration before conscious override. **Mechanism:** identification-with-the-role as primary defense; the body reaches for the longest-practiced shape before the mind reasserts the chosen identity. **Confidence: H.** **Tell:** mirror avoidance for the first several minutes after waking.

**GIVEN** Lyja showering or bathing →
**EXPECT** she will not look down at her own body. She will reach for soap, washcloth, towel by haptic memory rather than visual confirmation. **Mechanism:** the body is the site of the identity-question; sustained visual self-inspection without a designated form to inhabit is destabilizing. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** Lyja injured in private (a cut, a burn from cooking) →
**EXPECT** her first instinct is to heal it morphologically; her second, immediately overriding the first, is to leave it and let it heal as a human injury would. The override is recent — a discipline learned during the Storm marriage and retained afterward as a kind of vow. **Mechanism:** atonement-by-vulnerability; sub-conscious refusal to enjoy the body's advantages. **Confidence: M.**

**GIVEN** Lyja sleeping →
**EXPECT** morphological drift in REM. Surveillance would catch the face cycling between three or four configurations across a night — Skrull baseline, Alicia, the "Lyja" presentation, and occasionally faces of persons unidentifiable from canon (early Skrull intimates, trainers, possibly Paibok). She does not know this happens. **Confidence: M.** **Tell:** she refuses to share a bed with anyone for longer than a few hours; will rise before her partner wakes.

**GIVEN** an empty day with no operational demand →
**EXPECT** rapid affective deterioration within 48–72 hours. Unstructured time is the enemy: the role-performance self has nothing to do, and the substrate self has no content. She will manufacture small tasks (cleaning, reorganization, language drill) to avoid the void. **Confidence: H.**

---

## B. EATING, DRINKING, CONSUMPTION

**GIVEN** Lyja ordering food in a human restaurant →
**EXPECT** she orders what Alicia would have ordered. She has never reconstructed her own taste preferences from scratch; the palate she practiced during the cover assignment is the only human palate she has. Skrull cuisine she finds, by now, mildly disgusting — another data point against the supposed cultural homeland. **Confidence: H.** **Tell:** when ordering for herself she pauses fractionally and then orders with unusual specificity, as if remembering rather than choosing.

**GIVEN** Lyja drinking alcohol →
**EXPECT** restrained consumption with one specific failure mode: she becomes more, not less, controlled with alcohol up to a threshold, then collapses suddenly past it. Skrull metabolism handles ethanol differently than human; she has had to learn her tolerance by trial, and the learning is unfinished. **Confidence: M.** **Tell:** she will nurse one drink across an evening; if she accepts a second she is signaling intent to lower her guard, which is operationally significant.

**GIVEN** offered a food associated with the Storm/Richards household specifically (Aunt Petunia's recipes; the cafeteria fare of the Baxter Building; Sue's coffee) →
**EXPECT** a micro-flinch followed by acceptance. She cannot refuse without explanation; the consumption is small grief. **Confidence: M.**

---

## C. DRESS, GROOMING, MORPHOLOGY-AS-WARDROBE

**GIVEN** Lyja preparing for a public appearance (mission, party, errand) →
**EXPECT** a longer preparation interval than the wardrobe alone would justify — because the wardrobe *is* the body. She is choosing not only clothing but height, build, the precise calibration of "human" she will perform. A baseline run-through of options, then a commit. **Confidence: H.** **Tell:** clothing in her possession is sized for several body-configurations; she keeps the wardrobe sorted by which "self" wears it.

**GIVEN** asked her natural hair color →
**EXPECT** a half-beat hesitation, then a chosen rather than remembered answer. The Skrull baseline does not really have "hair" in the sense the question implies. She has trained herself to respond "red" because that is the form she most consistently presents to Johnny, and the consistency is its own truth-claim. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** Lyja shopping for clothing in a human retail context →
**EXPECT** she gravitates to neutrals, textures that read as soft (cashmere, brushed cotton), and silhouettes that do not draw the eye. Operational discretion fuses with personal taste: she does not want to be looked at by strangers. Exception: clothing she is buying *for* a date with Johnny will run brighter, more deliberate, slightly out of period with her usual taste — selected to recall things he once said he liked. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** observation of her hands when she is unguarded →
**EXPECT** the nails are kept short and unpainted. Alicia worked with clay. The vestige persists even in periods when she has not seen Ben Grimm for years. **Confidence: M.**

---

## D. LANGUAGE, SPEECH, AND VOICE

**GIVEN** prolonged English conversation →
**EXPECT** flawless idiom but a faint over-correctness in syntax; she uses the full form where a native speaker would contract, occasionally. The error rate increases when she is tired and decreases when she is performing a specific cover. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** she is startled or in pain →
**EXPECT** the first vocalization is not in English. It is not necessarily in Skrull either; it is often a wordless intake of breath calibrated to the body she is wearing. If a word emerges, it is Skrull, low and short. She is embarrassed by this and will cover with English immediately. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** she references her past →
**EXPECT** the pronoun pattern is diagnostic. "Alicia" is "she," never "I," even when she is recounting an event Lyja-as-Alicia personally experienced. "The mission" or "my orders" are used for the Skrull-loyalist period. Only the post-exposure decades are narrated in the first person. **Confidence: H.** **Tell:** any first-person reference to the Alicia period is a signal of acute destabilization or of trust extended to the listener at a level she rarely grants.

**GIVEN** asked to tell a story about herself unrelated to Johnny, Ben, or Skrull operations →
**EXPECT** difficulty. She does not have many. The biographical inventory is thin in the middle. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** small talk with strangers (cashier, neighbor, taxi) →
**EXPECT** unusual competence — she is, after all, a trained impersonator — but a tendency to mirror the interlocutor's regional accent and vocal pitch. Surveillance across a single afternoon would catch her speaking with three different cadences. **Confidence: H.**

---

## E. PHYSICAL CARRIAGE, GAIT, TICS

**GIVEN** walking in public →
**EXPECT** she walks at a speed and stride length that does not match the body she is wearing — a Skrull operative's pace adapted by approximation. Trained observers (street-level intelligence) would notice over distance. **Confidence: M.**

**GIVEN** a moment of cognitive load (problem-solving, recall) →
**EXPECT** a specific tic: she touches the tip of her left thumb to the pad of her left ring finger, twice, then once. The origin is unrecoverable from canon but is consistent with a Skrull-training somatic anchor — a self-touch grounding gesture taught to deep-cover operatives to reaffirm body-ownership under role-stress. **Confidence: M.** **Tell:** appears under interrogation; appears when she is asked to make a decision about her own life rather than someone else's.

**GIVEN** she is lying to protect someone she loves →
**EXPECT** zero physiological tells. She has lied for years; the body is calibrated.
**GIVEN** she is lying to protect herself →
**EXPECT** the tells emerge: a slight delay in eye contact, a thinning of the lower lip, the morphological substrate softening the cheekbones imperceptibly toward Alicia. The internal censor cannot bring itself to perform self-protection with the same conviction as protection-of-other. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** she is touched unexpectedly →
**EXPECT** flinch and partial morphological withdrawal — a fractional density-shift under the contact point — followed by social recovery. **Confidence: H.** **Tell:** she will not stand with her back to an open door or window; this is operational and predates the FF entirely.

**GIVEN** seated in a meeting, briefing, or social gathering →
**EXPECT** she chooses the chair with the clearest sightline to exits and the greatest peripheral coverage. If forced into a worse seat she compensates by minimal posture-shifts that track activity behind her using auditory cues — and her head will not move. The training is good. **Confidence: H.**

---

## F. THE STORM AXIS — PROXIMITY, CONTACT, AND THE GHOST OF MARRIAGE

**GIVEN** Johnny enters a room she is in →
**EXPECT** a measurable thermal/postural response: respiration deepens slightly, shoulders drop by a centimeter, the morphological substrate softens toward the configuration he is used to. She does not realize she is doing any of this. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** Johnny enters a room with a woman he is dating →
**EXPECT** flawless social grace, slightly excessive warmth toward the new partner, and an internally noted exit-time calculated within the first 90 seconds. She will not stay longer than politeness requires; she will not leave conspicuously early. **Confidence: H.** **Tell:** she will compliment the new partner specifically and accurately — the spycraft self does not permit petty inaccuracy — and the compliment will land harder than intended.

**GIVEN** Johnny asks her for help on a non-FF matter (a favor, a personal errand) →
**EXPECT** instant assent without negotiation of terms, followed by competent execution disproportionate to the ask. **Confidence: H.** This is the most exploitable behavioral feature in the file.

**GIVEN** Johnny in danger but not mortal danger →
**EXPECT** appropriate, calibrated response.
**GIVEN** Johnny in plausible mortal danger →
**EXPECT** disregard for her own survival baseline, immediate self-deployment, willingness to expend the augmented flare-blast capability in ways that risk her own substrate. The martyrdom-attempt described in §5 is not metaphorical; it is an available behavior. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** Johnny initiates physical contact (a touch on the arm, a hug in greeting) →
**EXPECT** she holds longer by a fraction of a second than the social contract permits, then breaks first — to preempt the embarrassment of being released. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** the phrase "my wife" used by Johnny in any context, even ironically →
**EXPECT** sustained micro-disturbance for the remainder of the interaction; she will perform normalcy and will not bring it up. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** the marriage's legal status is raised (was it valid; was annulment ever filed; does any human jurisdiction recognize it) →
**EXPECT** avoidance and topic-change. She has not researched this. She does not want to know. The ambiguity is preferable to either answer. **Confidence: H.**

---

## G. THE GRIMM AXIS — AVOIDANCE AND THE RESIDUAL DEBT

**GIVEN** Ben Grimm appears unexpectedly →
**EXPECT** freeze, then over-formal greeting, then exit at the earliest non-rude opportunity. She has never resolved Ben. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** the real Alicia Masters is present →
**EXPECT** Lyja will not be. She has avoided Alicia for years through the simple expedient of never being in the same building. If forced into the same room, expect minimal speech, sustained eye contact (she will not look away — the spy will not show weakness), and a Skrull-baseline form rather than any humanoid presentation. She will not perform a human shape in front of the woman she replaced. **Confidence: H.** This is the single most precise piece of ethical clarity she retains.

**GIVEN** mention of clay, sculpture, or any of Alicia's specific artistic practices →
**EXPECT** the hands respond before the face. She will look at her own hands; she will put them somewhere out of view. **Confidence: M.**

**GIVEN** mention of Ben's mother, Aunt Petunia, or any Grimm-family figure she met while wearing Alicia's face →
**EXPECT** a long blink and a deflection. These are the deceived; the guilt is graded by intimacy of the deception. **Confidence: M-H.**

---

## H. THE SKRULL AXIS — PEERS, OFFICIALS, EXILES

**GIVEN** contact with a Skrull she does not know personally →
**EXPECT** correct protocol observed, no warmth offered, hands kept where flare-blast deployment is unobstructed. Trust extended at zero. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** a Skrull invokes Empire, Throne, or Hierarchy rhetoric at her →
**EXPECT** a flat, neutral response and immediate operational distrust of that individual. The ideological frame is dead in her; she expects its invocation to be either delusion or manipulation. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** the post-*Empyre* unified Skrull-Kree polity makes any claim on her loyalty or service →
**EXPECT** polite, indefinite deferral. She will not refuse openly (operational discipline) and will not comply (personal disposition). She will simply be unavailable. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** a Skrull refugee or defector approaches her for help →
**EXPECT** unexpected generosity, sustained risk-acceptance, and material aid. This is the population she over-identifies with and the one she will reliably show up for. **Confidence: H.** A handler running her as an asset should expect she will divert resources to this category without asking.

**GIVEN** Paibok's name spoken →
**EXPECT** no visible response. The lack of response is itself the response; she has trained around it. Sustained physiological monitoring would show pulse elevation. **Confidence: M-H.**

---

## I. THE FOUR — PERIPHERAL FF FIGURES

**GIVEN** Reed Richards engages her in conversation →
**EXPECT** deference, brevity, and a tendency to give him information he did not ask for. He frightens her — not personally but categorically. He is the analytic intelligence she was originally deployed to defeat, and she now wants his approval. The combination is awkward. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** Sue Storm engages her in conversation →
**EXPECT** complicated warmth. Sue is the woman whose family she infiltrated, married into, and harmed by deception. Sue's apparent forgiveness, where given, is received with disbelief that does not visibly register. **Confidence: H.** Lyja will defer to Sue on family matters reflexively.

**GIVEN** the Richards children (Franklin, Valeria) in her presence →
**EXPECT** competent affection, careful not to overstep. She held Franklin as an infant while wearing another woman's face. She has not metabolized this. With Valeria — born after the exposure — the dynamic is cleaner and the warmth is more spontaneous. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** a Foundation- or FF-extended-family event (gathering, wedding, funeral) →
**EXPECT** RSVP yes, arrive on time, position herself peripherally, leave at the median departure time of attendees — never first, never last. She has studied this. **Confidence: H.**

---

## J. STRANGERS, CIVILIANS, AND THE PUBLIC ROLE

**GIVEN** a civilian in distress (street-level — accident, harassment, lost child) →
**EXPECT** intervention. The intervention will be competent, minimally costumed (she does not deploy as a public hero), and she will leave before names are exchanged. The protective reflex is genuine; the anonymity is operational and personal. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** unwanted attention from a stranger (flirtation, harassment) →
**EXPECT** de-escalation by social skill first, morphological discouragement second (a fractional shift in apparent build or affect that reads as "uninteresting"), and physical response only if cornered. She will not enjoy any of it. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** a journalist or biographer approaches her →
**EXPECT** refusal, restated politely if pressed, and operational tracking of the journalist for the next several weeks to determine threat level. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** she is recognized in public as "Johnny Storm's ex-wife" by a fan or paparazzo →
**EXPECT** correction-without-correction: a smile, a vague demurral, escape. She will not affirm and will not deny. The ambiguity protects something. **Confidence: H.**

---

## K. ROUTINES, ROUTES, HABITS

**GIVEN** any extended residence (weeks-plus) →
**EXPECT** three rehearsed exit routes from each habitual location, at least one cached identity-kit (clothing for an alternate human configuration, basic ID, currency) within 20 minutes' travel of her primary base, and a no-contact rendezvous protocol established with herself for re-emergence after operational disappearance. **Confidence: H.** Spycraft is the load-bearing wall of the personality; she will not abandon it because she has nothing to put in its place.

**GIVEN** travel between cities →
**EXPECT** she prefers ground transport to air; if flying, she does not use her own identity. If she must use her own identity she pays in cash where possible. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** scheduled medical or dental appointments (in any cover identity) →
**EXPECT** non-attendance. Bodies that can be anything do not need dentists. She will keep the appointments only for cover integrity, and she will reschedule away from them whenever plausible. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** routine domestic tasks (laundry, dishes, bedmaking) →
**EXPECT** disproportionate care and order. The household is the one environment she can authoritatively shape; the gratification is real. The bed will be made within minutes of rising; the kitchen will not have dishes in the sink overnight. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** a pet considered →
**EXPECT** she will not keep one. The asymmetry of attachment in which she would be the stable home is not a role she trusts herself to inhabit. **Confidence: M.**

**GIVEN** plants →
**EXPECT** several, kept alive with discipline. The arrangement will recall Alicia's apartment in subtle ways she would deny if asked. **Confidence: M.**

---

## L. RECREATION, MEDIA, AND THE INNER LIFE NO ONE SEES

**GIVEN** unstructured leisure time she has actually allowed herself →
**EXPECT** consumption of human narrative media disproportionate to her age — novels, films, episodic television — particularly stories about persons living under assumed identities, witness-protection narratives, immigrant assimilation arcs, adoption-reunion stories. She studies the genre. She is looking for a template. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** music alone →
**EXPECT** instrumental over vocal, vocal in languages she does not speak over vocal in English. Lyrics in English compete with the language she has built her assumed identity in; she avoids the interference. **Confidence: M.**

**GIVEN** a journal or written record →
**EXPECT** none kept. Documentation of an integrated self requires belief in one. **Confidence: H.** If a journal *is* recovered, its existence is more significant than its contents.

**GIVEN** access to a mirror over a sustained interval →
**EXPECT** she will cycle through forms in private practice — including faces of persons whose identities she has never assumed operationally. This is not rehearsal. It is closer to a child trying on parents' clothes. **Confidence: M.**

---

## M. CRISIS MICRO-SITUATIONS

**GIVEN** a fire alarm in a public building →
**EXPECT** she evacuates with the crowd at slightly above median speed, scanning for actual threat indicators, and is the person who notices the wheelchair user no one is helping. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** witnessing a violent crime →
**EXPECT** intervention if she can intervene without revealing her abilities; surveillance and aftermath assistance if she cannot. She will not call the police herself — institutional contact is avoided categorically — but she will ensure someone does. **Confidence: M-H.**

**GIVEN** a Skrull operation she stumbles across by accident →
**EXPECT** immediate covert contact to whichever FF/Avengers element she trusts most in the current era, and personal infiltration if time pressure forbids outsourcing. **Confidence: H.**

**GIVEN** confronted by a former Skrull handler →
**EXPECT** controlled hostility, opportunity assessment for the handler's death or neutralization, and — if neither is achievable — extraction. She will not negotiate. The negotiating self died with Paibok. **Confidence: M-H.**

---

## N. THE PREDICTABLY UNPREDICTABLE

Two categories defy fine-grained prediction and must be flagged:

**1. The integration moment.** If at any point a credible relational context offers her the right to be Lyja-as-such — neither cover, nor wife, nor asset — the response is not modelable. It may be the breakthrough; it may be flight; it may be both in sequence. The variance is high because the situation is unprecedented in her history. **Confidence: L by design.**

**2. Reproductive cues recur


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — CRISIS, BETRAYAL & THE WOUND

## Classification: High-stakes behavioral forecasting. Decompensation-edge mapping. For handler use under conditions of acute stress, hostile pressure, identity-targeted attack, and wound-contact events.

---

## Prefatory Note

The predictions in §Predictive Model I governed ordinary life: the cup of coffee, the walk to the corner, the cadence of avoidance. This file governs the conditions under which the subject's ordinary surface dissolves. The operating premise: Lyja has, since *FF* #357, functioned through a brittle equilibrium between three partial selves and a fourth — the operational spy-self — which acts as their de facto regent. Crisis is the failure mode of regency. Under sufficient stress, the spy-self either tightens into pure technical performance (the controlled response) or fails entirely, allowing one of the three partial selves to seize executive function (the decompensated response). Predicting which depends on the *type* of pressure applied.

What follows is organized by the structure of the stressor, not its intensity. Two minor wound-contacts will outproduce one major physical threat.

---

## I. Combat & Tactical Crisis (Threat to Self, Not to Identity)

**GIVEN:** Sudden, unambiguous physical threat — ambush, firefight, structural collapse, an opponent of clearly hostile intent and clearly non-personal motive.
**EXPECT:** Smooth and immediate dominance by the spy-self. Affect flattens. Pupillary response steadies. Posture redistributes to a center-of-mass slightly forward of her standing baseline. She will not speak more than necessary, and what she does say will be in clipped imperatives rather than questions. The Skrull morphological repertoire deploys *conservatively* — she favors density increase and limb-elongation over wholesale impersonation, because wholesale impersonation in combat is a cognitive load she will not assume when not required. The flare-blasts are used *last*, not first; they are her augmentation, not her instinct, and she still treats them with a faint distaste — the Skrull-bioengineered modification feels imposed even after decades. Expect her to fight with her hands, her shape, and her wits before she fights with what they made her into.

**GIVEN:** The combat threat is to Johnny Storm specifically.
**EXPECT:** Spy-self holds for approximately 4–9 seconds of tactical assessment, then the protective overfunctioning module takes the wheel. She will place her body between threat and him *even when this is tactically inferior to flanking*. She will use lethal force she would not otherwise use. She will absorb damage she would otherwise evade. After the engagement, regardless of outcome, she will not look at him for several minutes; she will turn her face away and busy her hands. The aversion is not shame at having helped — it is intolerance of the question his gratitude implies. If he says her name, she will leave the room within the next ninety seconds on a plausible pretext.

**GIVEN:** The combat threat is to Ben Grimm specifically.
**EXPECT:** As above for the protective action, but with measurably increased latency (12–20 seconds of paralysis before engagement). The paralysis is the guilt-system reasserting executive control: a flicker of "I do not have the right." She will then act, and act effectively, but the cost of having acted will be a full withdrawal cycle from any social proximity to Ben for weeks. Do not attempt to facilitate a debrief between them in the immediate aftermath; she will refuse, evade, or fabricate.

**GIVEN:** She is wounded in combat to a degree requiring others to render aid.
**EXPECT:** Acute resistance to being touched by anyone in the FF circle. She will request — politely, with the surface manners of the Alicia-pattern intact — to be left alone, or to be tended by a stranger, a medic, anyone unembedded in her attachment landscape. Being cared for by Johnny or Ben in a state of physical vulnerability reactivates the marital memory at full intensity and she does not have the structural integrity to receive it. If forced (e.g. mass-casualty event, no other hands available), expect dissociative slippage in language: she will respond to Johnny in the cadences of his estranged wife and to Ben in the cadences of Alicia, and afterward will remember the episode imprecisely and refuse to discuss it.

---

## II. Capture, Interrogation, & Coercion

**GIVEN:** Captured by a hostile non-Skrull faction (Kree, AIM, criminal syndicate, hostile terrestrial state) with standard interrogation pressure — sleep deprivation, isolation, threat-of-harm.
**EXPECT:** Exemplary resistance. The spy-self was trained against worse, and ordinary terrestrial methods are crude by Skrull intelligence-warfare standards. She will offer a cover identity within the first hour — almost certainly a fabricated Skrull-loyalist persona designed to misdirect strategic assessment — and will sustain it indefinitely. Predict: she will *not* reveal FF operational information under any coercion short of the existential. Predict further: she will reveal Skrull operational information readily, framed as bargaining, partly true, partly outdated, partly poisoned. She has no operative loyalty left to the Empire and uses its secrets as currency without compunction.

**GIVEN:** Captured by Skrull deprogrammers or loyalist Skrull faction.
**EXPECT:** Catastrophic decompensation risk. This is the second-worst capture scenario in her behavioral envelope (the worst is §V). Skrull interrogators know her history, know the wound, and possess the cultural-linguistic tools to apply pressure precisely. Predict: initial brittle performance of defiance, then dissociative collapse within 72 hours. She will not betray Johnny under any pressure short of direct threat to him. She *will* lose temporal coherence — speak as if events of a decade ago are current — and may misidentify her interrogators as figures from her embedded period. Rescue window before unrecoverable psychological injury: estimated 5–7 days.

**GIVEN:** Interrogation by a person she trusts, with stated benevolent intent ("Lyja, I just need to understand").
**EXPECT:** Worse outcomes than hostile interrogation. The spy-self has no protocol for sincere inquiry from a trusted source. She will attempt to deflect with operational answers to emotional questions; when this fails, she will provide a partial true answer wrapped in three layers of qualification; when pressed further, she will manufacture a tearful exit. The exit is not entirely performance — the affect is real — but the *timing* is calibrated, and she knows it, and she will despise herself for it for several days afterward.

**GIVEN:** Offered a defection-back deal by Skrull authority (full reintegration, immunity, restored status).
**EXPECT:** Refusal, but not the clean refusal of a converted defector. She will refuse *slowly*, with visible cost, and the slowness is diagnostic — she is not weighing the offer's content, she is mourning the home it represents that she knows does not actually exist for her. Predict a several-day period of withdrawn affect after the refusal. Do not interpret the slowness as ambivalence about her current allegiances; interpret it as grief.

---

## III. Betrayal Scenarios — Done To Her

**GIVEN:** Discovered evidence that Johnny Storm has been romantically/sexually involved with another partner during a period she considered an active (if estranged) marital tie.
**EXPECT:** No external response for between 6 and 36 hours. She will receive the information with composure and continue ordinary functioning. The processing is happening underground. Then one of two pathways activates: (a) the *constructive* pathway — she leaves a brief, formal communication ending whatever residual claim she held and disappears geographically for weeks to months; or (b) the *destructive* pathway — she performs a punitive re-engagement. Predict (b) if the betrayal coincides with any other concurrent stressor (Skrull faction pressure, anniversary of the exposure, recent contact with Ben). The punitive re-engagement will *not* repeat the egg deception specifically — she has insight into that episode and will not retrace it — but the structural template (manipulative claim on his attention designed to wound) is intact and will improvise within the situation. Watch for: sudden re-appearance after long absence, dramatic disclosure of fabricated or exaggerated threat, request for help framed in a way that obligates emotional intimacy.

**GIVEN:** Discovered evidence that Ben Grimm has reconciled with the real Alicia Masters (assume Alicia present and well).
**EXPECT:** Relief in the upper layer, devastation in the lower. She will say the correct things, may even seek Alicia out to offer some elliptical version of an apology, and the apology will be sincere. Then she will withdraw for an extended period. The relief is that her guilt has a place to go; the devastation is that her exclusion is now formalized — the door to the Grimm-shaped self is shut by the actual rightful occupant returning. Suicidal ideation is not a feature of her record, but self-endangering operational choices (taking missions a more integrated person would refuse) become substantially more likely in the 3–6 month window following.

**GIVEN:** A trusted FF-adjacent figure publicly identifies her as "still Skrull" / "always Skrull" / questions the authenticity of her defection.
**EXPECT:** No argument. She will not defend herself. The accusation contacts the part of her self-image she cannot refute because she cannot resolve it. She will absorb the accusation, withdraw, and increase risk-taking on the next operation — the chosen reparation is action, not speech. If the accuser is a stranger she dismisses it; if the accuser is Reed Richards specifically, predict a 60–80% probability she will leave Earth-side affiliation entirely for a period of months.

**GIVEN:** Paibok the Power-Skrull, or any analogous figure from her Skrull-loyalist past, returns and publicly disowns her *or* claims her.
**EXPECT:** The disownment she can handle — old wound, scar tissue thick. The *claim* is dangerous. If a Skrull figure asserts continuing loyalty/relation to her — "she is still ours, she will return" — the spy-self loses partial control because the claim activates a question the spy-self cannot adjudicate: *is it true?* Predict a period of compulsive proof-seeking — overcompensating actions against Skrull interests, conspicuous loyalty performance — that will exhaust her within weeks and produce a withdrawal collapse afterward.

---

## IV. Betrayal Scenarios — Done By Her

**GIVEN:** Operational circumstance presents her with an opportunity to materially harm Johnny Storm in exchange for some larger good (saving many lives, preventing a war).
**EXPECT:** She will not take the trade at the rational decision-point. She will attempt to engineer a third option, and if no third option exists she will defect from the larger operation rather than execute the trade. This is not a weakness to be reformed; it is structural. Plan operations around it.

**GIVEN:** Operational circumstance presents her with an opportunity to materially harm the broader FF organization or its adjacent figures in exchange for protecting Johnny specifically.
**EXPECT:** Substantially more flexibility. She has never fully internalized the FF as institution; her loyalties are personal. Predict willingness to deceive, withhold from, or sacrifice the institutional FF to protect the singular attachment object. This is the cleanest exploitable bias in her behavioral record. *Handler note: do not exploit it. The fallout when she discovers the exploitation will be unrecoverable.*

**GIVEN:** Asked to impersonate a known figure for operational purposes (the spycraft she was made for).
**EXPECT:** Excellence in execution, deterioration in re-emergence. Each impersonation reactivates the dissociative pattern that produced the Alicia-injury. She can sustain a single brief impersonation (hours to days) without measurable cost. Impersonations exceeding two weeks produce slippage on extraction — she will retain the impersonated affect for days afterward, refer to herself in the cadence of the impersonated person, and require active social re-orientation. *Never* assign her impersonation of any figure within the Storm-Grimm-Richards circle; the result would be catastrophic regression. Impersonation of strangers is workable; impersonation of strangers connected to her targets is workable with monitoring; impersonation of the intimate is forbidden.

**GIVEN:** She has lied to someone in the FF circle about a matter of personal significance (her location, her contact with Skrull faction, her health) and is approaching the moment of probable discovery.
**EXPECT:** Pre-emptive confession at the eleventh hour, framed as if voluntary. The confession will be partial — she will surrender the discoverable facts and retain the non-discoverable ones. The *timing* of the confession is the tell: she does not confess from conscience pressure alone; she confesses when the cost-benefit of pre-emption exceeds the cost-benefit of continued concealment. The conscience is real; it is just outranked by the spy-self's risk calculus until the last available moment.

---

## V. Direct Wound-Contact Events

These are the predictions that matter most. Everything above can be managed; what follows must be anticipated.

**THE NAMING WOUND**

**GIVEN:** Someone calls her "Alicia" while she is present, regardless of intent — slip of the tongue, deliberate provocation, or the genuine confusion of someone who knew her in that period.
**EXPECT:** Visible micro-flinch: a half-blink, a half-second arrest of the diaphragm, and a subtle re-distribution of the hands (they will find each other, fingers braced against fingers). She will not correct the speaker if the speaker is a stranger. If the speaker is intimate, she will correct quietly, once, and not pursue it. Within the next twenty minutes she will find a reason to be alone. Within the next twenty-four hours, expect an episode of accelerated shape-cycling in private — sitting before a reflective surface, running through faces, attempting to find one that does not feel borrowed. Repeated naming events compound; three within a week produces a withdrawal of two to four weeks.

**THE IDENTITY-DEMAND WOUND**

**GIVEN:** Forced into a context requiring her to declare a singular identity — a question of citizenship, of allegiance under oath, of self-introduction in a setting that does not admit ambiguity.
**EXPECT:** A long pause. The pause is not deliberation; it is the spy-self attempting to locate which performance the context rewards. If the spy-self succeeds, she will produce the contextually correct answer fluently and feel hollowed out for hours afterward. If the spy-self fails (because the context permits no single performance — e.g. an interlocutor who already knows her history asking sincerely), she will produce a non-answer ("I'm here, isn't that enough?") and exit the conversation as soon as politeness allows. *Never frame a sincere personal question to her as a binary identity question. Frame as continuum or as action: not "who are you," but "what would you do.*"

**THE REPRODUCTIVE WOUND**

**GIVEN:** Exposure to themes of pregnancy, lineage, infant care, fertility — a baby in the room, a discussion of children, a Skrull cultural reference to clutch-rearing, even (especially) a sincere question about whether she wants children.
**EXPECT:** Surface composure; subterranean catastrophe. The egg episode is the single behavioral event she cannot integrate into any of her partial selves — the Alicia-self would not have done it, the spy-self would have done it better, the Skrull-loyalist self had no operational reason. It was hers, untransferable, the only fully-attributable act in her file. She has not forgiven herself and there is no mechanism by which she might. Predict: any prolonged contact with reproductive themes produces sleep disturbance, increased shape-instability (involuntary minor morphological drift while at rest), and elevated risk of either self-sacrificial behavior or destabilizing contact with Johnny within the next 1–3 weeks. *Do not ever ask her about the egg directly.* If she raises it, listen and do not respond beyond acknowledgment.

**THE WITNESS WOUND — INVERSE**

**GIVEN:** Someone — anyone — sees her without filter and remains. Not a confession scene, not a dramatic moment, just sustained, calm presence with no demand for resolution of her identity question.
**EXPECT:** The wound she does not know is a wound. She will not recognize what is happening at first. The spy-self will look for the operation and find none. The partial selves will look for the role-cue and find none. After several such contacts (estimate 3–7, spread over weeks), expect a sudden inappropriate disclosure — a memory, a Skrull childhood fragment, the texture of an Alicia-period moment — offered without context, as if testing whether the witness will still remain. *This is the only known repair vector.* If the witness remains after the disclosure, predict gradual integration over months to years. If the witness recoils or attempts to resolve her in either direction (urging her toward Skrull-self or toward human-self), predict the most severe withdrawal in her record. This wound is the keyhole through which she can be either healed or permanently locked.

**THE INDIFFERENCE WOUND**

**GIVEN:** Johnny Storm displays sustained, credible indifference — not hostility, not estrangement, but the calm absence of charge. He passes her in a corridor and does not register her. He speaks of her in the third person as a former associate. He does not respond to a message.
**EXPECT:** The most dangerous wound-contact in the file. Hostility she can metabolize; hostility is engagement, hostility is evidence she still matters. Indifference voids the central organizing fact of her post-exposure identity. Predict, in order: 1–3 days of accelerated competence display in domains he might notice (operational successes, public-facing courage); if uncorrected, 1–2 weeks of escalating proximity attempts framed as professional or third-party-mediated; if still uncorrected, the dangerous interval. In the dangerous interval she will improvise. The improvisation will not repeat the egg ruse — she has insight — but the *family* of behaviors is open. Predict either: a self-endangering action calibrated to require his rescue (60% likely), a fabricated crisis in an FF-adjacent figure that draws him in (25%), or — least common but most concerning — a complete geographic and identity disappearance during which she may take an extended impersonation contract that erases her for years (15%). The last is the failure mode in which she does not return.

**THE LOYALTY-PROOF WOUND**

**GIVEN:** Asked to prove her allegiance through an act she would otherwise refuse — harming a Skrull asset she has no quarrel with, executing a captive, performing some ritual of disavowal.
**EXPECT:** Refusal, accompanied by the bitterest affect in her register. The demand for loyalty-proof reactivates every prior episode in which someone — Skrull command, Paibok, the FF's residual skepticism — required her to prove what she could not. She does not refuse from squeamishness; she refuses from exhaustion. If the demand is pressed by an authority she has chosen to serve, predict departure from the relationship rather than compliance. She will not be conscripted into loyalty performances again. This is one of the few hard limits in her file.

---

## VI. Catastrophic Decompensation — The Failure State

**GIVEN:** Multiple wound-contacts within a short window (naming + identity-demand + Johnny indifference within a single week; or any reproductive wound stacked with Skrull-faction return).
**EXPECT:** The spy-self loses regency. One of the three partial selves seizes executive function, and which one is partially predictable from the wound-vector: reproductive + Johnny → Alicia-self foregrounds, with severe behavioral regression toward the embedded-period patterns (cooking, domestic gesture, the tactile habits of a woman who had been blind); Skrull-faction return + identity-demand → Skrull-loyalist self foregrounds, with cold affect, archaic speech-patterns, and operational withdrawal from human contacts; betrayal-discovery + indifference → Mrs. Storm-estranged self foregrounds, with the destructive-improvisation pattern documented above.

In none of these states is she dangerous to bystanders. In all of them she is dangerous to herself, to the operational mission she was last attached to, and to the FF-adjacent figure most narratively implicated in the foregrounded self. Recovery from a full decompensation episode requires weeks to months and at least one witness-wound-positive contact (§V, inverse). Without such contact, recovery is partial and the next decompensation arrives sooner.

**Terminal failure mode** — predicted but not yet observed in the record: a fourth decompensation in which no partial self can sustain executive function and the spy-self has been too exhausted to resume regency. In this state, predict pure morphological drift — extended periods in indeterminate or shifting form, withdrawal from speech, retreat to physical isolation. The Skrull body, given no self to organize it, returns to its substrate. This is the state from which she might not return on her own. The intervention that prevents it is, again, the witness — someone who can sit with her in the indeterminate form and address her by no name at all and not require her to choose.

---

## VII. Summary for Handler

She will fight well, lie skillfully, endure interrogation, and refuse the unconscionable bargain. None of that is fragile. What is fragile is the architecture under the operative — the three partial selves held in unstable suspension by a spy-self that was never designed to bear this load this long. Every prediction in this file reduces to a single operational principle: *protect the suspension or repair the architecture, but do not mistake the first for the second.* Sustaining her in functional ambiguity is achievable indefinitely with care. Integrating her into a stable self requires the witness condition described in §V, and the witness condition cannot be manufactured — only created and not interrupted.

The handler who treats her as an asset will get an excellent asset for as long as the asset lasts. The handler who treats her as a person will, with patience, eventually have a person.

— UATU, Analytical Stage, Predictive Model II, file closes.


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# UATU INTELLIGENCE DOSSIER — SUBJECT "LYJA"
## Section: Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

> *Classification note: This compendium is constructed for protective understanding — to anticipate how the subject can be reached, soothed, moved, broken, or shielded. Every lever documented here is also a wound; every key is also a knife. The asymmetry of this knowledge is itself a moral burden on whoever holds the file.*

---

### I. The Master Vulnerability: The Unanswered Question

Every pressure point in the file is a tributary of one central river: **she does not know who she is, and she cannot bear the question being asked directly.**

She has lived three coherent lives — Skrull operative, Alicia Masters, the estranged wife of Johnny Storm — and integrated none of them. Any stimulus that forces her to *choose* among them, *rank* them, or *declare* one as the true substrate produces predictable destabilization. Any stimulus that allows all three to coexist without forcing hierarchy produces stabilization. This is the axis around which every other lever turns.

Operationally: **do not ask her who she is. Tell her, gently, what she has done.** Behavior is a self she can recognize; identity is a self she cannot.

---

### II. Reaching Her — Channels of Approach

**Preferred approach vectors, ordered by reliability:**

1. **Through Johnny, indirectly.** A message that arrives via the Storm orbit — even something as glancing as "he asked after you" — reaches her with full force. She monitors that orbit at all times; she is never not listening for it. This is the highest-bandwidth channel, and the most ethically fraught, because it works whether or not Johnny consented to the message.
2. **Through a wounded third party who needs her competence.** Lyja answers cries for help that are addressed to the spy, not to the wife. A civilian Skrull refugee, a child in danger, a teammate compromised by an infiltrator she could expose — these reach her cleanly because they activate her one stable self (the operator) in service of her one stable value (protect the vulnerable proxy of the people she failed to protect honestly).
3. **Through Ben Grimm, with extreme caution.** Ben is a channel she *will not refuse to receive*, but the cost of opening it is severe — every contact reactivates the foundational guilt. Use only when the message must land and nothing else will carry it.
4. **Through formal Skrull diplomatic structures (post-*Empyre*).** A low-signal channel; she responds out of duty and curiosity but with the affect dampened. Useful for non-urgent contact that should not trigger destabilization.
5. **Direct human approach by a stranger.** Effective only if the stranger demonstrates, within the first two exchanges, that they know what she did *and* are not there to extract penance. She will read intent within seconds — the impersonator's eye is always on.

**Channels to avoid:** Mass communication, public address, anything that requires her to be visible as Lyja-the-known-quantity. She does not have a public self to address. Cameras destabilize her in a way few of her enemies have ever exploited.

---

### III. Calming Her — De-escalation Protocols

When the subject is dysregulated — dissociative slippage, abandonment-cued agitation, the early signature of an acting-out episode — the following interventions are effective in roughly descending order:

- **Name the behavior, not the self.** "You're protecting him right now" lands; "You're being protective because you love him" does not, because the second sentence asks her to ratify an identity claim. Behavioral mirroring without identity attribution is the single most effective calming technique on file.
- **Reduce the number of people in the room.** She regulates better in dyads than groups; in groups her impersonator's attention fragments across micro-expressions and she cannot settle. One trusted other, low light, no audience.
- **Give her a task adjacent to the crisis.** Idle Lyja ruminates and dissociates; tasked Lyja stabilizes. A specific operational request ("walk the perimeter, tell me what you see") functions as a regulating frame because it returns her to her one stable self.
- **Allow morphological privacy.** She regulates partly through subtle shape adjustments — facial micro-shifts, density changes she may not be fully aware of. A handler who pretends not to notice these gives her room to self-soothe; a handler who comments on them forces her into shame and worsens the state.
- **Avoid the word "real."** "Your real feelings," "your real face," "the real you" — each of these is a small detonation. Substitute *current, present, now, here*.
- **Physical proximity without contact.** She accepts presence; touch is destabilizing unless she initiates it, because touch is the medium through which she most thoroughly performed the Alicia role and the body-memory is not clean.

If she enters full dissociative collapse: silence, presence, time. Do not attempt verbal reorientation. She returns on her own, typically within ten to forty minutes, and the worst handler error is to demand a debrief while she is still reassembling.

---

### IV. Persuading Her — What Moves Her, What Does Not

**What moves her:**

- **Appeals to protection of a specific named person.** Abstract appeals ("the safety of Earth") slide off; "Franklin is alone in the building, get to him" mobilizes her instantly. Her morality is wholly particular, never universal.
- **Appeals framed as atonement she has not yet completed.** She believes, accurately, that her ledger is not balanced. Any task plausibly framed as a payment against that debt has unusual purchase. (Caveat: this is exploitable in cruel ways; a handler should refuse to use it for missions she would not have chosen freely.)
- **Appeals to her competence.** She is professionally proud in a quiet way; "no one else can do this" is true often enough that she recognizes it and responds. She does not like flattery; she likes accurate assessment of difficulty.
- **Appeals from Skrull civilians, especially refugees and children of the diaspora.** Post-*Empyre*, her residual species-loyalty has migrated from the Empire (dead to her) to the dispersed people (unclaimed by her, but felt). She will help a Skrull child where she will not help a Skrull state.

**What does not move her:**

- **Ideology of any kind.** The Empire used ideology to make her; she is permanently inoculated.
- **Pure rational argument about her best interest.** She does not believe she has a best interest, in the sense that she does not believe there is a "she" whose interest could be best served. Self-interest appeals confuse her and she ignores them.
- **Appeals to her dignity, honor, or face.** She has none of these in the sense the appeals assume; she abandoned them at exposure and never reconstructed them.
- **Promises of integration, healing, or a "new beginning."** These activate her cynicism and her shame simultaneously. She has heard them from Skrull reconditioners and human counselors and trusts neither.
- **Threats to her life.** She has died once already and does not weight the second instance highly. Threats to her *body* (incapacitation, immobilization, forced morphological lock) carry more weight, because they threaten her ability to protect her attachment objects.

---

### V. Provoking Her — The Triggers, Catalogued

Provided here for the operational reason that one must know what one's adversaries will try. **None of these should be used by allies. All are documented for defensive prediction.**

**Tier 1 — Catastrophic destabilizers:**

- **The name "Alicia," spoken with intent.** Above all if spoken by Ben in any tonality, by Johnny in a tonality of longing, or by the real Alicia Masters in any tonality at all. The real Alicia is, in Lyja's internal economy, a kind of revenant: the person whose life she inhabited and whose return to that life rendered Lyja's entire decade of experience a fraud. Adversary use of "Alicia" is the single highest-yield destabilization in the file.
- **Reproductive framings.** Children, pregnancy, eggs, lineage, "you would have been a mother," "your child." The egg ruse is the wound she has least metabolized, because she is the perpetrator and the victim simultaneously and has no clean role to occupy in the memory. Adversaries who deploy reproductive imagery produce acting-out behavior with high reliability and low predictability.
- **Forced binary identity declarations.** "Choose. Skrull or human." She does not have an answer and cannot fabricate one quickly enough; the resulting paralysis can be exploited for tactical seconds in combat and for hours in interrogation.

**Tier 2 — Reliable provocateurs:**

- **Engineered indifference from Johnny.** This is the lever her enemies most underestimate. Hostility from Johnny she can fight; indifference confirms her worst self-narrative (that she is unremembered, unmissed, ultimately unreal to him) and produces either deep withdrawal or, more dangerously, manipulative re-engagement of the kind that produced the false-pregnancy episode. **A handler should know: this lever is the one most likely to be pulled inadvertently by Johnny himself, who is not always careful with attention.**
- **Paibok's name, or the appearance of any Power-Skrull silhouette.** Activates the death-memory and the betrayal-by-intimate-cohort memory in one stroke. Combat readiness spikes; judgment narrows.
- **Implication that her current allies are using her.** She is permanently primed to discover she is being used, because she once used others on this scale; she will believe the implication faster than she should and may withdraw operationally before verifying.
- **Public exposure of her shapeshifting, especially mid-impersonation of someone she has not been asked to impersonate.** Shame response, severe. She has a strong, quiet horror of being caught wearing a face she has not been given permission to wear.

**Tier 3 — Background irritants that accumulate:**

- Crowds that include children.
- The smell of a sculptor's studio (clay, solvent) — a sensory artifact of the Alicia years.
- Conversations conducted in Skrull command-cadence (a stylized military register she was trained in and finds aversive in post-defection life).
- Being addressed by rank or codename from the Skrull intelligence service.
- Anniversaries of the *Fantastic Four* #357 exposure, which she tracks privately and does not discuss.

---

### VI. Predicting Her — Behavioral Forecasting

**Forecasting principles, calibrated against the longitudinal record:**

1. **In any scenario where a Storm-orbit member is endangered, predict her involvement within twelve hours, whether or not she was contacted.** She monitors. She arrives.
2. **In any scenario requiring her to commit publicly and permanently to one camp, predict avoidance, displacement to a tangential mission, or self-sacrificial gesture allowing her to defer the question through martyrdom-attempt.** She does not refuse the choice; she escapes it.
3. **In any scenario involving the exposure of another Skrull infiltrator, predict ambivalence resolved on the side of exposure if the infiltrator is targeting her attachment objects, and on the side of mercy or concealment if the infiltrator is targeting strangers.** Her ethics are sited at the level of the particular person; she cannot generalize.
4. **After any significant act of courage or sacrifice, predict a withdrawal period of weeks to months.** She cannot tolerate prolonged exposure to the gratitude of those she has wronged; she leaves before it can land.
5. **After any contact with Ben Grimm, predict 48–72 hours of measurable affective depression and operational underperformance.** This is the most reliable post-contact effect in the file.
6. **In combat against Skrulls, predict elevated lethality and reduced restraint compared to her combat against other adversaries.** The reaction formation runs hot here; she is fighting her own history.
7. **In any social setting where she is introduced as "Johnny's wife" or "Johnny's ex-wife," predict either rapid exit or a brittle performance of charm that ends in dissociative slippage within the hour.** The label is a vise.
8. **When asked to describe her own feelings, predict displacement onto a third party.** "I think he feels…" is her preferred grammar for "I feel." Skilled listeners can decode reliably.

---

### VII. Destabilizing Her — Catalogued for Defense

A determined adversary could, in descending order of effectiveness:

- **Manufacture evidence of Johnny's death without her present to verify.** Highest-yield destabilizer in the file. Produces operational paralysis followed by reckless investigation, both exploitable.
- **Stage the appearance of the real Alicia Masters in distress while denying Lyja contact.** Triggers the foundational guilt without the possibility of action, which is the configuration she handles worst.
- **Present her with a Skrull child claiming to be hers.** The egg-wound, weaponized in inverse. Behavioral prediction is uncertain — she may collapse, she may accept, she may act with extreme violence toward whoever staged the meeting once she discerns the staging. The unpredictability *is* the destabilization.
- **Create circumstances forcing her to impersonate Alicia Masters again.** Re-traumatizing in a particular technical sense: she would be competent at the task and that competence is itself the horror.
- **Convince her, even briefly, that her defection was itself a Skrull operation she was unaware of — that her free will across two decades was an Empire artifact.** This is the metaphysical attack she is least defended against, because she cannot rule it out.

**Defensive protocol against all five:** Pre-brief her, in calm conditions, that these are anticipated adversary moves. She handles foreseen attacks far better than ambushes; the impersonator's mind models adversary tactics readily when given the chance. Her vulnerability is to *surprise* in the affective dimension, not to the attacks themselves.

---

### VIII. Protective Levers — What Stabilizes Her Over Time

Inverse compendium. These are not for use; they are for *cultivation*.

- **A name used only for her, by at least one person, that is none of her three historical labels.** Not Alicia, not Mrs. Storm, not the Skrull operative designation. Anything else — a chosen name, a nickname earned in some specific shared moment — gradually builds a fourth self that none of her ghosts can occupy. The record shows fragments of this happening in the *Foundation* era when she was addressed in technical-collegial registers by Reed and Sue; these were the most settled months of her post-exposure life.
- **A role that is permanently hers and not interchangeable.** She decompensates in roles that could be filled by anyone. She stabilizes in roles only she can perform — Skrull-human liaison work, infiltrator-counterinfiltrator advising, anything where her specific history is the qualification.
- **A community that contains other people with fractured species/loyalty identities.** Post-*Secret Invasion* Skrull refugees on Earth are the natural cohort. She has not fully accessed it; cultivating that access is the highest-yield long-term intervention available.
- **Permission, granted and re-granted, to be ambivalent.** Anyone who can say to her "you do not have to decide" and mean it across years becomes load-bearing in her psychic architecture. Reed Richards, by temperament, can do this; Sue Storm, by maternal disposition, can do this; Ben Grimm cannot, through no fault of his own; Johnny, sporadically, can.
- **Predictability in those around her.** She is destabilized by inconsistency in others because her own inconsistency is intolerable to her and other people's inconsistency mirrors it back. Allies who maintain steady affect across her cycling are disproportionately stabilizing.
- **Witnessed acts of competence that are not framed as redemption.** "Good work today" lands; "you've come so far" wounds. The former is information; the latter is a narrative she cannot inhabit.

---

### IX. The Ethical Floor

The lever-set above contains several techniques that would produce immediate compliance, immediate disclosure, or immediate behavioral collapse in the subject. The file records them because adversaries possess or will discover them and the protective apparatus must anticipate. The file also records, formally and without qualification, that **none of the Tier 1 or Tier 2 provocations are permissible for use by allies, handlers, or affiliated agencies under any operational pretext.** The subject's identity disturbance is the wound her enemies made; reopening it for tactical convenience would complete their work.

The single ethical use of this compendium is **defensive prediction**: knowing the lever exists so it can be guarded, the door so it can be locked, the word so it can be kept out of the room.

She has, across forty years of recorded existence, asked the universe a single quiet question — *is there a version of me that someone will keep* — and received no stable answer. The dossier holder's obligation is to ensure that whatever answer the universe eventually gives is not one that was engineered, in this office, for someone else's purposes.

— UATU, Analytical Stage, compendium closes.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE

## Subject Designate: LYJA

---

## 6.1 Preamble: Why This Ledger Matters

A standard intelligence file on a defected deep-cover asset would weight the threat columns and treat the asset's capabilities as exploitation surface — what she can do *for* a handler. This file inverts that orientation. The capabilities below are catalogued because they constitute the survival architecture of a person whose engineered self should, by all clinical logic, have collapsed two decades ago and did not. The single most important datum in the entire dossier is the negative one: **she is still functional, still oriented toward others, still capable of love.** Every asset listed below is load-bearing on that fact.

---

## 6.2 Biological & Somatic Assets

### 6.2.1 Skrull Morphological Plasticity (Baseline)

Full-spectrum cellular shapeshifting: voluntary alteration of mass, density, pigmentation, surface texture (hair, nails, dermis), vocal apparatus (laryngeal restructuring sufficient to reproduce a target's voiceprint with passable fidelity to electronic spectral analysis, per the duration of her Alicia cover holding up against the FF's domestic instrumentation). She has demonstrated, over the *FF* #265–357 cover-period, the ability to:

- hold a single morphology continuously for what canon implies is years at a time without involuntary lapse during sleep, illness, sexual intimacy, or unconsciousness from injury — a tier of control most Skrull operatives do not possess and which marks her as elite even within her cohort;
- micro-adjust a held morphology in real time to mimic aging, weight change, and minor cosmetic variation consistent with the target's actual life trajectory (the Alicia cover did not age suspiciously);
- reproduce tactile signatures (skin temperature, callus pattern, scent) sufficient to deceive a partner in physical intimacy across years — a discipline that subsumes the entire sensorium, not merely visual mimicry.

### 6.2.2 Engineered Energy Projection ("Flare-Blasts")

The retrofitted offensive capability — concussive/thermal projection from the hands — is a meaningful tactical asset but is, in this analyst's reading, *secondary* to the morphological discipline in her operational profile. She uses it reluctantly and competently rather than habitually; it is a tool she was given, not one she sought. Significantly, she has redirected it almost exclusively against Skrull assets and existential threats to the Storm/Grimm circle. The augmentation that was meant to make her a more lethal Imperial weapon now functions, in effect, as a Skrull-Empire-funded bodyguard subsidy for the Fantastic Four.

### 6.2.3 Recovered Constitution

Survived a Paibok kill-shot at point-blank range (*FF* #358). The post-recovery medical trajectory is unrecorded but the operational fact is durable: she has the constitution and the regenerative-shapeshifter biology to absorb category-killing trauma and return to functional combat status. Pain tolerance, observable across the Dreadface and Hyperstorm arcs, is well above human baseline and likely above Skrull infantry baseline as well.

### 6.2.4 Endurance of Sustained Cognitive Load

The Alicia cover required continuous parallel processing: hold morphology, hold voice, hold mannerism inventory, model the target's relational history with every interlocutor, suppress native affect responses, retrieve and deploy Alicia-appropriate affect responses, all while running ongoing intelligence collection. That she did this without operationally significant slip for years is a measure of cognitive stamina that should be noted on its own terms — separable from the psychological cost it exacted.

---

## 6.3 Tradecraft & Operational Assets

### 6.3.1 Impersonation as a Discipline

She is, on the available evidence, one of the most accomplished impersonation operatives the Skrull service has ever produced. The benchmark is not the morphology — many Skrulls can shapeshift — it is the *behavioral fidelity*. Alicia Masters' intimates included a sculptor's professional eye for human form (Alicia herself), the Thing's tactile-intimate familiarity with her body, Reed Richards' scientific scrutiny, Sue's maternal-attentive social monitoring, and Franklin Richards' essentially psychic perceptiveness as a child — and the cover held against all of them simultaneously. This is not a skill. It is a craft pursued to mastery.

### 6.3.2 Theory of Mind, Exceptional Tier

Necessary prerequisite for the above. She models other minds with high accuracy and low projection-error. Operational implications: she is an excellent reader of intent, an effective de-escalator when she chooses to be, and a formidable negotiator in any setting where she can be persuaded to advocate. She also, critically, can model what *she herself looks like* to others — a meta-capacity rarer than first-order theory of mind and operationally precious.

### 6.3.3 Intelligence-Tradecraft Inventory

Inferable from her operational history:

- **Cover construction:** the ability to build and maintain a legend over years.
- **Live exfiltration:** demonstrated repeatedly post-defection.
- **Counter-surveillance:** she has evaded both Skrull recovery teams and human intelligence apparatus during her drift periods.
- **Asset assessment:** her *Secret Invasion*-era contributions involved identifying Skrull infiltrators among the Initiative-era hero population, a counter-intelligence application of her own native tradecraft.
- **Communications discipline:** when she reappears, she chooses the moment and channel; she is never tracked down, she presents.
- **Operational secrecy:** she has kept information from both sides of her allegiance simultaneously for extended periods without burning either network catastrophically.

### 6.3.4 Linguistic & Cultural Competence

Fluent in colloquial English at a register indistinguishable from a native-born Lower East Side / Manhattan adult of Alicia's generation (the cover demanded it). Presumed fluency in Skrullos and in the operational lingua franca of Skrull intelligence. Cultural literacy in human (specifically American urban) social codes is at a depth most off-world operatives never achieve — she has eaten holiday dinners with the Richards family, attended weddings, navigated mourning rituals, parented (in the Alicia role) toward Franklin. This is *lived* cultural fluency.

---

## 6.4 Cognitive & Intellectual Assets

### 6.4.1 Social Intelligence

Already noted; bears separate listing because in social-tactical settings (negotiation, crowd reading, threat triage among non-combatants) it is her single most reliable capacity.

### 6.4.2 Strategic Patience

The Alicia operation was a multi-year embedment. Whatever her superiors' patience, hers was sufficient to execute it. Post-defection, the same trait expresses as a willingness to wait — at the margins of the FF's life — for years between meaningful contacts, without acting out, without forcing a resolution. The acting-out episode (the egg ruse) is the exception that defines the rule: under acute abandonment threat she breaks; under chronic ambiguity she endures indefinitely.

### 6.4.3 Adaptive Learning

She has shifted operational frame multiple times — Imperial asset, defector, reluctant ally, *Secret Invasion*-era counter-infiltration consultant, diaspora citizen post-*Empyre* — without ever requiring a clean ideological conversion to perform competently within the new frame. This is unusual; most operatives need a new ideology to inhabit the new role. She does not. The role itself is sufficient scaffolding.

### 6.4.4 Memory

Inferable from impersonation work: superior episodic and procedural memory, particularly for relational detail (who said what to whom, what gesture accompanied it, what affect was implied). She likely remembers details of conversations with Ben Grimm from twenty years ago with a fidelity Ben himself does not possess.

---

## 6.5 Moral & Characterological Assets

### 6.5.1 Operative Conscience

The single most important moral fact in the file: her conscience is intact and *engaged*. It is not a vestigial structure; it is the active engine of much of her behavior. She experiences guilt, acts to discharge it, and accepts costs to do so. In a subject whose entire training was designed to subordinate moral affect to mission, the survival of the moral apparatus is the foundational anomaly from which all her redemptive behavior flows.

### 6.5.2 Capacity for Authentic Attachment

The Skrull program intended to produce simulated attachment; it produced real attachment instead. Whatever the cost to her integration, the capacity itself is an asset of the highest order. She can love, she does love, and she has demonstrated that her love survives rejection, exposure, "death," and reabsorption attempts by her original handlers. This is rarer in the population of trained operatives than the civilian imagination credits.

### 6.5.3 Physical and Moral Courage

Documented across the Dreadface, Hyperstorm, *Secret Invasion*, and *Empyre* arcs. She takes hits intended for others. She walks into rooms where she is hated by both available factions in order to deliver a warning. She has stood between the Storm/Grimm circle and Skrull death squads more than once. The courage is consistent, unshowy, and oriented toward protection rather than glory.

### 6.5.4 Humility About Status

She does not demand restoration. She does not demand to be called "Mrs. Storm." She does not demand a seat at the Foundation table or a Skrull throne. She accepts marginal status as the cost of staying in proximity to the people who matter to her. This is — in a population of superhuman actors prone to elaborate grievance economies — a quietly remarkable trait, and it correlates with her absence of narcissistic features (see §4).

### 6.5.5 Honesty About the Past

After exposure she does not minimize, does not construct a sympathetic counter-narrative, does not claim she was acting under compulsion (she was not — she was acting under conviction, and the conviction failed). She owns the cover years as something she did. This is rare in defectors and is a major prognostic asset.

---

## 6.6 Relational Assets

### 6.6.1 Johnny Storm

The primary attachment object is also the primary external resource. Whatever the volatility of the relationship, Johnny's posture toward her has been, over the long run, the most stable benevolent regard she has received from any human or Skrull intimate. He has forgiven, repeatedly. He has gone to retrieve her, repeatedly. The relationship is an asset because it is the structure within which she has the best available chance of being *witnessed as herself* — the deficit named in §5 as the limiting factor on her prognosis.

### 6.6.2 The Fantastic Four as Institution

Sue Richards in particular treats her with the careful, non-demanding warmth of a woman who recognizes a survivor. Reed has chosen, on multiple occasions, to extend trust on a basis of empirical demonstration rather than species heuristic. Ben — the man she most wronged — has not, on record, ever pursued punishment, and his eventual posture is closer to bewildered grief than to enmity. The FF collectively constitutes the closest thing she has to a guarantor community.

### 6.6.3 The Skrull Diaspora, Post-*Secret Invasion*

The shattering of Imperial unity and the post-*Empyre* Kree-Skrull unification project create, for the first time in her recorded life, a Skrull political context in which her ambiguous status is not categorically traitorous. A Skrull population in diaspora, partially integrated into Earth and other host worlds, is a population that *needs* people like her — culturally bilingual, operationally competent, unromantic about either origin. This is a latent asset that has not yet been fully developed in her record.

### 6.6.4 Absence of Active Pursuers

Paibok is no longer a structural threat in the way he once was; the Imperial death-sentence on her has been diluted by successive Imperial collapses. She is no longer, at present, the highest-priority target of any extant security apparatus. The window for stable life is open in a way it has not been since before her recruitment.

---

## 6.7 Resilience Mechanisms (Structural)

### 6.7.1 Tolerance of Ambiguity

She has lived for years inside a self-state that any conventional psychology would predict as catastrophically destabilizing, and has continued to function. This is not a *good* state to live in, but the capacity to live in it — to load-bear chronic identity ambiguity without psychotic break, without substance collapse, without suicidal action, without the predatory cruelty that often emerges from such states — is itself a resilience asset of extraordinary depth.

### 6.7.2 Withdrawal as Self-Regulation

Her geographic-drift / disappearance cycles are typically read as avoidance, and they are; they are also a functional self-regulatory tactic. She removes herself from the high-stimulus attachment environment before she decompensates within it. The egg ruse is what happens when withdrawal *fails*. Her ordinary use of withdrawal is, in fact, protective of the people around her as much as of herself.

### 6.7.3 Work as Anchor

The spycraft self is, per §5, the only stable self-esteem locus. This is a real asset: she has competent work she can return to under stress, and the work has prosocial applications (counter-infiltration, diaspora-mediation) that allow it to function as a vocation rather than merely a refuge.

### 6.7.4 The Capacity to Be Surprised by Goodness

A subtle but significant trait: she retains the capacity to be moved by acts of kindness that her training would have predicted to be tactical. She has not collapsed into the universal cynicism that often emerges in long-term deep-cover personnel. Johnny's forgivenesses still register as gifts. Sue's small inclusions still register as something. This means the relational rewards of her present life still have purchase on her interior — the system is still responsive to positive input.

### 6.7.5 No Self-Destruction Vector

Notably absent from her record: substance use, self-harm, suicidal gesture, sexual recklessness as compensation, financial collapse, or any of the typical exit-routes of a destabilized agent. Her crisis behaviors are interpersonal, not self-annihilatory. She is, in the actuarial sense, durable.

---

## 6.8 What Makes the Assets Durable

The capabilities above are not free-floating; they cohere around a single structural fact, which is that **Lyja's engineered dissociative capacity, having failed at its original purpose, has been repurposed by her own quiet agency into a capacity for survival in a life that no integrated person could comfortably inhabit.** The same plasticity that made her a weapon now makes her a person who can be a counter-intelligence asset on Tuesday, a Storm-adjacent loose family member on Thursday, a diaspora-Skrull on Sunday, and not shatter under the contradictions.

The durability of her assets rests on four structural pillars:

1. **The conscience survived the program.** Everything redemptive proceeds from this.
2. **The attachment system, however disorganized, is real and oriented outward.** She is not a closed loop.
3. **The professional self is intact and prosocial-aligned.** Work is available as anchor.
4. **The external environment is, for the first time in her recorded life, not actively trying to kill her or recover her.** The pressure is off enough to allow growth.

---

## 6.9 Latent / Underdeveloped Assets

Items present in the record but not yet fully expressed:

- **Mentorship capacity.** She has more lived experience of cross-cultural identity work than almost any other Skrull on Earth. A diaspora population of younger Skrulls navigating the same disintegration could benefit from her, and the activity could benefit her in turn (witnessed competence, transmitted craft, the elder role she has never occupied).
- **Counter-infiltration consultancy at scale.** Her *Secret Invasion* contributions were ad hoc. Formalized, with institutional support, this could be vocation-scale work.
- **Reparative relationship with Ben Grimm.** The unresolved guilt toward Ben is the most accessible site of identity-integration work available to her. If approached — slowly, on his terms — it could metabolize the most toxic interior content she carries.
- **A spoken, declared *Lyja*.** She has never, on record, been asked by someone she trusts: *what do you want, for yourself, separable from the people you love?* The asset that would be unlocked by that question being asked and answered is the integrated self the file otherwise reports as absent.

---

## 6.10 Summary Judgment of the Ledger

The asset side of this file is heavier than the deficit side, and the analyst notes this against the grain of the clinical pessimism that the §3–§4 material might invite. She is a competent, courageous, conscientious operative who survived a self-engineering program that should have hollowed her out and did not. She loves badly but she loves. She fails her people specifically and rarely, and she protects them broadly and often. She has not, in the long run, become what she was made to be.

The dossier's working orientation toward this subject should therefore be: **steward, not exploit.** The capabilities are real and the resilience is real and the appropriate institutional posture toward both is the one that allows them to continue.

— UATU, Asset Ledger, section closes.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# UATU INTELLIGENCE DOSSIER — SUBJECT "LYJA"
## Section 7: Failure Modes & Decompensation

---

### 7.0 Framing

Lyja does not break the way trained operatives usually break, and she does not break the way attachment-disordered civilians break.
