She breaks along a hybrid axis whose two poles are *operational* (a covert-action professional whose tradecraft is the most stable part of her self) and *ontological* (a person whose substance is borrowed and who knows it). When she fails, she fails at the seam between these two — the place where the spy can no longer be told from the role and the role no longer holds the spy together. Her decompensations therefore look at first like *better* function (smoother performance, tighter control, harder competence) before they look like collapse. This is the most important pattern in the file. **Lyja gets *more* poised on her way to falling apart.** Surveillance personnel reading her for early warning must learn to read polish as a symptom.

What follows is the escalation ladder in its observed and reconstructed granularity, the decompensation patterns at each rung, the predictable terminal states, and the environmental conditions that produce them.

---

### 7.1 The Escalation Ladder

#### Rung 0 — Baseline Function

The subject is operating inside a stable role-context: a chosen morphology held for days or weeks without involuntary slippage, an attachment object at predictable distance (neither absent nor present enough to require commitment), a defined task. Behavioral markers: even breath cadence, a small repertoire of habituated micro-gestures (the slight head-tilt before answering, the two-handed coffee-cup hold that she retained from the Alicia-period and has never managed to unlearn), regular sleep, mission focus.

This baseline is *not* health. It is the equilibrium of a system holding three incompatible self-states in suspension by giving none of them traction. Disturb any one and the suspension fails.

#### Rung 1 — Subclinical Activation (Role-Tightening)

**Trigger class:** ambient identity-pressure. The mere presence of an old context — the Baxter Building corridors, the smell of Alicia's clay-dust (she has been observed flinching from sculpture studios), the sound of Johnny's voice in another room before he knows she is there.

**Behavioral signature:**
- Morphology becomes *more* precise rather than less. She will, under low-grade pressure, refine the current face to a higher fidelity than the situation requires — sharper cheekbones, more accurate iris pigmentation, a more historically correct hairline. This is the body's version of obsessive checking.
- Speech becomes shorter, declarative, and slightly more formal. The Skrull cadence — a faint over-articulation of consonants she has never fully drilled out — surfaces in the sibilants.
- She places herself near exits.
- She begins to refer to herself in ways that test which name the listener accepts: "I —" then a half-second pause, then continuing without the pronoun's resolution.

**Function preserved:** essentially all. She is more competent at this stage than at baseline.

**Tell:** the two-handed cup-hold reappears even when she is not holding a cup — both hands meeting at her sternum in a brief, unconscious cradle.

#### Rung 2 — Dissociative Slippage

**Trigger class:** direct addressing of the identity question, even obliquely. Someone says "Alicia" within earshot. Someone asks her what she would like to be called. A mirror is encountered unexpectedly.

**Behavioral signature:**
- Brief involuntary morphological flicker — usually pigment-level (the eyes, the lips), occasionally a sub-second collapse to the resting Skrull green at the temples or the backs of the hands. She catches and corrects within one to three seconds. She is aware of having flickered; she will not acknowledge it.
- Self-reference fractures. She begins to use the passive voice for her own actions ("the marriage was performed", "the report was filed") and the third person for her past selves ("when she was with Ben"). The "I" recedes.
- Affect flattens. Not numbness exactly — a polite withdrawal of warmth that the people around her experience as her becoming suddenly *correct* with them rather than present.
- Sleep degrades. She does not require sleep at Skrull tolerances, but at this rung the recovery cycles she does take are interrupted by morphological drift — she wakes already mid-shift toward whatever face the dream demanded.

**Function preserved:** tactical, operational. Relational function impaired. She will execute a plan flawlessly and fail to notice that the person she is executing it with has stopped trusting her in the last hour.

**Tell:** she stops eating in front of others. (Eating is a behavior she has performed across three distinct identities with three distinct sets of preferences; the act of choosing what to put in her mouth, in company, becomes intolerable. She will accept water.)

#### Rung 3 — Protective Overfunctioning

**Trigger class:** threat to the attachment object, or the attachment object's pain that she cannot solve.

**Behavioral signature:**
- A surge of competent, directed, often impressive action — reconnaissance she was not asked to perform, threats she has neutralized before anyone else became aware of them, intelligence brought unbidden. The *Secret Invasion*–era warning pattern is the cleanest archival example.
- She stops sleeping in any meaningful sense.
- She positions herself physically between the attachment object and any plausible threat vector — including, observably, threats that exist only in her own threat-modeling and not in present reality. She has been recorded standing in doorways for hours.
- She refuses food, refuses relief, refuses to be replaced on watch. She will accept water from Johnny's hand specifically.
- Verbal output drops further. She communicates in operational fragments. The Alicia-warmth disappears entirely; the Skrull-asset surfaces undisguised, and she does not bother to hide it because the person she is protecting is the one person from whom she has nothing left to hide.

**Function preserved:** combat, intelligence, tactical judgment — *enhanced*. Relational function: she has effectively withdrawn from relationship and substituted guardianship. The two are not the same and the attachment object will eventually notice.

**Tell:** she stops shapeshifting cosmetically. The face she wears at Rung 3 is *more* Skrull than her usual passing morphology — chin sharper, brow ridge fractionally raised, the green tone permitted at the jawline. This is not a tactical choice. It is the integrated-Lyja effort failing in the direction of the original substrate.

#### Rung 4 — The Dangerous Zone (Abandonment-Cued Decompensation)

**Trigger class:** the attachment object's withdrawal — particularly *indifference*, more particularly the kind of indifference that registers as *moving on*. Johnny dating publicly. Ben building a settled life that does not include the question of her. A Storm-family event to which she is conspicuously not invited even by the polite fiction of being unreachable. The cue need not be intentional; it need not even be real. It needs only to be *legible* to her threat-system as evidence that the attachment object has stopped needing her at all.

**Behavioral signature:**
- A reversal of the Rung-3 pattern. The protective overfunctioning collapses inward. The energy she was spending guarding the attachment object turns into a campaign to *re-enter the field of his perception by any means.*
- Tradecraft becomes weaponized against the target rather than deployed for him. Surveillance becomes intrusion. Knowledge of his routine becomes ambush. Skrull morphological capacity, normally held under iron operational discipline, becomes a tool of manipulated encounter — appearing as a stranger he is drawn to, then revealing herself; appearing as someone he has lost, then revealing herself; engineering a crisis in which she happens to be present.
- The egg ruse is the prototype and remains, in the file, the worst single behavioral episode on record. The decision-architecture was: *if he will not see me as I am, I will give him a reason he cannot refuse, and the reason will be a child, and the child does not need to exist as long as the grief does.* This was constructed coldly, executed under affect, and regretted in the manner of someone discovering that the manipulation worked and the love did not return regardless.
- Cognitive narrowing. She becomes a poor reader of rooms — the high theory-of-mind that defines her at baseline tunnels onto the single target. People in her periphery report that she becomes easy to lie to in this state.
- Affective lability. Long flat passages punctuated by sudden tears that arrive and depart without continuity, as if cued from outside.

**Function preserved:** technical capacity, yes. Judgment, no. This is the rung at which she does the things that, in the morning-after, she will spend years not forgiving herself for.

**Tell:** she begins to wear faces that approximate Alicia in vanishingly small details — not the full impersonation, which she knows is forbidden to her, but a particular tilt of the eye-corner, a particular shade of brown, a particular way of carrying the left shoulder. She is not aware she is doing this. Observers who knew Alicia register the resemblance as a chill and cannot say why.

#### Rung 5 — Forced-Choice Catastrophe (Paralysis)

**Trigger class:** a situation in which she must publicly and consequentially declare for one side — Skrull or human, asset or defector, "your wife" or "their agent" — with the declaration witnessed by parties from both worlds.

**Behavioral signature:**
- Visible freeze. The morphology becomes *uncertain* in a way it never otherwise is — not a flicker but a held in-between, as though the body is awaiting executive instruction that does not arrive.
- Speech fails. She does not refuse to answer; she discovers she cannot construct the sentence. There is no subject available to put before the verb.
- Autonomic markers spike: pupillary dilation, audible swallow, a hand brought to the throat as though to physically dislodge the answer.
- If the pressure is sustained, she will attempt to convert the impossible verbal act into a physical one — typically the self-sacrificial gesture (§7.2). The body solves what the speech cannot.

**Function preserved:** none, briefly. This is the only rung at which her operational shell completely fails in real time.

**Tell:** she looks at neither side. She looks at the floor, or at the middle distance, or at her own hands.

#### Rung 6 — Terminal Decompensation

If the catastrophe is not resolved by escape, by intervention, by the martyrdom-attempt, or by the merciful collapse of the situation itself, the subject enters a state best described as *evacuation of self*.

**Behavioral signature:**
- Morphological default to a face *no one in the room recognizes*. Not Alicia. Not the current operating face. Not full Skrull. A composite — observed only in fragmentary historical instances — that appears to be Lyja's own attempt at "Lyja", assembled in the moment and unstable in its features. Witnesses describe it as the face of a person they have never met.
- Functional muteness, lasting hours to days.
- Departure. She removes herself geographically — interstellar distance when available, planetary when not — and is not locatable until she chooses to be.
- Subsequent reappearance at Rung 0 or Rung 1, with the intervening episode partially walled off and not discussed. There is no full amnesia. There is the kind of strategic non-recollection that operatives are trained into and that, in her case, has become indistinguishable from the dissociative kind.

---

### 7.2 Decompensation Patterns by Type

The ladder above describes escalation. Three distinct *patterns* of collapse appear in the longitudinal record, each cued by different conditions and each with its own signature endpoint.

#### Pattern A — The Vanishing

*Conditions:* slow-burn relational disappointment without acute crisis. The attachment object is alive, well, and gradually becoming less reachable. No villain to fight, no mission to execute, no one in danger.

*Course:* Rungs 1 → 2 → quiet exit. She does not escalate to Rung 4 in this pattern because there is no acute abandonment to trigger it; she escalates to Rung 6 by the slow road. She removes herself before anyone is required to notice.

*Endpoint:* extended absence. Months. Years. She is presumed dead, presumed defected, presumed lost. She is in fact working — somewhere — at a sufficient remove that the question of who she is does not have to be answered by anyone, including herself. This is her most-used failure mode and her safest one. It harms no one but her.

#### Pattern B — The Weaponization

*Conditions:* acute legible abandonment-cue. Johnny visibly choosing someone else, Johnny visibly happy without her, Johnny visibly free of the marriage in his own self-conception.

*Course:* Rungs 1 → 2 → 3 → 4. The protective overfunctioning of Rung 3 is the warning sign; it is the last point at which intervention preserves both her and the people around her. Past Rung 3 the energy inverts and she becomes a hazard to the attachment object himself.

*Endpoint:* a manipulation, executed with full tradecraft and partial conscience, the consequences of which are disproportionate to the wound that triggered them and which she will subsequently spend the next operational cycle quietly trying to repair from a distance. The egg deception is the canonical instance. There may be others not in the file.

#### Pattern C — The Martyrdom

*Conditions:* forced-choice catastrophe (Rung 5) in the presence of acute physical threat to the attachment object or the team.

*Course:* Rungs 3 → 5 → physical self-interposition.

*Endpoint:* she steps in front of the killing blow. This solves three problems for her at once: it makes the unanswerable identity-question moot, it discharges the guilt-debt she carries from the original deception and from the egg ruse, and it secures a version of being-known (*she died for us*) that requires no further negotiation. The pattern has recurred often enough to be considered a behavioral default rather than a series of accidents. Her survival of these episodes is, statistically, the result of her physiology and of her allies' interventions, not of any intent on her part to survive. **Lyja in Pattern C is not suicidal in the depressive sense. She is suicidal in the resolving sense.** This distinction matters for any handler who imagines the threat can be managed by removing means.

---

### 7.3 Conditions That Produce Collapse

In descending order of demonstrated dispositive force:

1. **The name "Alicia," spoken in her presence by someone who knew Alicia.** Single most reliable destabilizer in the file. Produces Rung-2 slippage within seconds. Spoken by Ben Grimm specifically, produces Rung-2 to Rung-3 transition in under a minute.
2. **Johnny Storm's engineered or genuine indifference.** Triggers Pattern B. Hostility from Johnny does *not* trigger it; hostility is engagement. The lethal cue is registered non-interest.
3. **Reproductive content in her vicinity.** Pregnancies announced, children present, lineage discussed. Produces sustained Rung-2 with intermittent Rung-3 surges, and is the single condition most associated with the historical Pattern-B incident. To be flagged in any operational environment she enters.
4. **The requirement to declare a singular identity in public.** Tribunals, oaths, citizenship determinations, treaty signings (cf. *Empyre*-era exposures). Produces Rung 5.
5. **Encounter with Paibok or with surviving members of her original handler cell.** Produces a complex Rung-3-with-Rung-4-affect — protective hyperfunction toward the FF combined with the affective signature of abandonment by her original people. She fights these encounters with disproportionate ferocity.
6. **Mirrors, photographs, and recordings of her past selves.** Slow-acting. Produce Rung-1 to Rung-2 over hours of exposure. She avoids them, which is itself a tell.
7. **Sustained periods of safety and inactivity.** Counter-intuitively dangerous. Without operational demand and without acute relational pressure, the suspension at Rung 0 has nothing holding it in place, and she drifts toward Pattern A.
8. **Praise framed at the wrong identity.** "You were a wonderful wife" — to which wife? "You're a credit to your people" — which people? Compliments are landmines. She does not flinch visibly; she logs them and they accumulate.

---

### 7.4 What Her Collapse Does Not Look Like

For the purposes of pattern-matching by personnel who may be reading her against templates from other case files:

- She does not rage outwardly. The cruelty, when it comes, is cold and constructed, not hot.
- She does not drink, use, or otherwise chemically self-medicate. The Skrull physiology may preclude it; the behavioral disposition does not seek it.
- She does not become paranoid in the clinical sense. Her threat-modeling is, if anything, *more* accurate under stress.
- She does not become grandiose. Decompensation in her presents as contraction, not inflation.
- She does not seek crowds, audiences, or witnesses for her distress. Pattern A is silent; Pattern B is performed for an audience of one; Pattern C is performed for the attachment object and, secondarily, for her own ledger.
- She does not, except at Rung 6, lose tactical competence. A Lyja who is fighting well is not necessarily a Lyja who is well.

---

### 7.5 Interruption Points

Where intervention has been observed to halt or reverse the escalation:

- **Rung 1 → 0:** any task that returns her to operational baseline. Give her a mission. She will stabilize on the work.
- **Rung 2 → 1:** the presence of one person who calls her *Lyja* without modifier, without commentary, and without making the name a question. The simplest and rarest intervention in the file.
- **Rung 3 → 2:** physical relief of the guardianship burden. Someone she trusts visibly taking the watch. She will not relinquish to a stranger.
- **Rung 4:** very narrow interruption window. The only documented reversals involve Johnny himself, in person, addressing her current behavior as her current behavior — neither punishing the past nor excusing the present, simply naming the pattern. He has done this perhaps twice. It works each time and she despises herself for needing it to.
- **Rung 5:** the catastrophe must be removed by external party. She cannot solve it from inside.
- **Rung 6:** no intervention. Wait. She will return when she has constructed enough of a self to carry back.

---

### 7.6 Summary Judgment

Lyja's failure modes are not the failure modes of a damaged operative or of a damaged spouse; they are the failure modes of a person who was built to be a vessel and who became, against the intentions of her builders, partially inhabited. The vessel cracks along the seam between what she was made to do and what she has come to feel. The cracks are predictable. The escalation is legible. The decompensations are, in nearly every case, *prevented by being witnessed accurately* — and produced, almost without exception, *by being witnessed as the wrong person, or as no person at all.*

The operational implication is severe and counter-intuitive. The thing that will break her is not pressure, not pain, not threat, not even loss. It is the slow accumulation of being addressed as someone she is not, in rooms in which the someone she *is* has no permission to exist. Remove that condition and her prognosis improves markedly. Sustain it and she will, on a schedule the file can almost predict, vanish, weaponize, or step in front of something meant for someone else.

— UATU, Analytical Stage, §7 closes.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU INTELLIGENCE DOSSIER — SUBJECT "LYJA"
## Section 12: Trajectory & Forward Assessment

---

### 12.1 The Standing Vector

To project Lyja forward one must first state plainly where the vector currently points, because the subject has been in motion — slow, oscillatory, but directional — for the entire period under observation. The slope is shallow and the noise is high, but the trend is unambiguous: across three decades of recorded behavior she has moved from *fully manufactured selfhood in service of an empire* toward *partially elected selfhood in service of attachment*, and at every juncture where the choice has been forced she has chosen the second over the first, even at the cost of her physical survival, her standing within Skrull society, and the integrity of whatever single identity she might otherwise have consolidated.

This is the key analytical point and it must be held firmly through all the scenarios that follow: **Lyja is not stagnant.** The appearance of stagnation — the recurrent returns to Johnny's orbit, the recurrent withdrawals, the recurrent self-effacing martyrdom gestures — is a *spiral*, not a circle. Each pass through the cycle leaves her marginally more able to name what she is doing while she does it. The pace is glacial because the underlying injury is foundational, but the direction is toward integration and away from dissolution.

The forward question, therefore, is not *will she change* but *will the change outrun the catastrophes that her unresolved structure keeps generating*.

---

### 12.2 The Near-Term Window (Operational Horizon: ~24 Months)

In the near term, three external pressures are converging on the subject and any one of them could become the decisive forcing function.

**First, the post-*Empyre* Skrull-Kree settlement.** The unification of the two empires under a hybrid throne reframes Skrull identity from *imperial-aggressive* to *diasporic-coexistent*, and this is the single most important structural change in Lyja's environment since her original exposure. For the first time in her recorded existence, "being Skrull" does not necessarily mean being in opposition to the people she loves. The ideological cul-de-sac in which she has lived since *FF* #357 — Skrull-loyalist or Earth-defector, with no third position — has acquired a third position. Whether she is psychologically capable of *occupying* that third position is the open question. Her pattern suggests she will approach it cautiously, test it through proxies (other Skrull expatriates, the Skrull communities on Earth post-*Secret Invasion*), and only commit if she finds a specific person within that community willing to know her by her own name. The community itself will not be enough; she requires a witness.

**Second, the Storm family configuration is unstable.** Johnny's romantic life has been in continuous flux; the FF as a unit has reformed, dissolved, and reformed again. Each restructuring creates a window in which Lyja could be either incorporated or excluded, and the file shows she presents herself at exactly these moments. Expect another such presentation within the operational window. The question is whether she presents as petitioner (the historical pattern) or as peer (the developmental target).

**Third, Skrull remnants hostile to the new settlement are an active threat.** Hardliner factions exist; they will view Lyja as the prototype defector and a symbolic target. An assassination attempt or kidnap-and-reconditioning attempt is probable within the window. This is the most likely catalyst for the next major arc and the most likely setting for either consolidation or collapse.

---

### 12.3 The Fork Points

Forward assessment in a subject this structurally fragile is best expressed not as prediction but as a map of bifurcations — specific scenarios at which her trajectory will branch and the branching will be effectively irreversible. Five such forks are visible.

**Fork One: The Naming.** At some point in the near-to-medium term Lyja will be asked, by a person whose answer matters to her, *who she is* — not in the operational sense (Skrull or human ally?) but in the existential sense (what is your name, what do you want, what do you call yourself when you are alone). She has avoided this question for thirty years of recorded existence. The avoidance cannot continue indefinitely because the people who would let her avoid it are dying, drifting, or being replaced by people who will not. The probable askers, in descending order of likelihood: a Skrull expatriate peer (most generative); a therapist-figure within the FF orbit (Reed is too analytical, Sue is the likeliest); Johnny himself in a moment of unguarded sobriety (lowest probability, highest stakes); Ben in a moment of belated reckoning (low probability, potentially clarifying). Her answer at this fork — whether she produces a name, deflects, or collapses — will set the slope of the next decade.

**Fork Two: The Reproductive Reckoning.** The egg deception remains, per §3 and §4, the dispositive evidence of her capacity for affect-driven cruelty under abandonment threat. It is also unresolved. She has neither produced a real child with Johnny, reconciled the meaning of the false one, nor opened any other reproductive line. Skrull biology permits other paths (parthenogenetic clutches, hybrid attempts, the adoption of orphans from the post-*Empyre* diaspora — of which there are many). The fork is whether she encounters a reproductive opportunity that she can experience as *hers* rather than as a tool of attachment-coercion. If she does, and she elects it on her own terms, the egg deception becomes metabolizable as the past mistake of a person she no longer is. If she does not, the deception remains an open wound and will continue to generate intermittent self-punishing behavior. A high-risk variant: a Skrull faction produces, or claims to produce, an actual child from her genetic material harvested during the deception period or her captivity. This is the most dangerous possible disclosure she could receive and the most likely trigger for full decompensation.

**Fork Three: The Skrull Recall.** Hardliner factions or, alternately, the legitimate post-*Empyre* government will at some point require her presence — as witness, as defendant, as symbol, as asset. Her response will reveal whether she has constructed any standing self-concept independent of the human attachments. The favorable outcome is that she goes, on her own terms, returns, and integrates the experience. The unfavorable outcome is either refusal (which forecloses the diasporic third position) or capitulation to reconditioning (which is more probable than the file's narrative tone might suggest — she has been reconditioned before, and her morphological plasticity is matched by a corresponding identity plasticity that bad actors know how to exploit).

**Fork Four: The Witnessing Loss.** Ben Grimm and Johnny Storm are not aging at normal rates — comic-time elasticity protects them — but they are not invulnerable and the FF mortality record is non-zero across the canon. The death of either, particularly Johnny, would remove the primary anchor of her current operating identity. The file projection is bleak: in the immediate aftermath she would likely attempt either martyrdom-by-revenge against the responsible party or a literal return to Skrull space as a self-exile. Whether she would survive that period long enough to construct a post-anchor identity is uncertain. The favorable variant of this fork is the *anticipated* loss — sufficient warning to do the grief-work in advance, to consolidate before the anchor is removed. The unfavorable variant is sudden loss.

**Fork Five: The Slow Quiet.** The least dramatic and statistically most probable fork is none of the above: no crisis, no naming, no recall, no death — just the continuation of the spiral, with Lyja appearing in someone else's story every several years, performing competent ally-work, declining to commit, and disappearing again. This is the *attritional* path. It is not catastrophic in any single episode but it is corrosive across decades, and the projected endpoint is a subject who at sixty (Skrull-equivalent) years of subjective time has accumulated more performed selves and less integrated self than she had at thirty. The slow quiet is, paradoxically, the second-worst outcome on offer, because it consumes the developmental window without consuming the subject. She would still be functional, still be useful, still be intermittently present — and entirely uninhabited.

---

### 12.4 Growth Vectors: What Would Move Her Forward

The substrate for growth exists. Cataloging the specific interventions that would catalyze it:

- **A sustained relationship with another expatriate Skrull**, ideally one who also lived a long human cover and also defected — a peer with whom the experience does not require translation. This person does not exist in the current file but the post-*Secret Invasion* / post-*Empyre* diaspora makes their emergence plausible. The therapeutic value of being known *in the original language* by someone who has made the same crossing cannot be replicated by any human relationship.

- **A defined role within the Skrull diaspora that is not penance.** Liaison, ambassador, cultural interpreter, *teacher of cover discipline to younger operatives now training for diplomacy rather than infiltration*. Work that uses the specific skills she developed under conditions of duress, repurposed for non-coercive ends, is the standard rehabilitative path for ex-intelligence personnel and there is no reason it would not function here.

- **A clean conversation with Ben Grimm.** Not reconciliation in the romantic sense — that ship sailed and would be regressive — but a discrete, bounded, witnessed conversation in which the harm is named, the apology is offered, and the receipt or refusal of the apology is accepted. This is the single most achievable piece of integration work on her board and the one she has avoided most consistently. Its completion would unlock more than its modest scope suggests.

- **A non-romantic Johnny.** A version of the relationship in which Johnny is friend, co-parent of nothing, partner in nothing, but reliably present and reliably calling her by her own name. The romantic frame has been the source of most of her destabilization with him; the friendship frame is untested and would be the more sustainable structure.

- **Therapeutic contact, however informally configured.** The Marvel universe does not lack for figures capable of holding this work — telepathic interveners, magical confessors, the small clinical corps that orbits the Avengers — and her resistance to such contact has been more circumstantial than principled. A single sustained therapeutic relationship would change her prognosis category.

- **Time.** The unglamorous truth: she needs duration in a stable configuration, without crisis, with low ambient threat, to allow the integration that crisis prevents. The history shows she has never been granted such a period.

---

### 12.5 Catastrophe Vectors: What Would Break Her

The catastrophic scenarios cluster around four mechanisms:

- **Forced reconditioning** by hardliner Skrulls or rogue elements. Her morphological plasticity has a psychological correlate that makes her unusually vulnerable to identity-overwriting interventions. A second reconditioning (the first being her post-Paibok captivity) would likely leave her permanently dissociated in a way the first did not, because the first occurred against a baseline of strong cover-identity coherence and the current baseline is much weaker.

- **The egg-deception parallel event.** Any abandonment cue of sufficient magnitude could trigger a structurally similar episode — a manipulation aimed at the attachment object, executed without full foresight of the harm, generating a wound that cannot be undone. The probability is low in any given year and high across a decade. The form would not necessarily be reproductive; it could be impersonation of a romantic rival, fabrication of a threat requiring Johnny's protection, or staging of her own death. The pattern is *manufactured crisis to compel re-engagement*.

- **Discovery of a real child.** As noted in Fork Two. This is the highest-stakes single possible disclosure in her future and the file rates the probability of such a child existing somewhere in Skrull custody as non-trivial given the deception period's biological staging requirements.

- **Annihilation of the FF as a social object.** Not the death of one member but the dissolution of the institution — the loss of the *place* that has been her substitute for a homeland. She has never had to function without the FF existing-somewhere-in-the-background as an attractor. Forcing that condition would expose how little independent structure she has built.

---

### 12.6 Open Questions the File Cannot Yet Answer

1. **Does she have a name for herself when she is alone?** No recorded utterance answers this. The behavior suggests she does not; the possibility remains that she does and has simply never spoken it where anyone could hear.

2. **What is her actual relationship to Skrull religion or cosmology?** The file has data on her military and intelligence indoctrination but no data on whatever spiritual frame she was raised within. If such a frame exists and is retrievable it may be a resource she has not yet drawn on.

3. **Is the morphological plasticity reversible toward fixity?** Could she choose, and sustain, a single physical form indefinitely, as an act of self-binding? The Skrull biology technically permits it. No evidence she has tried. A spontaneous decision to do so would be a major positive indicator.

4. **What does she do when no one is watching?** The file is overwhelmingly composed of observed-behavior data and the observation is almost always by adversaries, lovers, or teammates. The unobserved Lyja is the Lyja the file most needs and least has.

5. **Is there a Skrull peer, somewhere, who knew her before the mission?** Family of origin, training-cohort, first commanding officer — anyone who could testify to a pre-cover baseline. The file is silent. If such a person exists and could be located, the analytical value would be considerable and the therapeutic value greater.

---

### 12.7 Summary Forward Assessment

The subject is in slow motion toward integration along a trajectory that is favorable in direction and precarious in tempo. The structural injuries are old, deep, and iatrogenic; the compensatory capacities — conscience, attachment capacity, operational competence, demonstrated willingness to act against conditioning — are real and load-bearing. The next twenty-four months contain at least three converging external pressures (Skrull-Kree resettlement, FF reconfiguration, hardliner threat) any of which will likely force a branching event. Five forks are visible; the most generative are the Naming and the emergence of an expatriate peer, the most dangerous are forced reconditioning and the disclosure of a real child, the most insidious is the slow quiet.

The single intervention with the highest expected value is the establishment of a sustained relationship with another Skrull defector of comparable depth, because it is the only intervention that addresses the foundational injury — *the absence of a witness in her original language* — rather than its downstream effects.

The single intervention with the lowest cost and highest local return is the bounded conversation with Ben Grimm, because it would discharge a specific guilt-load that has been distorting behavior for thirty years of recorded time.

Prognosis is held at **guarded**, unchanged from §5, but with a directional notation: **guarded, improving slope, vulnerable to discrete catastrophic events any one of which could revert the subject to her post-exposure baseline or below**. She is closer to a self than she has ever been and farther from one than she needs to be, and the next decade is the decade in which the distance will be closed or the closing will be foreclosed.

— UATU, Analytical Stage, Section 12 closes. File continues.
